# Builderforce.ai ŌĆö Roadmap & Gap Register

> Single source of truth for planned work and deferred issues for the Builderforce.ai sub-project. The [README](./README.md) documents what exists today; this file tracks what's next, what's done, and what's broken. Deferred issues found during work are appended to the **Consolidated Gap Register** below.

---

## Platform Roadmap (umbrella ŌĆö Builderforce.ai ┬Ę BuilderForce Agents ┬Ę MambaCode.js ┬Ę SSM.js)

> **Vision**: Human as the manager ŌĆö developers supervise, prioritize, approve, and steer AI agents rather than writing code themselves.

## Key Metrics

**Acquisition:** GitHub stars (target 10K by Q2 2026) ┬Ę npm weekly downloads (5K by Q2 2026) ┬Ę Discord members (2K by Q2 2026)

**Activation:** Projects with `.builderforce/` initialized (500 active projects) ┬Ę workflows executed/day (1K/day by Q2 2026) ┬Ę MCP connections (200 by Q3 2026)

**Retention:** DAU/MAU Ōēź 30% ┬Ę weekly active agents connected to Builderforce ┬Ę average sessions/user/week

## Next Milestones

The items below are the next high-impact milestones, ordered by business priority. Items marked **P0** are blocking shipped features; **P1** are required for full enterprise readiness.

### P0 ŌĆö Blocking Today

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Remote task result streaming** | Multi-agent orchestration actually returns results. Today `remote:<id>` steps complete but return empty output, making dependent workflow steps non-functional. Fix: `correlationId` round-trip on `ClawRelayDO` so the originating agent awaits the `remote.result` frame. |
| **Execution WebSocket streaming** | Replaces 2-second polling loop in `clawlink-adapter.ts` with a server-push stream; cuts execution latency and load on the Builderforce relay. |
| **Live Orchestration Workspace** (Builderforce SPA) | Real-time DAG view of running agents ŌĆö task status, role, model, streaming output. Required to demo and sell the multi-agent story; Devin and Windsurf Cascade both ship this. |
| **BuilderForce Agents as MCP Provider** | Exposes `project_knowledge`, `codebase_search`, `git_history`, and `workflow_status` via the `/mcp` endpoint on the local gateway. Cursor and Continue.dev users can call BuilderForce Agents tools without switching to the BuilderForce Agents TUI ŌĆö this is a distribution multiplier. |

### P1 ŌĆö Enterprise Readiness

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Diff staging & inline approval API** | Agent file edits buffered for human review before landing on disk. Risk-averse teams (the highest-value buyer segment) require this. `/diff`, `/accept`, `/reject` commands are already in the TUI; the Builderforce-side `pending_diffs` table and relay frame complete the loop. |
| **Spec & workflow storage API** | `/spec` workflow outputs (PRD, arch spec, task list) pushed to Builderforce and queryable by goal/status/project. Turns ephemeral planning runs into auditable, reviewable artifacts with a lifecycle. |
| **Spec review + workflow portal SPA** | Web UI for product owners to view, review, and approve agent-generated specs, then trigger implementation workflows. |

### P2 ŌĆö Observability & Unit Economics

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Token usage dashboard** | Historical context pressure, token spend, and compaction events per session. Required before any usage-based pricing model can be built. |
| **Agent run audit trail** | Immutable, queryable log of every tool call (name, args, result, duration) per run. Required for SOC 2 / compliance-sensitive buyers. |
| **Fleet capability management SPA** | Per-agent online status, reported capabilities, and declared capabilities ŌĆö UI for the `remote:auto[caps]` routing already implemented in the orchestrator. |
| **Persona registry API** | Team-shared agent personas synced from Builderforce to all agents via heartbeat response; no more manual YAML file distribution. |

### P3 ŌĆö Future Moat

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Model cost tracking** | Per-session cost estimate, monthly budget alerts, per-project breakdown. Foundation for COGS control and chargeback. |
| **Approval workflow API** | Agent requests human approval before destructive operations (`rm`, force-push, deploy). Relay frame triggers browser notification; execution is suspended until approved/rejected. |
| **Spec import (GitHub Issues / Linear / Jira)** | `/spec import <url>` converts an issue tracker ticket into a Builderforce spec and starts the planning workflow. |
| **Cross-agent memory sharing** | Opt-in memory sync between agents with tenant-scoped access control, deduplication by content hash, and `#private` tag filtering. |

---

## Known Implementation Gaps (Builderforce.ai API)

Gaps found during audit on 2026-03-28. Severity reflects impact on shipped user flows.

| Gap | Location | Severity | Resolution |
|-----|----------|----------|------------|
| User suspension enforcement ŌĆö no `is_suspended` column; revoking tokens doesn't prevent new logins | `adminRoutes.ts:2247`, `schema.ts` | **CRITICAL** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö `0039_user_suspension.sql` + login/middleware check |
| Admin password reset sends no email ŌĆö only writes audit log | `adminRoutes.ts:2230` | **CRITICAL** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö generates 24-hr magic link + sends email |
| Confluence connectivity test always returns `ok: true` without testing credentials | `integrationRoutes.ts:316` | **HIGH** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö `testConfluence()` added |
| Freshservice connectivity test always returns `ok: true` without testing credentials | `integrationRoutes.ts:316` | **HIGH** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö `testFreshservice()` added |
| Agent channels endpoint always returns `[]` ŌĆö stub with no DB query | `clawRoutes.ts:1103` | **HIGH** | Documented gap ŌĆö no channel registry table exists; needs schema design |
| Helcim checkout creates no recurring billing schedule ŌĆö subscriptions are one-time charges | `HelcimProvider.ts:78` | **HIGH** | Documented ŌĆö requires Helcim recurring billing API call after `APPROVED` webhook |
| Helcim webhook mapping is a placeholder ŌĆö all `APPROVED` events become `subscription.activated` | `HelcimProvider.ts:130` | **HIGH** | Documented ŌĆö requires Helcim webhook payload schema from dashboard |
| Magic link email was a `console.log` stub ŌĆö users never received sign-in emails | `oauthRoutes.ts:350` | **CRITICAL** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö `EmailService.ts` created; wired to Resend |
| Marketplace pricing migration orphaned in wrong folder ŌĆö runtime error: `column marketplace_skills.price_cents does not exist` | `Builderforce.ai/migrations/003_*.sql` (never applied ŌĆö runner reads `api/migrations/` only) | **CRITICAL** | Ō£ģ Fixed ŌĆö ported to `api/migrations/0042_marketplace_pricing_and_developer_api.sql` |

| Risk | Probability | Impact | Mitigation |
|------|------------|--------|------------|
| Anthropic/OpenAI ships multi-agent IDE tool | High | High | Double down on self-hosting + open source moat |
| Cursor/Windsurf adds MCP + multi-agent | Medium | High | Ship live workflow DAG and agent mesh ŌĆö unique differentiators |
| Model API costs too high for free tier | Medium | Medium | Aggressive rate limiting + BuilderForce AgentsLLM margin |
| Enterprise sales cycle too long | High | Low | Focus on SMB Teams plan first; use as reference for enterprise |

## PHASE 4 ŌĆö Multi-Agent Orchestration at Scale [Q3 2026]

These items completed the platform's multi-claw coordination layer. All five are shipped.

### P1 ŌĆö Visual Task Dependency Graph

- [x] **Backend** ŌĆö `GET /api/workflows/:id/graph` endpoint (`workflowRoutes.ts`): merges `workflowTasks` dependency edges with live telemetry spans into a DAG response (`nodes` + `edges`)
- [x] **Frontend** ŌĆö `WorkflowDagView.tsx`: pure-SVG topological layout (Kahn's algorithm), status-colored nodes, cubic-bezier edges, duration/cost annotations
- [x] **Frontend** ŌĆö Tasks/Graph tab switcher in `WorkflowsContent.tsx` ŌĆö detail view fetches graph lazily on first tab open

### P1 ŌĆö Cross-Claw Context Sharing

- [x] **Backend** ŌĆö `GET /api/claws/:id/context-bundle` endpoint (`clawRoutes.ts`): returns the last-synced `.coderClaw/` files as a JSON bundle (`{ files: [{ path, content, sha256 }] }`)
- [x] **Relay** ŌĆö `builderforce-relay.ts` fetches the context bundle from the origin claw before forwarding a `remote.task` frame; SHA-256 deduplicates unchanged files
- [x] **Schema** ŌĆö `ContextBundleResponse` type in `openapi/schema.ts` and `api-contract.ts`

### P1 ŌĆö Streaming Result Aggregation

- [x] **Backpressure** ŌĆö `remote-result-broker.ts`: max 5 concurrent remote tasks, FIFO wait queue, 600 s default timeout
- [x] **Retries** ŌĆö `remote-subagent.ts`: 3-attempt exponential backoff (500 ms ŌåÆ 1 s ŌåÆ 2 s) on network errors and 5xx responses; emits `task.retry` telemetry spans
- [x] **Mesh UX** ŌĆö `FleetMeshContent.tsx`: SVG fleet graph (hub + claw nodes), real-time online/offline indicators, remote dispatch panel with preset payloads; rendered on the Workforce page when Ōēź2 claws are registered

### P2 ŌĆö Shared OpenAPI Contract

- [x] **Builderforce** ŌĆö `src/openapi/schema.ts`: TypeScript interfaces for every CoderClaw Ōåö Builderforce endpoint (registration, heartbeat, forward, context-bundle, telemetry, workflows, team memory)
- [x] **CoderClaw** ŌĆö `src/infra/api-contract.ts`: mirror declarations so the claw has zero runtime dependency on the server package
- [x] **Endpoint** ŌĆö `GET /api/openapi.json` (in `index.ts`): OpenAPI 3.1 document served from production at `https://api.builderforce.ai/api/openapi.json`

### P2 ŌĆö Cross-Claw Memory Sharing (Team Memory Mesh)

- [x] **Backend** ŌĆö `POST /api/teams/memory` + `GET /api/teams/memory` (`teamMemoryRoutes.ts`): claw-key or tenant-JWT auth, `#private` tag support, newest-first pagination
- [x] **Client** ŌĆö `KnowledgeLoopService.pushMemoryToMesh()` in `knowledge-loop.ts`: fires after every completed agent run, pushes activity summary + tags to the mesh; `pullTeamMemory()` caches entries in `.coderClaw/memory/team-memory.json` (5 min TTL)
- [x] **Schema** ŌĆö `TeamMemoryEntry` type in `openapi/schema.ts` and `api-contract.ts`

## Consolidated Gap Register

> **Reorganized 2026-06-14.** Resolved/closed items are collected under **Ō£ģ Done / Resolved**; the remaining open items are grouped by **revenue impact** (Direct ŌåÆ Growth ŌåÆ Core ŌåÆ Internal). Revenue tiering is a first-pass heuristic ŌĆö adjust freely. The thematic feature write-ups are preserved verbatim under **­¤ōō Archived thematic context**. Full audit trail: `git log`.
>
> **Stats ŌĆö 341 register items:** Ō£ģ 53 resolved ┬Ę ­¤öō 288 open. Open by revenue impact ŌåÆ ­¤Æ░ Direct 15 ┬Ę ­¤ÜĆ Growth 10 ┬Ę ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core 190 ┬Ę ­¤¦╣ Internal 73.

### ­¤¦Ą Isolation Tracks ŌĆö parallel agent assignment

Dispatch **one agent per track**. Tracks are **file-disjoint by construction**, so agents run in parallel without stepping on each other. An agent assigned a track edits **only** files under that track's _Owns_ paths, works **only** the open gaps whose primary file lives there, and draws migration numbers **only** from its reserved band. Anything outside its paths belongs to another track ŌĆö use the shared-hub rules below, never edit cross-track.

| Track | Owns (primary paths) | Gap focus | Mig band |
|---|---|---|---|
| **T1 ┬Ę Marketing & SEO Web** | `frontend/src/app/{page.tsx,compare,integrations,marketplace/[slug],product,agents,blog,pricing,projects/[id],sitemap.ts}` ┬Ę `frontend/src/lib/{seo,content,structured-data,og,marketplaceSeo,blogData,routeMarketing}.*` ┬Ę `frontend/src/components/{PublicShell,MarketingHeader,AppFooter,PageContainer,RouteMarketing,QuickStart,blog/*}` ┬Ę `frontend/public/{robots.txt,install.*}` ┬Ę routes `pendingPromptRoutes.ts` | ­¤ÜĆ Growth | ŌĆö |
| **T2 ┬Ę App UI & Brain** | all other `frontend/src/{app,components}/**` ┬Ę `frontend/src/lib/brain/**` ┬Ę `brain-embedded/**` ┬Ę route `dashboardRoutes.ts` | ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core (UI/UX) | 0180ŌĆō0189 |
| **T3 ┬Ę Gateway & LLM** | `api/src/application/llm/**` ┬Ę `api/src/infrastructure/cache/**` ┬Ę route `llmRoutes.ts` | ­¤Æ░ Direct + LLM Core/Internal | 0130ŌĆō0139 |
| **T4 ┬Ę Cloud Runtime & PR loop** | `api/src/application/{runtime,repos}/**` ┬Ę `api/src/infrastructure/relay/**` ┬Ę routes `runtimeRoutes.ts`,`repoRoutes.ts`,`repoAnalysisRoutes.ts`,`taskRoutes.ts`,`agentRuntimeRoutes.ts` | ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core (cloud agents) | 0140ŌĆō0149 |
| **T5 ┬Ę On-Prem Agent Runtime** | `agent-runtime/**` ┬Ę `packages/**` | ­¤¦╣ Internal (engine/pi/tui) | ŌĆö |
| **T6 ┬Ę Studio & Voice** | `studio/**` ┬Ę `studio-embedded/**` ┬Ę `voice/**` ┬Ę routes `studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts`,`studioWeightRoutes.ts` ┬Ę frontend `components/{LlmStudioPanel,VoiceClonePanel}`,`app/ide/voice` | ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core (video/voice) | 0150ŌĆō0159 |
| **T7 ┬Ę Tenant ┬Ę Embed ┬Ę Governance** | `builderforce-embedded/**` ┬Ę `frontend/src/{app,lib}/embed/**` ┬Ę `api/src/application/seams/**` ┬Ę `api/src/infrastructure/auth/segment*` ┬Ę routes `tenant*`,`embedRoutes.ts`,`governanceRoutes.ts`,`segment*`,`seamRoutes.ts`,`webhookRoutes.ts`,`biRoutes.ts`,`mcpExtensionRoutes.ts`,`reportRoutes.ts` | ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core + ­¤¦╣ Internal (multi-tenant) | 0160ŌĆō0169 |
| **T8 ┬Ę Workflows ┬Ę Boards** | `api/src/application/{workflow,boardsync,swimlane}/**` ┬Ę routes `workflow*`,`board*`,`integrationRoutes.ts`,`githubWebhookRoutes.ts` ┬Ę frontend `components/workflow-builder/**`,`app/workflows/**` | ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Core (orchestration) | 0170ŌĆō0179 |
| **T9 ┬Ę Platform ┬Ę DB ┬Ę CI** _(steward)_ | `api/migrations/**` ┬Ę `api/scripts/**` ┬Ę `.github/workflows/**` ┬Ę `frontend/eslint.config.js` ┬Ę root tsconfig/lint ┬Ę schema-drift allowlist | ­¤¦╣ Internal (migrations/drift/tests/lint) | 0190+ |
| **T10 ┬Ę Docs & QA** | `docs-site/**` ┬Ę `qa-e2e/**` ┬Ę `api/src/application/qa/**` ┬Ę route `qaRoutes.ts` ┬Ę frontend `components/QaContent.tsx` | QA + docs | ŌĆö |

**Shared hubs ŌĆö append-only, never edit another track's block:**
- `api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts` ŌĆö append new tables at the end; **T9 stewards** ordering + drift.
- `api/src/index.ts` ŌĆö append route mounts only.
- `frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts` ŌĆö append API-client blocks only.
- `frontend/src/lib/content.ts` ŌĆö **T1 owns**; other tracks request copy changes via T1.
- This **Consolidated Gap Register** ŌĆö append entries; run the "organize + calculate gaps" pass only when no other agent is mid-edit (it rewrites section counts).

**Migration numbering is the one true serialization point** (duplicate numbers already bit us ŌĆö see the `0109`/`0111` collision gap). Draw **only** from your band; **T9** issues any number outside a band. Next free single slot: **0129**.

**Run each track in its own git worktree + branch** (`git worktree add ../bf-T2 -b track/T2`). File-disjoint paths only prevent *merge* conflicts ŌĆö pointing two agents at the **same working copy** still lets their edits interleave mid-run (and a shared `tsc`/`pnpm` build clobbers). One worktree per track = one branch per track = truly parallel; merge the branches back when each track lands. Track boundaries are **convention, not enforced** ŌĆö an agent that ignores its _Owns_ scope can still stray (the durable fix is a CI/pre-commit guard that rejects a branch touching files outside its declared track ŌĆö logged in the register).

**Dispatch example:** _"Agent A ŌåÆ T1 (Growth) ┬Ę Agent B ŌåÆ T3 (Gateway/Direct) ┬Ę Agent C ŌåÆ T9 (Internal/DB),"_ each in its own worktree/branch. Three agents, zero file overlap.

- Ō£ģ **AGENTIC TESTER ŌĆö heatmap-driven exploratory testing ŌĆö 2026-06-21 (migration 0206, files only).** Added the autonomous, container-run half of Agentic QA. (2) **Plan + queue** ŌĆö `POST /api/qa/explorations` snapshots the heatmap, derives an ordered plan over the hottest zones (`buildExplorationPlan`, deterministic, heat carried onto each step), and persists a `qa_explorations` row ([qaRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/qaRoutes.ts), [qaTypes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/qa/qaTypes.ts), migration [0206](Builderforce.ai/api/migrations/0206_agentic_tester.sql)). (3) **Container harness** ŌĆö `qa-e2e` gains an `explore` mode + `Dockerfile`: claims a queued exploration (`POST /explorations/claim`), drives a real Chromium through the plan, and captures runtime errors from four live sources (console / pageerror / failed-or-5xx network / crash) plus assertion failures, each inheriting the zone's heat ([explorer-engine.ts](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/src/explorer-engine.ts), [explore.ts](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/src/explore.ts), [Dockerfile](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/Dockerfile), [agentic-tester.yml](Builderforce.ai/.github/workflows/agentic-tester.yml) runs in the Playwright container). (4) **Feedback loop** ŌĆö `POST /explorations/:id/findings` (deduped per run by fingerprint) ŌåÆ `qa_findings`; `POST /findings/:id/task` opens a board task via `TaskService.createTask` (priority by severity), links it, marks the finding `task_created`. (5) **UI** ŌĆö "Agentic Tester" section in [QaContent.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx): heatmap bars, Run button, explorations list, per-exploration findings with "Create task". **Verification:** api `tsc` + `check:schema` + `check:migrations` clean; frontend `tsc` clean; qa-e2e `tsc` clean; unit tests for plan/severity/fingerprint added (run in CI ŌĆö vitest not installed locally). Migration `0206` is a **file only ŌĆö not applied to any live DB**. Residual gaps below were NOT closed this pass:
  - ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ **No auto-dispatch of the container from the platform.** Queuing an exploration in the UI does not yet spawn the container; a scheduler drains the queue (CI cron / manual `workflow_dispatch` / `docker run`). (primary: [cloudDispatch.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/runtime/cloudDispatch.ts))
  - ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ **Heat is workspace-wide, not per customer site.** `qa_journey_events` has no `project_id` (capture runs in the app shell), so a project-mode exploration runs against the customer target but ranks zones from Builderforce-app usage. (primary: [qaTypes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/qa/qaTypes.ts))

Migration `0205` is a **file only ŌĆö not applied to any live DB**. Residual gaps below were NOT closed this pass:
  - ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ **Per-project activity attribution missing in the tenant rollup.** `activity_events` has no `project_id`; the rollup gives tenant totals + a by-**repository** breakdown but not a true by-**project** rollup. Wiring would map `activity_events.repository_full_name`ŌåÆ`project_repositories(owner/repo)` and/or `credential_id`ŌåÆ`integration_credentials.project_id`.   - ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ **Orphan activity (contributor_id NULL) is not claimable.** Ingestion (`POST /api/contributors/activity`) drops events whose `contributorExternalId` resolves to no identity (`contributorId=null`) ŌĆö they never roll up and the merge/consolidate tools can't reach them. Needs an "unattributed activity ŌåÆ create/attach contributor" claim flow (and optionally auto-create a contributor + identity on first sight). Unblocks complete attribution of ingested activity. (primary: [contributorRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/contributorRoutes.ts))
  - ­¤¦╣ **Unified engagement is not persisted to history.** `GET /api/members/engagement` computes on the fly (cached); unlike task scorecards it isn't snapshotted into `member_metrics_period`, so there's no trend/period history for the composite engagement score. Unblocks engagement-over-time charts. (primary: [engagement.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/metrics/engagement.ts))
  - ­¤¦╣ **Merge revert is best-effort against post-merge collisions.** If a survivor gains a colliding identity or team membership AFTER a merge, `unmergeContributors` restores via `onConflictDoNothing` (documented in-file) rather than reconciling ŌĆö a rare edge that can leave the source missing a re-added identity on revert. (primary: [mergeService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/contributors/mergeService.ts))

- Ō£ģ **MULTI-TRACK GAP-BURNDOWN SWEEP ŌĆö 2026-06-21 (T1ŌĆōT10, file-disjoint, shared checkout).** One agent per isolation track closed the **code-actionable** subset of the open register end-to-end (logic + wiring + tests + package typecheck); genuinely-blocked items (live-DB migration apply, deploy, real browser/WebGPU/GPU, external repos, unprovisioned secrets, product decisions) were left **open** with their blocker named (they remain below). **Verification (whole repo, post-merge):** all 8 touched packages `tsc --noEmit` clean; **api 1132 tests / frontend 286 / agent-runtime 8140 / studio 150 / studio-embedded 16 / brain-embedded 38 all green**; api `check:schema` + `check:migrations` + `check:tracks` pass. New migrations are **files only, not applied to any live DB**. Closed this pass:

- Ō£ģ **RESOLVED (2026-06-30) ŌĆö Tenant-scoping (IDOR) audit: ~31 cross-tenant access holes found & fixed across 6 files.** Prompted by the `GET /api/tenants/:id` fix ŌĆö a parallel audit of ~40 route files found the same class everywhere: handlers reading/mutating a tenant-owned row by a request-supplied id without filtering on `c.get('tenantId')`.   - **[runtimeRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) (6):** `/tasks/:id/state`, `/tasks/:id/cancel`, `/executions/:id`, `/executions/:id/cancel`, `/executions/:id/state` (PATCH), `/executions/:id/stream` (WS) all loaded/cancelled/mutated executions by id with no tenant check ŌåÆ new shared `loadOwnedExecution(c, svc, id)` guard (404 on not-found/mismatch).

  - **[teamRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/teamRoutes.ts) (1 + cache leak):** `GET /by-project/:projectId/workforce` read another tenant's roster (`loadProjectTeamMembers` lacked a `teams.tenantId` join ŌĆö now threaded through [assigneeRecommender.ts](api/src/application/metrics/assigneeRecommender.ts)); ALSO the `teamsByProjectCacheKey`/`teamsWorkforceCacheKey` were keyed by projectId only ŌåÆ one tenant's cached result could be served to another ŌåÆ both now tenant-prefixed (+ invalidation threaded).
  - **[devTeamRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/devTeamRoutes.ts) (2):** `DELETE /:id/members/:contributorId` had no team-ownership check; `POST /:id/members` didn't verify the contributor belongs to the tenant (ŌåÆ cross-tenant PII via `GET /:id`) ŌåÆ both now tenant-verified.

- Ō£ģ **PARTIAL (2026-06-28) ŌĆö VS Code onboarding: in-extension PROJECT creation shipped; WORKSPACE creation/switching is web-only (auth-constrained).** A new user needs a workspace (tenant) + a project before managing tasks. Overlay hides on the frame's first `resize` (real paint). User action to recover an already-open stale tab: reload the extension (or close+reopen the tab). **­¤ö¼ ROOT CAUSE NARROWED (2026-06-22 sideload build):** the Copy-log trace showed the frame NEVER posts `ready` (its JS never executes) ŌĆö so it is NOT the gate (gate is post-`ready`); the `/embed` document's script is blocked in the webview while the API works (Diagnose: tenant token + `/api/projects` 200). Leading cause: VS Code webviews run under COEP and a cross-origin frame lacking `Cross-Origin-Resource-Policy: cross-origin` is blocked (and/or the app service-worker hangs in the webview partition). Fix shipped in the extension: the frame is now loaded as `<iframe credentialless>` (ephemeral no-cookie/fresh-storage partition ŌĆö allowed under a COEP parent without CORP; auth rides postMessage not cookies) plus an iframe DOM `load`-event probe to distinguish a frame-level block from a post-load JS block. **If `credentialless` does not clear it, the durable fix is frontend:** add `Cross-Origin-Resource-Policy: cross-origin` to the `/embed/*` middleware response AND to `/_next/static/*` asset headers (so the framed doc + its chunks are embeddable under COEP) ŌĆö deploy-pending. **­¤ö¼ NARROWED FURTHER (2026-06-23 sideload):** with `credentialless` the iframe DOM `load` event NOW FIRES (`iframe credentialless: true` + `iframe DOM load event fired`) but still no `ready`/paint ŌåÆ the document loads, its JS just never posts `ready`. Ruled OUT the app-shell gate: `classifyShell('/embed/*')` returns `'none'` ([ConditionalAppShell.tsx](frontend/src/components/ConditionalAppShell.tsx) `NO_CHROME_PREFIXES`), so the embed page renders with no auth chrome. So the failure is inside the page's own JS (a GLOBAL provider from the root [layout.tsx](frontend/src/app/layout.tsx) ŌĆö AuthProvider/BrainProvider/Theme/Emulation/etc., which wrap EVERY route incl. `/embed` ŌĆö erroring or Suspending in the webview/credentialless context, so the embed subtree never mounts ŌåÆ `useEmbedFrame` never posts `ready`). Extension v2026.6.23 now captures all parent-side signals (every inbound postMessage, `securitypolicyviolation`, `window error`/`unhandledrejection`, robust source-tag matching so an origin quirk can't drop `ready`). The cross-origin page's own console is the only place the real exception shows; the parent webview cannot read it. Sideload build now `clients/vscode` 2026.6.23 (local test version, not a release).

- ­¤¦╣ **builderforce-memory `/install` requires a local checkout, not portable to work machines** ŌĆö The Claude Code `/install` skill (`~/.claude/skills/install/`) registers the MCP server by absolute path to a built `builderforce-memory` checkout (default `C:/code/agentic/builderforce-memory`, override via `--home`). `@builderforce/memory-mcp` and `@builderforce/memory` are not published to npm, so on a machine without the repo the install fails. Publishing both (the `memory-mcp` bin is now disk-persistent via `BUILDERFORCE_MEMORY_FILE`, so the published binary is durable) would let the installer use `npx -y @builderforce/memory-mcp` and work anywhere with zero checkout ŌĆö the main blocker to using this memory at work.
- ­¤¦╣ **stdio MCP recall is lexical (Jaccard), not SSM-embedding** ŌĆö The headless stdio binary does not stand up the SSM runtime/GPU, so cross-session recall uses word-overlap. SSM-embedding recall requires embedding the package in-process and passing `runtime` to `createLocalMemoryStoreBackend` (or a networked builderforce.ai backend). Fixing it upgrades recall quality (and therefore token savings) for the Claude Code integration.
- ­¤¦╣ **Internal (test isolation) ŌĆö `getOrSetCached`'s module-global L1 `Map` is never reset between tests, making cache-backed tests order-dependent.** Surfaced by the CI failure in [cloudMemory.test.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudMemory.test.ts): the `recall clamps the limit` test populated L1 key `am:recall:1:0:5:q` with `[]`, and the later `degrades to {ok:false}` test reused the same tenant/query/limit, getting an L1 hit (`ok:true`) instead of running the failing loader. Fixed in this pass by giving the degrade test an isolated tenant (99) + unique query (cold cache). Durable fix unblocks safe co-location of any future cache-dependent tests: export a `__clearL1CacheForTests()` from [readThroughCache.ts](api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts) (clears the module-level `l1` Map) and call it in a shared `beforeEach`, so tests don't have to hand-pick collision-free keys. Primary file: `api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts`.

The CF coders I added 400'd on tools (`[cloudflare] 400: tools[0].function: Field required`): the old `/ai/run/<model>` path with a hand-rolled `toCloudflareTools` flattener sent `{name,ŌĆ”}`, but the newer FC models (kimi/glm) want the OpenAI-nested `{type:'function',function:{ŌĆ”}}`. - **Cloud coding runs 413'd on small-context models + a gateway error wrongly marked the run COMPLETE; context-aware model selection added, but true context COMPACTION is still a gap** (2026-06-15). A 97K-token coding context hit a 32K-window Cloudflare model (`@cf/qwen/qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`) ŌåÆ HTTP **413** "exceeded this model context window limit", surfaced as a misleading "Gateway 429", and the **container** loop (`api/container/server.mjs`) then ran `finalize` (ŌåÆ COMPLETED) instead of failing. Fixed: (a) **413 Ōłł `CASCADE_STATUSES`** so a context overflow fails over to a bigger-window model (pool ordered big-window-first; a strict pin also drops + cascades on 413); (b) the container loop routes a gateway `turn.error` to the `fail` channel (self-heal/retry), never `finalize` ŌĆö the in-Worker + durable surfaces already mapped `ok:false`ŌåÆFAILED; (c) **context-aware first-pass selection** ŌĆö `VendorModelEntry.contextWindow` (live values), `estimateRequestTokens` + `modelsFittingContext` filter the seed to models whose window fits BEFORE the SSM learned-routing ranks them (small-window models stay in the pool for small tasks, never seeded into an oversized one); (d) gateway errors now name the resolved model + candidate chain ("which model failed"); (e) **context COMPACTION** (`api/src/application/llm/compactMessages.ts`) ŌĆö both cloud loops compress the conversation BEFORE each paid call when it exceeds a ~40K-token budget: the bulky middle (accumulated read_file/search tool results) is summarized into ONE "builder-memory" note via the free-pool gateway (`buildGatewaySummarizer`, same pattern as `BrainService.summarizeChat`), with lossy elision as the no-LLM fallback. Pinning the system prompt + the task + the recent tail, and the tail-never-starts-on-a-`tool`-message rule, keep tool-call pairing valid. The in-Worker/durable loop mutates `messages` in place (persists into CloudLoopState so the DO doesn't re-summarize the same prefix); the container `llm` op RETURNS `compactedMessages` and `server.mjs` adopts them as its loop state. A `context.compacted` timeline event reports beforeŌåÆafter tokens. So a long run no longer re-sends a ballooning history ŌĆö cheaper, and small/fast CF coders stay viable for longer.
- **Cloud coding runs drained the operator's metered Anthropic key ($10/mo cap hit 100%) ŌĆö root-caused to the cascade reaching the funded direct-Anthropic floor too eagerly; FIXED in the gateway** (2026-06-15). **RESOLVED ŌĆö Cloudflare binding + catalog:** `wrangler whoami`/`secret list` confirmed `CLOUDFLARE_AI_API_TOKEN` + `CLAUDE_API_KEY` were bound but **`CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` was NOT** (a misnamed `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_API_TOKEN` secret existed instead), so the vendor `apiKeyFrom` returned null and Cloudflare (`PAID_LEAD_VENDOR`, free neurons) was DEAD on every call ŌåÆ all overflow floored to the metered Anthropic key. Operator added `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` as a secret (NOT committed ŌĆö account id kept out of `wrangler.toml` for security). The stale `@cf/meta/llama-3-8b-instruct` (404s) was replaced with the live `@cf/meta/llama-3.1-8b-instruct-fp8`, and 3 live function-calling-verified CF coders were added to the pool (`@cf/zai-org/glm-4.7-flash` 128K, `@cf/moonshotai/kimi-k2.7-code` 256K, `@cf/meta/llama-3.3-70b-instruct-fp8-fast` 24K) so coding overflow burns free neurons before any metered coder. Fixes landed in `api/src/application/llm/**` + `api/src/infrastructure/auth/cooldownStore.ts`: (a) an Anthropic usage-cap **400** (`invalid_request_error` "reached your specified API usage limits") was classified as a fatal caller `request_error` ŌåÆ it short-circuited the cascade with no failover AND wrote no cooldown; now `throwClassified4xx`/`isCapacityLimitBody` map any capacity/credit-balance 4xx to a retryable 429 so it fails over to another provider; (b) coding runs were capped at `FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET=2` free coders before escalating to paid/metered coders ŌĆö now `CODING_FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET` (the whole free coding pool, ~9) is walked first so the metered floor is genuine last-resort (10+ models before Claude); (c) a capacity limit now cools the **whole vendor for 60 min** on the first strike (new `capacity` `CooldownClass`) instead of the 5-min transient, so a capped key stands down instead of being re-reached/re-billed every run. (The Cloudflare-binding root cause is RESOLVED ŌĆö see the entry above.) **Residual:** no per-turn telemetry event fires when a cloud run actually bills the direct-Anthropic floor (`claude-sonnet-4-6`/`claude-opus-4-8`) ŌĆö the metered-floor hit is observable only via usage rows after the fact; a `metered_floor_used` event on the timeline (sibling of `coding_model_degraded`) would make "we spent on the paid Claude key" loud in real time. Unblocks: provable, real-time cost visibility + an alarm before a spend cap is blown.
- **Cloud agents got first-class git tools (get-latest / undo / redo / status / diff / history) ŌĆö on-prem only ever had a read-only `git_history` that was never migrated** (2026-06-15). Root cause of the task-78 failures: the container agent worked on a stale branch (branched off an old main, never re-synced) so its build broke against old code and its PR would have reverted ~6.7K lines ŌĆö and it had no tool to pull the latest. Fixed by adding 6 git verbs to the SHARED registry (`packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts`, canonical command text in `buildGitCommand`), gated to the `shell` capability so they reach the Container + on-prem-shell surfaces but NOT the shell-less durable Worker: `git_status`, `git_diff`, `git_history` (migrates the pi-only on-prem tool), `git_sync_latest` (fetch+merge base ŌåÆ never build on stale code), `git_undo`/`git_redo` (reflog pair, dirty-tree-guarded). Container execution is mirrored in `api/container/server.mjs` (`gitTool`) with the surface-specific twist that it persists via Worker-side GitHub-API commits, so each mutating op first fast-forwards the local clone to the remote head, then operates, then pushes (`--force-with-lease` for undo/redo). Covered by `cloudAgentGitTools.test.ts` (10) incl. injection-safety; full api suite green (952). **Container clone is now a FULL clone** (`server.mjs` ŌĆö dropped `--depth 1`), so `git_sync_latest`, `git diff main`, and `git merge-base` work reliably (a shallow clone had no merge-base with the base branch); `git_sync_latest` is a plain `git fetch`+merge, no `--unshallow` dance. **The cloud system prompt now instructs the agent to call `git_sync_latest` FIRST** (shell-surface line in `prepareCloudRun`), so a stale branch is synced before any edit instead of relying on the tool description alone. **Remaining residuals:** (1) the shell-less durable Worker surface still has NO git sync ŌĆö a durable run on a stale branch can't self-update (it commits via API, no shell); a base-merge-over-API path would be needed (the Container surface, which is where multi-step coding runs, is covered). (2) On-prem's shared-registry surface (`NODE_FILE_SURFACE_CAPS`) intentionally omits `shell`, so it surfaces git via its NATIVE bash tools, not the shared git tools ŌĆö the legacy pi `git-history-tool.ts` can be deleted once the pi loop is retired.
- **Cloudflare Workers AI now LEADS every paid pool, but the catalog is only 3 models ŌĆö expanding it would "use Cloudflare more"** (2026-06-15). Cloudflare bills in neurons with the first ~10K/day FREE, so paid routing should drain that allowance before any metered vendor. Done in `LlmProxyService.ts`: new `PAID_LEAD_VENDOR='cloudflare'` + shared `leadPoolWithVendor()` floats Cloudflare to the head of `PRO_PAID_MODEL_POOL` (general paid) and `CODING_PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS` (coding paid fallback / backstop); the coding-pool default coder is deliberately left as the strong `claude-sonnet-4.6` (cost-first routing must not regress agentic coding quality ŌĆö Cloudflare leads only the *fallback*, not the primary default). Residual: the Cloudflare catalog (`vendors/cloudflare.ts`) has just `llama-3-8b`, `gemma-4-26b-a4b-it`, `qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`; adding more enabled Workers AI checkpoints (e.g. larger Llama / Qwen coders) would stretch the free allowance further across request shapes. Blocked on the operator's list of which Workers AI models are enabled on `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` (a model not enabled returns `success:false` and cooldown-cycles). Unblocks: more paid traffic served on the free neuron allowance instead of metered vendors. Also note: general PRO paid traffic now tries Cloudflare's small general models (8B/26B) first after the free pool ŌĆö acceptable per the cost directive and adaptively corrected by PRD-13 learned routing (`rankModelsForAction`), but a quality-sensitive Pro tenant may prefer a per-tenant opt-out toggle (not built).
- **On-prem coding-execution repo-prep is now a modular `RepoSyncStrategy` port + skills declare skill-to-skill deps; two follow-ups remain** (2026-06-16). The hard-coded "is this the latest code from the repo?" clone/checkout was duplicated inline in the swimlane dispatch loop ([builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts)) and the V2 ticket workspace ([builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts) `ensureTaskWorkspace`). Extracted into one injected [repo-sync.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/repo-sync.ts) `RepoSyncStrategy` (clone-if-missing ŌåÆ WIP-safe refresh-to-latest on reuse ŌåÆ branch mode `new-branch` vs idempotent `ticket-branch`), fixing the latent stale-reuse bug (the ticket workspace previously never re-synced) while preserving accumulated uncommitted WIP. Skills gained a `requires.skills` dependency ([dependencies.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills/dependencies.ts), enforced in `filterSkillEntries`): `coding-agent` now depends on `github`, which is auto-included when active and disables `coding-agent` if `gh` is absent. **Residuals:** (1) `builderforce skills check`/status ([skills-status.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills-status.ts)) and the install flow ([skills-install.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills-install.ts)) do NOT yet surface a skill-dependency unmet reason ("coding-agent disabled: requires github ŌåÆ gh missing") nor auto-install a depended-on skill ŌĆö the dependency is enforced only for prompt inclusion. (2) This `RepoSyncStrategy` covers the on-prem agent-runtime paths only; the **cloud** durable Worker surface still has no git sync (see the cloud git-tools entry above) ŌĆö unifying both behind one sync contract is the larger play. Fixing (1) unblocks honest skill diagnostics + one-shot dependency installs; (2) unblocks a single repo-prep policy across on-prem and cloud. Owner: T5 (on-prem runtime).
- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED ŌĆö `surface=container` runs were reaped as "orphaned" mid-build because the 90s liveness ceiling was shorter than a single shell command** (2026-06-15, execution #71 triage + fix). Root cause: the container heartbeated `executions.updated_at` **only on each `op:'llm'` step** (`cloudAgentEngine.ts`). A `run_command` shell step runs up to `COMMAND_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 min` (`api/container/server.mjs`) and made **no callback to the Worker until it finished** (its `op:'event'` is sent only *after* completion). Meanwhile BOTH liveness checks fail any cloud run whose `updated_at` is older than **90s** ŌĆö `RuntimeService.CLOUD_ORPHAN_MS = 90_000` (read-path) and `staleExecutionReaper.CLOUD_RUNNING_DEADLINE_MS = 90_000` (cron). So the first build/install/test step that exceeded 90s (this repo's `pnpm install && pnpm test` is ~2 min ŌĆö CI shows 1m58s) let the heartbeat go stale and the reaper killed the run *while the container was still legitimately running the command* ŌåÆ "went silent mid-run past the ~30s wall." The 600s command timeout vs 90s orphan ceiling was a **6.6├Ś mismatch**, and long shell commands are the container surface's entire reason to exist, so it fired on essentially every real build. Compounding: once a file was written the PR existed, so `isSelfHealEligible` (`openPrCount === 0`) was false and the orphan couldn't self-heal onto the durable runner ŌĆö it just failed (execution #71 had PR #34 open); and `AgentContainerDO.onError` never fired because the container was healthy and busy, it was the Worker-side reaper killing a live run (so the triage's "image is likely unstable" hint was misleading). **Fix:** the container now fires a dedicated `op:'heartbeat'` on a 30s timer for the whole run lifetime (`runLoop`, independent of LLM steps), and the Worker bumps `updated_at` via a shared `heartbeatExecution` helper (DRY ŌĆö the `llm` op uses it too). The heartbeat response also carries `cancelled`, so a cancel during a multi-minute build SIGKILLs the in-flight child immediately and the loop breaks before spending another LLM call, instead of waiting out the 10-min command timeout. **Residual:** the container surface still has no separate orphan deadline ŌĆö liveness is correctly measured from the heartbeat now, but if the internal `container-op` endpoint is itself unreachable for >90s the run is still reaped; a container-specific ceiling (Ōēź a couple beats) would harden against transient Worker-side outages.
- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED ŌĆö container runs (`surface=container`) cloned the BASE branch, never the ticket's HEAD branch, so every pass started blind to prior work** (2026-06-15). Root cause caught in execution #67 triage: prior runs commit their WIP to the ticket's head branch (`builderforce/task-<id>`, `ctx.branch`) via the Worker, but `api/container/server.mjs` cloned `git clone --depth 1 -b <baseBranch>` ŌĆö and a `--depth 1` clone is single-branch, so the head branch and all earlier passes were silently absent. The container landed on a stale `main` (`git status` ŌåÆ "On branch main", `git log --all` ŌåÆ one commit), and the agent burned its whole budget + multiple LLM steps rediscovering that the file it was asked to fix "doesn't exist on disk." Fixed by carrying `headBranch: repo.ctx.branch` in the container clone spec (`runtimeRoutes.ts`) and having the container clone the head branch first, falling back to the base branch only on run #1 when the head branch doesn't exist on the remote yet. Also emits a `runtime.clone` success event recording the branch actually checked out, so triage never has to reverse-engineer it from `git status` again. Residual: the head-branch clone is still `--depth 1` (shallow) ŌĆö an agent that needs base-branch history (e.g. `git diff main`, `git merge-base`) won't have it; unblocks full-history container work by deepening selectively (`git fetch --depth=N` / `--unshallow`) when a command needs it.

New end-to-end personality feature: a persona can carry a `PsychometricProfile` (full framework suite ŌĆö HEXACO / regulatory-focus / need-for-cognition / decision-style / moral-foundations / Thomas-Kilmann / Schwartz / Enneagram / dispositional) deterministically compiled into BOTH system-prompt directives AND execution levers (think-depth floor, reasoning-on, temperature) by [psychometrics.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/psychometrics.ts) and injected at run time via [buildPersonaSystemBlock](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/personas.ts) + [resolveActivePsychometricParams](agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts) in [attempt.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts). The LIVE path is `platform_personas` (migration `0199` + [adminRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/adminRoutes.ts) ŌåÆ agent-host sync ŌåÆ [registerPlatformPersonasAsRoles](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/agent-roles.ts)). The editor ([PsychometricEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/PsychometricEditor.tsx) ŌĆö sliders/questionnaire/import) is wired into the tenant persona modal ([personas/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/personas/page.tsx)) and Pro-gated via [PlanLimits.psychometricPersona](api/src/domain/tenant/PlanLimits.ts) + [personaRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/personaRoutes.ts). **Gap:** tenant "My Personas" persist to `localStorage`, not the DB, so a profile a tenant authors there is never synced to an agent host and never executes ŌĆö only admin-managed platform personas do. **Fixing** (server-back tenant personas in a `tenant_personas` table + sync them down the assignment path the way `platform_personas` flow) unblocks self-serve Pro personality that actually changes how a tenant's agents think. Owner: T1/T2.
