- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-14 (T9).** 4 recent prefix collisions renumbered into T9ŌĆÖs band (0109ŌåÆ0190, 0114ŌåÆ0191, 0120ŌåÆ0192, 0121ŌåÆ0193); 8 historical ones grandfathered in `.migration-collisions-allowlist.txt`; `check-migrations.mjs` fails CI on any new duplicate prefix. ORIGINAL GAP: **Duplicate migration numbers: `0109` (`0109_execution_cloud_agent_ref.sql` + `0109_execution_messages.sql`) AND `0111` (`0111_boards_project_unique.sql` + `0111_agent_feedback_and_perf.sql`).** The migrations dir keys ordering off the numeric prefix, so a runner that sorts by prefix-then-name applies each pair in filename order (`agent_feedbackŌĆ”` before `boardsŌĆ”` for 0111; `cloud_agent_ref` before `messages` for 0109) but a runner that dedupes/keys on the bare prefix token could skip one. Both `0111` files are independent CREATE-only DDL with no ordering dependency between them, so the practical risk is the same latent skip, not a broken sequence. The `0111_agent_feedback_and_perf.sql` number was assigned by task spec (gap [1247]) before noticing `0111_boards_project_unique.sql` already held it. Fixing (renumber one file of each colliding pair to the next free slot and update any applied-migrations ledger that already recorded the old name) unblocks: an unambiguous, gap-free migration sequence.

- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-14 (T9).** `migrate.mjs` now applies each file + its ledger INSERT in one `sql.transaction([...])` so a mid-file failure rolls the whole file back ŌĆö no half-applied schema. ORIGINAL GAP: **The migration runner is not transactional per file ŌĆö a mid-file failure leaves a partial apply.** [scripts/migrate.mjs](api/scripts/migrate.mjs) executes statements one-by-one and only records the migration in `_migrations` after all succeed; a failure midway (e.g. 0056's first attempt hit a missing table after 15 tables were already altered) leaves the DB half-migrated with the file un-recorded. 0056 was made idempotent + guarded so re-running converges, but not every migration is written that way. Fixing (wrap each migration file's statements in a single `BEGIN/COMMIT` so a failure rolls the whole file back) unblocks: no half-applied schema states, safe to author non-idempotent migrations.

- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-14 (T9).** `ci.yml` now builds brain-embedded in the link-dep prerequisites step alongside sdk/studio/studio-embedded. ORIGINAL GAP: **`brain-embedded` is a `link:` dep but is NOT built in CI's "link: dep prerequisites" step like its siblings (`sdk`/`studio`/`studio-embedded`).** [ci.yml](.github/workflows/ci.yml) only runs `npm install` (ŌåÆ `prepare` build) for those three before `pnpm install`. The Vitest `react` resolution failure was fixed in this pass via [vitest.config.ts](frontend/vitest.config.ts) `resolve.dedupe: ['react','react-dom','react/jsx-runtime']` (forces the frontend's single React copy instead of reaching into `brain-embedded/node_modules`, which the frontend-only CI job never installs). This works today **only because `brain-embedded/dist` is committed to git** (unlike `sdk/dist`/`studio/dist`/`worker/dist`, which are gitignored). If brain-embedded's `dist` is ever added to `.gitignore` to match the sibling convention, CI will break again because no build step regenerates it. Fixing (add `(cd brain-embedded && npm install --no-audit --no-fund)` to the prerequisite step so the package is built+installed consistently with its siblings, then `dist` can be safely gitignored) unblocks: a uniform link-dep build story with no committed build artifacts.

- **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-14 (T9).** `.github/isolation-tracks.json` manifest + `check-track-scope.mjs` (CI job `track-scope.yml` + pre-commit hook) reject out-of-scope files and out-of-band migrations per `track/<id>` branch ŌĆö isolation is now enforced, not honor-system. ORIGINAL GAP: **Isolation-track boundaries are convention-only ŌĆö no CI/pre-commit guard enforces a branchŌĆÖs declared track.** The READMEŌĆÖs ­¤¦Ą Isolation Tracks table assigns each agent a set of _Owns_ paths + a reserved migration band, but nothing rejects a commit/branch that edits files outside its track or grabs a migration number from another band. A sloppy or confused agent can silently cross tracks, reintroducing the merge/parallel-safety problem the tracks exist to prevent. Fixing (a pre-commit hook + CI job that maps a `track/<id>` branch name ŌåÆ the trackŌĆÖs path globs and migration band, failing on any out-of-scope file or out-of-band migration) unblocks: **enforceable** parallel-agent isolation instead of honor-system isolation. Prereq + DRY: extract the table into a machine-readable manifest (e.g. `.github/isolation-tracks.json`) that BOTH the guard and the README render from, so the two never drift.

### ­¤Æ░ Open ŌĆö Direct revenue / monetization (15)

_Billing, plan tiers (Free/Pro), marketplace purchase/payout, pricing & entitlement gates, metering, cost attribution._

- **Per-user sub-ledger from `metadata.userId` is not implemented.** The gateway debits the tenant's daily plan budget; if the SDK's `metadata.userId` is set, the gateway could maintain a per-user sub-ledger and enforce per-user caps. Tenant apps continue to enforce per-user budgets locally. Needs a product decision (per-user cap UX in the portal) plus a `tenant_user_token_caps` table and a query in the chat route. Fixing unblocks deletion of tenant-side `tokenLedger.charge` plumbing.

- ~~**Pending invitations don't reserve a plan seat.**~~ **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-21.** Did BOTH halves: (1) **invite time** ŌĆö new shared `seatCapacityForTenant(db, tenantId)` ([planLimitsGuard.ts](api/src/presentation/middleware/planLimitsGuard.ts)) counts active `tenant_members` + `status='pending'` `tenant_invitations` toward the tally, and `checkSeatLimit` now blocks once members + pending Ōēź maxSeats (so a manager can't queue invites the plan can't honour; the 402 message shows the members/pending breakdown). (2) **accept time** ŌĆö `acceptPendingInvitations` ([tenantRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/tenantRoutes.ts)) now does an EXPLICIT per-tenant seat re-check (members-only, since the pending row is being consumed) with a live per-run counter, so a plan DOWNGRADE after invites were queued can't over-seat: an un-seatable invite is left `pending` (visible in the manager's invitations list, auto-retries when a seat frees up) instead of silently auto-accepting past the cap (replaces the swallowed-error path). api typecheck + 1141 tests green.

- **Cost attribution (ticket ŌåÆ project ŌåÆ workspace ŌåÆ account) covers only the cloud-agent execution loop ŌĆö web/SDK and on-prem host spend isn't attributed.** Cost now stamps the full rollup chain on `llm_usage_log`: `task_id` (ticket, the finest grain ŌĆö migration 0104), `project_id` (0103), and `tenant_id` (account). **Workspace (segment) is intentionally NOT a column here** ŌĆö 0056 keeps `llm_usage_log` tenant-level (platform/infra ledger; its segment trigger RAISEs for segmented tenants), so workspace-level cost is derived by joining `project ŌåÆ segment` (projects.segment_id), not denormalized. Stamped from the run's task in [recordCloudUsage](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts); surfaced as ticket spend on the execution panel (`GET /tasks/:id/cost`) and the "By Project" card ([LlmUsageContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/LlmUsageContent.tsx)) rolling up to the account total. STILL UNATTRIBUTED (task_id/project_id null ŌåÆ account-level only): (a) gateway chat/image calls via `logUsage` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) ŌĆö no ticket/project context on a raw LLM call; (b) self-hosted **on-prem host** runs, which meter via the gateway path not `recordCloudUsage`, so a host executing a ticket records cost with no task/project; (c) the future CloudRunnerDO must pass `taskId`+`projectId` to `recordCloudUsage` or its spend regresses to unattributed. Also missing: a **workspace (segment) rollup** surface (the join exists; no endpoint/card yet) and a **project-page** spend widget (only the execution panel + LLM-usage dashboard show it). Fixing (thread a ticket/project hint through the gateway `_builderforce` metadata for agent-attributed calls; resolve executionŌåÆtaskŌåÆproject on the host-run usage write; add segment + project-page rollups) unblocks: complete spend at every level of the hierarchy. (Backfill for past cloud rows handled in 0103/0104 via executionŌåÆtaskŌåÆproject.)

- **hired.video's tailor worker runs its own client-side 6-model cascade against the gateway, using a deprecated model id.** The 2026-06-07 trace (`handleTailor`, `worker.js`) shows hired.video looping its *own* model list ŌĆö `qwen3-next:free`, `qwen3-coder:free`, `gemma-4-31b:free`, `hermes-3-405b:free`, `cerebras/llama3.1-8b`, and `anthropic/claude-3-haiku` (retired on the first-party Anthropic API) ŌĆö one builderforce call each, duplicating the gateway's failover and pinning models that no longer exist. The tailor's plan (free vs pro) is also unconfirmed; with the backstop added this pass, builderforce now *funds* the paid fallback for free-plan calls (~$0.0001/call by design). The hired.video repo is not in this workspace. Fixing (in hired.video: drop the client-side cascade ŌĆö send one request with no `model` hint and let the gateway route; remove the `claude-3-haiku` pin) and confirming the intended billing posture for tailor unblocks: no wasted duplicate attempts, no doomed deprecated-model pins, and clarity on who pays for the free-tier backstop.

- **Gateway + agent-runtime prompt-cache TTL is fixed at 5-minute ephemeral ŌĆö no 1-hour opt-in.** This pass wired Anthropic prompt-cache breakpoints into the gateway request path ([promptCaching.ts](api/src/application/llm/promptCaching.ts) ŌåÆ injected in [openrouter.ts `buildBody`](api/src/application/llm/vendors/openrouter.ts)) and into agent-runtime's OpenRouter/Anthropic system prompt ([extra-params.ts `addAnthropicSystemCacheControl`](agent-runtime/src/agents/pi-embedded-runner/extra-params.ts)), completing the caching+metering pair the gateway already read via [`pickUsage`](api/src/application/llm/vendors/types.ts) (`cache_read_tokens`/`cache_creation_tokens`). Both always emit `cache_control: { type: 'ephemeral' }` (5-min TTL). For bursty tenants with a large stable prefix and gaps >5 min between calls, a 1-hour TTL (`{ type: 'ephemeral', ttl: '1h' }`, ~2x write cost) would keep the prefix warm across idle gaps ŌĆö pi-ai already supports this for *direct* Anthropic via `cacheRetention: 'long'`, but the gateway/OpenRouter path doesn't expose it. Fixing (a per-request `_builderforce: { cacheTtl: '1h' }` hint / per-`useCase` profile that flips the marker, in both surfaces) unblocks: cache hits across multi-minute idle gaps for high-prefix tenants. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 (T3) ŌĆö gateway side shipped.** `_builderforce.cacheTtl:'1h'` is now honoured end-to-end on the gateway: [promptCaching.ts](api/src/application/llm/promptCaching.ts) `applyPromptCaching(messages, model, ttl)` emits `{ type:'ephemeral', ttl:'1h' }` on every breakpoint when requested; the hint is read by `resolveCacheTtl` in [LlmProxyService.ts](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts), threaded through `dispatch` ŌåÆ `VendorCallParams.cacheTtl` ŌåÆ [openrouter.ts `buildBody`](api/src/application/llm/vendors/openrouter.ts) (the only vendor that needs the marker). The `_builderforce` envelope is still stripped before vendor dispatch, so the hint never reaches the upstream as a body field. tsc 0 + new TTL unit tests. **Still open:** the agent-runtime surface (T5) ŌĆö wiring `cacheTtl:'1h'` / `cacheRetention:'long'` through pi-ai's direct-Anthropic path ŌĆö and an optional per-`useCase` profile that auto-selects 1h.

- **No per-tenant cap on the always-on premium fallback chain.** [LlmProxyService.PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) is appended to every non-strict candidate chain (Free plan included) ŌĆö when the (now 2-attempt-capped) free section is exhausted, the proxy falls through to `googleai/gemini-2.5-flash` ŌåÆ `googleai/gemini-2.5-flash-lite` ŌåÆ OpenRouter `google/gemini-2.5-flash-lite` so callers never see a cascade-exhausted 429. The residual risk: a Free-plan tenant in a tight retry loop can drive arbitrary spend against the Builderforce `GOOGLE_API_KEY` / `OPENROUTER_API_KEY` because there's no per-tenant overflow cap or daily budget on the premium-fallback path, and the new 2-free-cap means the cascade reaches paid endpoints *faster* than the previous design. Fixing (track premium-fallback hits in `llm_usage_log` against a per-tenant `paid_overflow_daily_cap`, default ~$0.50/day, and surface the cap in the superadmin tenants page) unblocks: hard ceiling on overflow cost while preserving the "zero `LLM_UNAVAILABLE` escapes" guarantee. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 (T3) ŌĆö backend shipped (migration 0130, not yet applied to any live DB).** [Migration 0130](api/migrations/0130_paid_overflow_cap.sql) adds `tenants.paid_overflow_daily_cap` (millicents; NULL ŌåÆ plan default = $0.50/day free, unlimited pro/teams; -1 = unlimited) and `llm_usage_log.paid_overflow` (+ partial index). The proxy now classifies a funded-overflow resolution via `isPaidOverflowModel` (premium-fallback Ōł¬ backstop models) and stamps `ProxyResult.paidOverflow`, which both gateway surfaces write to the usage row. A new `disablePaidOverflow` option on `LlmProxyService`/`llmProxyForPlan` drops the premium-fallback chain AND skips the backstop; the route helper `isPaidOverflowExhausted` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) sums today's overflow `cost_usd_millicents` and flips it once the cap is hit ŌĆö so the tenant's PRIMARY pool keeps serving while the funded path is closed (preserving the guarantee for tenants under cap). `resolvePaidOverflowCapMillicents` ([usageLedger.ts](api/src/application/llm/usageLedger.ts)) is the single cap-resolution source. tsc 0 + new overflow tests. ~~**Still open:** (1) apply migration 0130 to the live DB; (2) surface/edit the cap in the superadmin tenants page (frontend ŌĆö T2/T7); (3) image-gen overflow (FluxAPI premium fallback) is not yet classified (separate from the chat path).~~ **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-21 (operator confirmed migration 0130 + all commits deployed).** (1) Deployed. (2) **Superadmin cap editor shipped** ŌĆö new `PATCH /api/admin/tenants/:id/paid-overflow-cap` ([adminRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/adminRoutes.ts), audit event `PAID_OVERFLOW_CAP_CHANGED`, mirrors the token-limit-override route) + `paid_overflow_daily_cap` on the admin tenants list query; `adminApi.setTenantPaidOverflowCap` + a new dollar-denominated [TenantPaidOverflowCapEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/admin/TenantPaidOverflowCapEditor.tsx) (plan-default / unlimited / custom-$ Ōåö millicents) rendered in BOTH admin tenant views alongside the token + premium editors. (3) **Image-gen overflow now classified + capped** ŌĆö `ImageProxyResult.paidOverflow` (true only when the funded `PREMIUM_IMAGE_FALLBACK_MODELS` serves, via new exported `isImagePaidOverflowModel`), a `disablePaidOverflow` option on `ImageProxyService`/`imageProxyForPlan` that drops the FluxAPI fallback, and the image route ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts) `POST /v1/images/generations`) now calls the SAME shared `isPaidOverflowExhausted` gate and stamps `paidOverflow` on the image usage row ŌĆö so a Free tenant over its daily cap stops billing our FluxAPI key (free pool still serves) exactly like the chat path. api 1136 + frontend 286 tests green; both typecheck clean; schema-drift/migrations/tracks pass.

- **Pro plan's free-tier section is now also capped at 2 attempts.** [LlmProxyService.FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) (= 2) is applied universally in `buildCandidateChain`, so Pro tenants' cascade is `[2 free, ...PRO_PAID_MODEL_POOL, ...PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS]` instead of the previous "walk all free + all paid + cross-vendor" chain. Net effect is positive (Pro tenants reach their paid premium models faster) but the design is uniform with Free plan ŌĆö there is no Pro-specific carve-out that, say, lets Pro tenants try 5 free models before paying. If Pro customers report missing free-tier breadth, the fix is to take `FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET` from a plan-aware lookup instead of a single constant. Fixing unblocks: plan-tier-differentiated cascade depth.

- ~~**Image gen shares the chat per-tenant daily token budget at a flat 1000-tok/image rate.**~~ **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-21 ŌĆö chat tokens and image credits are now SEPARATE budgets.** [Migration 0131](api/migrations/0131_image_credits_daily_limit.sql) adds `tenants.image_credits_daily_limit` (override: null ŌåÆ plan default, -1 ŌåÆ unlimited, Ōēź0 ŌåÆ explicit). Plan defaults in [PlanLimits.ts](api/src/domain/tenant/PlanLimits.ts) (`imageCreditsDailyLimit`: free 10 / pro 1000 / teams 5000) + single-source resolver `resolveImageCreditsDailyLimit`. Gateway changes ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)): (a) the chat token-cap query now **EXCLUDES** image-product rows (`notInArray(llm_product, IMAGE_PRODUCT_NAMES)`), so image usage no longer eats the text budget (or vice-versa); (b) new `enforceImageCreditCap` gate runs BEFORE image dispatch ŌĆö sums today's image-product usage (`total_tokens / IMAGE_TOKEN_COST`, the shared constant) and returns a distinct `image_credit_limit_exceeded` 429 (with `Retry-After` to UTC midnight) when over budget; superadmin + unlimited skip, query fails open. `image_credits_daily_limit` threaded through `resolveTenantPlan`/`TenantAccess`. Superadmin can set the per-tenant override in the admin tenants page via a new `IMAGE_CREDITS_LIMIT_CHANGED`-audited `PATCH /api/admin/tenants/:id/image-credits-limit` + `TenantImageCreditsEditor`. **DRY:** the three near-identical override editors (token cap / paid-overflow cap / image credits) were consolidated onto one shared [TenantIntegerOverrideEditor](frontend/src/components/admin/TenantIntegerOverrideEditor.tsx) (null/-1/custom semantics, per-kind label+unit+transform config). api 1141 + frontend 286 tests green; schema-drift/migrations/tracks pass.

- **Gateway keys, usage metering, and rate limiting are tenant-only ŌĆö no segment dimension.** `tenantApiKeys` and claw keys map to a tenant; `llm_usage_log` and `TenantRateLimiterDO` meter/limit per tenant. An integrator calling the gateway/SDK can't say which end-client a call is for. Fixing (add `segment_id` to keys + usage log + a segment header on `/v1/*`, namespace the rate-limiter DO by `tenant:segment`) unblocks: per-segment metering, quotas, and chargeback for integrators reselling the platform.

- **Spec assumes a per-Segment credit ledger + `viewer` projection + `AI_USE_CASES`/`callAiAndCharge` facade that does not exist in BuilderForce.** Doc 01 ┬¦8 / doc 05 ┬¦6 lean on BurnRateOS's AI facade; the BuilderForce gateway meters per *tenant* via `llm_usage_log` + plan token limits with no `AI_USE_CASES` registry, no `viewer`, no segment dimension (grep: no `AI_USE_CASES`/`callAiAndCharge`). Extends the per-segment-metering gap above. Fixing (port the use-case registry + per-segment credit ledger + viewer-projection into BuilderForce, or map them onto the existing gateway primitives with a `segment_id` added to usage) unblocks: the `dev.*` + `pm.*`/`agile.*` use cases billing per end-client as the spec requires.

- **Project modality entitlement gate is partial ŌĆö the `comingSoon` flag gates the LLM modality, but the Pro+ paid gate for Video can't be enforced client-side because the frontend `Tenant` type carries no plan/tier field.** [frontend/src/components/IDENew.tsx](frontend/src/components/IDENew.tsx) disables `comingSoon` modalities in the switcher (config-driven from [frontend/src/lib/modality.ts](frontend/src/lib/modality.ts)), so the mechanism exists. But [frontend/src/lib/types.ts](frontend/src/lib/types.ts) `Tenant` exposes only `{ id, name, slug, role }` ŌĆö no plan ŌĆö so the agreed Pro+ gate on the heavy Video modality has no data source to read. Fixing (surface the tenant plan/tier on the `Tenant` object via the auth/tenant token claim or a `/api/tenants/:id` fetch, add a `requiresPaidPlan` flag to the Video `ModalityDef`, and gate the switcher on it) unblocks: revenue protection on the 6GB-VRAM modality.

- **Free tier is capped to diagnostic + recommendation by design; Pro multi-repo/large-repo evidence trimming is still coarse.** `planConfig` in [AnalysisRunnerDO.ts](api/src/infrastructure/relay/AnalysisRunnerDO.ts) gives Free 2 artifacts / ~9k tokens and Pro all 6 / ~120k, with `selectEvidence` sized per-repo. Very large or many-repo Pro projects can still overflow a single artifact's prompt budget (no cross-repo prioritization, no per-artifact evidence subsetting). Fixing (rank repos by relevance, subset evidence per artifact kind, summarize-then-analyze for huge trees) unblocks: reliable full analysis on monorepos / large estates.

- **Publishing an agent sets `published`+price but agents are NOT yet a marketplace artifact type, so there is no purchase/payout path.** The marketplace artifact enum is `skill | persona | content` ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)); `marketplace_purchases` + the Stripe-intent purchase route ([marketplaceRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/marketplaceRoutes.ts)) don't know about agents. So a published agent's price is stored + displayed but cannot actually be transacted, and "revenue" isn't collected/paid out. Fixing (add `'agent'` to `artifactTypeEnum`, surface published agents in the marketplace listing/detail, and wire the purchase + payout path for agents) unblocks: real agent monetization end-to-end.

- **"Hire" is still only a counter ŌĆö it does not provision/deploy the agent.** [POST /api/ide/agents/:id/hire](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts) increments `hire_count`; there's no instantiation of the hired agent into the hirer's workspace (no claw bind / cloud-runtime registration). Fixing (on hire, create a tenant-scoped agent instance or bind to a runtime per the agent's `runtime_support`) unblocks: hiring that actually puts an agent to work.

- **The new IDE dashboard exposes a "New Video project" create path with no Pro+ entitlement gate.** [/ide/dashboard](frontend/src/app/ide/dashboard/page.tsx) renders a project-type chooser (Designer / Video / LLM) driven by [modality.ts](frontend/src/lib/modality.ts) and calls `createProject({ modality })` directly ŌĆö so a free-plan tenant can now create a `video` project and open the heavy (6 GB-VRAM) Video modality from the launcher, not just via the in-IDE switcher. This is the same root gap already logged above ("Project modality entitlement gate is partial ŌĆ” the frontend `Tenant` type carries no plan/tier field"): the chooser only honors `comingSoon`, and Video isn't `comingSoon`. Fixing (surface tenant plan/tier on the `Tenant` object, add a `requiresPaidPlan` flag to the Video `ModalityDef`, and gate both the dashboard chooser card AND the IDE switcher on it ŌĆö one shared check) unblocks: revenue protection on the Video modality across every create surface. Bundle with the existing partial-gate entry ŌĆö same fix closes both.

### ­¤ÜĆ Open ŌĆö Growth / acquisition & retention (10)

_SEO, marketing surfaces, onboarding / connect flow, public & embed presence, funnel capture, notifications._

- **`builderforce.ai/docs/*` proxy ŌĆö needs deploy + one post-deploy verification.** Live symptom was `404` on *every* `/docs/*` path. **Corrected root cause** (the earlier "stale artifact built before `base:/docs`" theory was wrong ŌĆö disproven by `https://builderforce-docs.pages.dev/agents-overview` serving real content while `.../docs/agents-overview` 404s): Astro `base: '/docs'` only prefixes the emitted *links/assets*, it does **not** nest the build *output* ŌĆö content is written to `dist/` root and served at the pages.dev **root** (`pages.dev/agents`, `pages.dev/_astro/*`). The apex proxy in [frontend/next.config.js](frontend/next.config.js) was forwarding `/docs/* ŌåÆ pages.dev/docs/*` (a path that doesn't exist), so all paths 404'd. **Fixed this pass** by making the proxy **strip** the `/docs` prefix (`/docs/:path* ŌåÆ pages.dev/:path*`), and by relocating the rebrand redirect stubs to `dist` root (dropped `/docs` from the `redirects` *source* keys in [docs-site/astro.config.mjs](docs-site/astro.config.mjs), kept it in destinations). Both ship on the next push to `main` (frontend `build-and-deploy` + `deploy-docs`); the content fix only needs the frontend redeploy. **Remaining follow-up:** verify post-deploy that `@cloudflare/next-on-pages` actually *proxies* the external rewrite via `fetch` rather than 301-redirecting to `builderforce-docs.pages.dev` ŌĆö some versions mishandle absolute-URL `dest`. If the URL bar changes / goes cross-origin, fall back to a Cloudflare Workers Route `builderforce.ai/docs/*` ŌåÆ tiny proxy worker, or bind the docs project to `docs.builderforce.ai`. Fixing unblocks: every `/docs/*` link across the marketing site resolving same-origin.

- **Marketing / public-shell pages still center on `.page-inner`; not migrated to the new `PageContainer`.** This pass introduced [PageContainer](frontend/src/components/PageContainer.tsx) (`full` / `readable` / `narrow` width tiers, all left-aligned to kill the sidebar-gutter gap) and migrated every authenticated AppShell route plus `/prompts`, `/admin/llm-traces`, and `.admin-page` onto it. Deliberately left on their existing centered layout: `/marketplace` + `/models` (shared `.page-inner` = `max-width:1100px; margin:0 auto` in [globals.css](frontend/src/app/globals.css)) and the pure-marketing routes (`/pricing`, `/blog`, `/product`, `/`), because their hero-style centered design is intentional. They render in the same `PublicShell` `Sidebar`+`.content`, so when signed in they show the same left gutter the user flagged. Fixing (decide per-page whether marketing centering should yield to left-aligned `PageContainer`, then migrate `.page-inner` consumers and retire the class) unblocks: one consistent page-width primitive across the whole app, no parallel `.page-inner` / `PageContainer` width systems.

- **Marketplace / prompt detail views are client-side overlays with no per-entity route ŌĆö individual agents, skills, personas, and prompts are unindexable and have no rich link previews.** Both [marketplace/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/marketplace/page.tsx) and [prompts/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/prompts/page.tsx) open detail in an in-page modal/drawer, so there is no `/marketplace/{slug}` or `/prompts/{slug}` URL. The listing pages now have per-page metadata + a dynamic OG image (added this pass via [seo.ts](frontend/src/lib/seo.ts) + [og.tsx](frontend/src/lib/og.tsx)), but an individual published agent/skill/prompt has no crawlable page, no per-entity `<title>`/description/JSON-LD, and no per-entity OG card. Fixing (add server `ŌĆ”/[slug]/page.tsx` routes with `generateMetadata` driven by a shared `buildEntitySeo(kind, record)` adapter + a per-entity `opengraph-image.tsx`, and emit them into [sitemap.ts](frontend/src/app/sitemap.ts) from the live API ŌĆö cached read-through, verified/public-only, thin-entity gated) unblocks: indexable long-tail marketplace/prompt pages and correct Slack/LinkedIn/X previews when a specific agent or prompt is shared. This is the SPA-style "UGC detail" surface the marketing-presence review flagged. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 ŌĆö skills detail surface shipped (the registryŌĆÖs public face).** New SSR `/marketplace/[slug]` route (+ dynamic `opengraph-image`) over a cached, increment-free public read (`GET /marketplace/skills/:slug?seo=1` via `getOrSetCached`, invalidated on PUT) with `generateMetadata` + a `marketplaceSkillSchema` JSON-LD graph, emitted into [sitemap.ts](frontend/src/app/sitemap.ts) from the live published-skills list (best-effort). api + frontend `tsc` 0. **Still open:** per-entity public routes for prompts, personas, and published *agents* need their own public read endpoints + slug surfaces.

- **`/skills/[slug]` and `/personas/[slug]` carry edge-runtime + OG-image scaffolding yet are crawler-blocked and absent from the sitemap.** Both routes ([skills/[slug]/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/skills/%5Bslug%5D/page.tsx), [personas/[slug]/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/personas/%5Bslug%5D/page.tsx)) run on the edge and look intended for public sharing, but `/skills` and `/personas` are `Disallow`-ed in [robots.txt](frontend/public/robots.txt) (they double as authenticated app surfaces) and neither appears in [sitemap.ts](frontend/src/app/sitemap.ts). So if these detail pages are meant to be the public, shareable face of a published skill/persona, they are currently invisible to search + AI crawlers; if they are purely in-app, the per-route edge runtime is dead ceremony. Fixing (decide public-vs-app: either split a public `/workforce/skills/{slug}` surface with metadata + sitemap + a robots `Allow`, or drop the edge runtime and treat them as app-only) unblocks: a coherent public/app boundary and, if public, skill/persona SEO. Related to the marketplace-detail entry above ŌĆö same "Workforce content has no public, indexable home" root cause. **UPDATE 2026-06-14:** the sibling programmatic-SEO surface (`/compare/{slug}`, `/integrations/{slug}`) now provides the public, indexable home for comparison/integration intent (robots `Allow` + sitemap); the skills/personas public-vs-app split itself remains the open decision here.

- **`/agents/*` marketing pages lost their `.cc-shell` background wrapper.** [agents/layout.tsx](frontend/src/app/agents/layout.tsx) was simplified to a pass-through now that PublicShell provides the chrome; the old layout set `background: var(--bg-deep)` on a `.cc-shell` wrapper. The agents pages now inherit the global shell background. Verify the agents showcase/integrations/skills/shoutouts pages still read correctly; if any relied on `.cc-*` ambient styling (from the deleted MarketingNav style block), restyle them. Fixing unblocks: confirmed visual parity for the /agents cluster. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 (T1):** the code-level risk this flags ŌĆö a page still depending on the deleted `.cc-*` styles ŌĆö is **cleared**: a repo-wide grep finds **zero `cc-shell` / `.cc-*` references** in `frontend/src`, so nothing is left styling against the removed wrapper. Only the human visual spot-check of the /agents cluster remains (needs eyes on the rendered page; not a code change).

- **Per-route marketing teasers for authed routes are not indexable (SEO opportunity).** Logged-out visitors hitting an authed route now get a feature teaser + login/CTA via [RouteMarketing](frontend/src/components/RouteMarketing.tsx) + [routeMarketing.ts](frontend/src/lib/routeMarketing.ts) (gated in [ConditionalAppShell](frontend/src/components/ConditionalAppShell.tsx); middleware no longer redirects them to /login). But those routes stay `Disallow`-ed in [robots.txt](frontend/public/robots.txt) and the authed pages are client components with no `generateMetadata`, so the teasers render the root default `<title>` and aren't crawlable. They could become real per-feature SEO landing pages (e.g. `/ide` ŌåÆ "In-browser IDE for AI agents"). Fixing (allow select feature routes in robots, add `generateMetadata` per route ŌĆö or canonicalize them to `/product#<section>` ŌĆö and emit to the sitemap) unblocks: a feature-landing-page long-tail without building separate marketing URLs. `/debug` intentionally uses the generic default teaser (internal route, no marketing copy needed). **UPDATE 2026-06-14:** `/compare` + `/integrations` are now in `robots.txt` Allow + `sitemap.ts`; the authed feature-route teasers (`/ide`, etc.) remain `Disallow`-ed with no per-route `generateMetadata` ŌĆö still open.

- **Landing-page prompt ŌåÆ Brain handoff routes into the internal tool/action registry only ŌĆö no real MCP (Model Context Protocol) backend.** The home-page prompt input ([frontend/src/app/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/page.tsx)) saves the visitor's prompt and the global Brain replays it after auth ([pendingPrompt.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/pendingPrompt.ts) + [FloatingBrain.tsx](frontend/src/components/brain/FloatingBrain.tsx) ŌåÆ [BrainPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) `initialPrompt`). "MCP-ing" the request currently means the Brain acts via its existing in-app action registry ([BrainActionsContext.tsx](frontend/src/lib/brain/BrainActionsContext.tsx)) ŌĆö there is no MCP client/connector that calls external MCP servers (Gmail, Drive, Calendar, etc.). Fixing (a real MCP connector layer: server registry, OAuth, tool discovery, and a bridge from `BrainActionsContext` tool specs to MCP `tools/call`) unblocks: the Brain acting on external systems over the actual protocol, not just registered page actions.

- **Pending-prompt capture is `localStorage`-only ŌĆö single browser, not cross-device.** [savePendingPrompt/takePendingPrompt](frontend/src/lib/brain/pendingPrompt.ts) stash the landing prompt in `localStorage`, so a visitor who types on their phone then signs up on their laptop loses the prompt. Per the product decision (2026-05-31) this pass deliberately skipped a server-side anonymous record. Fixing (a public `POST /api/pending-prompts` keyed by an anonymous session id + a `pending_prompts` table with TTL/expiry, associated to the user on first authenticated request) unblocks: cross-device prompt continuity and analytics on abandoned prompts. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 ŌĆö durable server record + claim shipped.** New `pending_prompts` table ([migration 0128](api/migrations/0128_pending_prompts.sql), **not yet applied to any live DB**), public `POST /api/pending-prompts` (fired best-effort from the landing page alongside the localStorage save) + web-authed `POST /api/pending-prompts/claim` that stamps `user_id`+`claimed_at` and replays through the BrainŌĆÖs `FloatingBrain` fallback ([pendingPromptRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/pendingPromptRoutes.ts)). Adds durability, abandoned-prompt analytics, and same-browser recovery after a storage clear. **Still open:** true phoneŌåÆlaptop continuity ŌĆö the claim is keyed by a per-browser `anon_id`, so the anonId must still be threaded through the signup link/email to reconnect across *different* browsers.

- **Deploy notifications shipped (in-app auto-reload banner + OS Web Push); fan-out is synchronous/unbounded, untested in CI, and only fires from the `cf-deploy` path.** This pass made the PWA actually surface new versions on every deploy: (a) [public/sw.js](frontend/public/sw.js) now carries a per-build `__BUILD_VERSION__` stamp ([scripts/stamp-sw-version.js](frontend/scripts/stamp-sw-version.js)) so the SW bytes change each deploy (root cause the banner never showed); (b) [PwaUpdateBanner.tsx](frontend/src/components/PwaUpdateBanner.tsx) checks for updates on focus/visibility/online and auto-reloads after a 60s countdown; (c) real Web Push ŌĆö [webPush.ts](api/src/application/notifications/webPush.ts) (VAPID ES256 + RFC 8291 `aes128gcm`, pure Web Crypto, no Node dep), [pushSubscriptionRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/pushSubscriptionRoutes.ts) (`/api/push/{public-key,subscribe,notify-deploy}`), `push_subscriptions` (migration [0126](api/migrations/0126_push_subscriptions.sql)), SW `push`/`notificationclick` handlers, [pushNotifications.ts](frontend/src/lib/pushNotifications.ts) client + [DeployNotificationsManager.tsx](frontend/src/components/DeployNotificationsManager.tsx) opt-in; (d) [notify-deploy.mjs](frontend/scripts/notify-deploy.mjs) wired into `cf-deploy`. **Residuals:** (1) [deployNotificationService.ts](api/src/application/notifications/deployNotificationService.ts) selects ALL subscriptions with no LIMIT and fans out synchronously in 50-wide batches inside the request ŌĆö a large subscriber base risks the Worker subrequest/CPU ceiling and a slow deploy-script call; needs a Cloudflare Queue (none bound in `wrangler.toml`) or a cron-batched fan-out. (2) No automated test for the VAPID/`aes128gcm` crypto in-repo ŌĆö it was validated this pass only via a throwaway Node signŌåÆverify + encryptŌåÆdecrypt round-trip; add a vitest that asserts the encrypt path decrypts with a known client keypair. (3) Push fires ONLY when a deploy runs `npm run cf-deploy`; a direct `wrangler deploy` or a CI path that doesn't call the hook won't notify, and the feature is inert until `VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY`/`VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY`/`VAPID_SUBJECT`/`DEPLOY_NOTIFY_SECRET` secrets are provisioned (`node api/scripts/gen-vapid-keys.mjs` then `wrangler secret put`). (4) The deploy push targets every subscription globally (correct for an app-version event) but there's no per-user notification preference beyond browser-level unsubscribe. Fixing (1)+(2) unblocks: a deploy fan-out that scales past a handful of users and is regression-guarded. **UPDATE 2026-06-14 ŌĆö REMOVED. Push is the host platform's job (BurnRateOS.com), not Builderforce's, so the entire self-hosted Web Push stack was deleted: frontend `pushNotifications.ts`/`DeployNotificationsManager.tsx`/`notify-deploy.mjs` + the SW `push`/`notificationclick` handlers, and backend `pushSubscriptionRoutes.ts`/`webPush.ts`/`deployNotificationService.ts`/`push_subscriptions` (dropped in [migration 0195](api/migrations/0195_drop_push_subscriptions.sql), **not yet applied to any live DB**) + the `VAPID_*`/`DEPLOY_NOTIFY_SECRET` env and `gen-vapid-keys.mjs`. This resolves the `api.builderforce.ai/api/push/public-key` 503 (VAPID was never provisioned because push was never Builderforce's responsibility) and closes residuals (1)ŌĆō(4) above. The in-app `PwaUpdateBanner` auto-reload (separate from push) is unaffected. Open: BurnRateOS must own the OS-level "new version" notification if that UX is still wanted; Builderforce no longer emits it.

- **Voice marketing-accuracy (#1991) + consent/provenance gate (#1996) are unaddressed in this pass.** The PRD's `VIBEVOICE_AVAILABLE`/`VIBEVOICE_CDN` flags and the Pricing/comparison copy claiming VibeVoice is live were **not found in the repo** (no `frontend/lib/services/tts-engines.ts`), so there was nothing to scope here ŌĆö but the marketing-accuracy obligation stands once a real UI lands: do not imply cloning is live until #1994 ships. Separately, the consent attestation (`consent_attested_at` + `consent_text_version` on `studio_voice_clones`, ToS ┬¦9a), provenance disclosure on published listings, moderation gate on publish, and right-to-delete cache invalidation (PRD ┬¦5) are **not built** ŌĆö they gate GA and depend on the `studio_voice_clones` table existing (#1994). The npm client carries `verifySpeaker` (re-upload identity check) as a building block. Building ┬¦5 unblocks legal GA of human-voice cloning.

### ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Open ŌĆö Core product capability (190)

_The product itself: cloud-agent execution, engines & tools, PR/repo loop, IDE, Studio (video/voice), workflows, boards, brain, QA, observability._

- **Brain-driven writes only refresh the Tasks board ŌĆö other data views still go stale until manual reload (2026-06-14).** A generic refresh bus now exists ([brainDataEvent.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/brainDataEvent.ts): mutating platform capabilities `dispatchBrainDataChanged({domain,method})`; consumers subscribe via `onBrainDataChanged`), but only [TaskMgmtContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) subscribes (domains `tasks`/`executions`/`projects`). Every other page that holds its own list state and can be mutated by the Brain ŌĆö Projects list, Specs/PRD list, Workflows, Workforce/agents, Boards/swimlanes, Prompts ŌĆö still shows stale data after a Brain action until the user reloads. Fixing (one `onBrainDataChanged([...], reload)` effect per view) closes the BrainŌåöUI staleness gap platform-wide.

- **Remove `@mariozechner/pi-*` entirely ŌĆö ONLY `pi-tui` remains; the blocker is the atomic `src/tui`ŌåÆ`ink` flip.** `pi-agent-core`, `pi-ai`, and `pi-coding-agent` are at **0 imports and removed from `agent-runtime/package.json`** (the loop, model client, tools, OAuth/Codex, and embedded runner are all native/pi-free). `@mariozechner/pi-tui` is the **last** dep: ~6,500 LOC of interactive CLI (`agent-runtime/src/tui/*`, 17 component sites ŌĆö `Container`/`Markdown`/`Editor`/`SelectList`/`SettingsList`/`Component`/`TUI`/ŌĆ”). **Ō£ģ Built 2026-06-14 ŌĆö the ink replacement is real, not a skeleton:** `@builderforce/tui`'s [ink-renderer.ts](packages/tui/src/adapters/ink-renderer.ts) now mounts a live `ink`(^7)+`react`(^19) render tree (chat scrollback, status footer, history-aware input editor, focus-trapping `select`/`settings`/`confirm` overlays) behind the `TuiRenderer` port; `TextMetrics` is `string-width`/`cli-truncate`-backed; the two `pi-tui` text-metric sites (`tui-overlays`, `searchable-select-list`) already moved to a native `truncateToWidth` in `terminal/ansi.ts` (`ansi.test.ts`). `@builderforce/tui` `tsc` 0. **Ō£ģ Wired into `agent-runtime` 2026-06-14:** [renderer-registry.ts](agent-runtime/src/tui/renderer-registry.ts) (composition root: `headless`+`ink` registry, default ink, `resolveTuiRenderer`) + [ink-session.ts](agent-runtime/src/tui/ink-session.ts) `runInkSession` ŌĆö a complete runnable ink chat loop through the port (inputŌåÆ`chat.send`; gateway `chat`/`agent` eventsŌåÆchat surface via the renderer-agnostic `TuiStreamAssembler`), reachable today via `BUILDERFORCE_AGENTS_INK_TUI=1 builderforce tui`; the `wireInkSession` core is DI'd + headlessly unit-tested (`ink-session.test.ts`, 6 tests). `tsgo` 0, 138 `src/tui` tests green. **Remaining (TTY-verified):** bring `runInkSession` to parity with the legacy pi-tui `runTui` (slash-command autocomplete, bash mode, session switching, verbose stats), flip the default, then delete the legacy pi-tui `src/tui` components and drop `@mariozechner/pi-tui` from [package.json](agent-runtime/package.json). Fixing unblocks the last third-party agent-framework dependency leaving the runtime.

- **TUI render seam built (`@builderforce/tui`) ŌĆö the 18-site `pi-tui` migration + live `ink` render tree are the deferred tail (terminal-verified).** The framework-agnostic `TuiRenderer` contract + DI `RendererRegistry` + headless renderer + `ink` adapter skeleton landed ([packages/tui/](packages/tui/), `tsc` 0); see the pi-cutover entry's pass-14 update + [specs/builderforce/11-prd-engine-consolidation.md](specs/builderforce/11-prd-engine-consolidation.md) ┬¦5.1 Stage 4. **Remaining:** (a) migrate the 18 `@mariozechner/pi-tui` import-sites in `agent-runtime/src/tui/*` onto the port (they extend pi's `Component`/`Container`/`Editor`/`SelectList` classes directly ŌĆö reexpress as view-intent); (b) build the live `ink` render tree in [ink-renderer.ts](packages/tui/src/adapters/ink-renderer.ts) (`start()` currently throws; add `ink`/`react`, swap placeholder width metrics for `string-width`/`cli-truncate`); (c) drop `pi-tui` from `agent-runtime/package.json` + `pnpm install`; (d) the On-Prem default-engine decision. Fixing unblocks: the last `@mariozechner/pi-*` dependency removal + a swappable terminal framework.

- **Cloud agents are wired but only happy-path validated ŌĆö 50 gaps catalogued, none yet closed.** A new PRD ([specs/builderforce/09-prd-cloud-agent-validation.md](specs/builderforce/09-prd-cloud-agent-validation.md)) summarizes the three cloud execution paths (V1 pi loop, V2 Claude Agent SDK, cloud-Worker fallback) and enumerates 50 falsifiable gaps across dispatch, workspace/PR lifecycle, engine parity, steering/cancel, telemetry integrity, billing/BYO-key, and security/isolation. P0 highlights: cloud V2 runs `bypassPermissions` + Bash on shared infra with no documented sandbox (GAP-G1); cloud-Worker fallback has no steering/cancel honoring (GAP-S5/S6); no test reconstructs a run from `tool_audit_events`+`usage_snapshots`+`llm_usage_log` by `execution_id` (GAP-O1) nor asserts ledger==snapshot (GAP-O2); errored/cancelled runs leak the task workspace (GAP-W2); BYO-key-missing may silently fall to platform-billed key (GAP-B2). Fixing (execute PRD 09 phases 9aŌåÆ9d, starting with telemetry/billing integrity then isolation, plus a `pnpm qa:cloud-agents` golden-path E2E) unblocks: cloud agents shippable as a GA runtime alongside self-hosted hosts.

- **Shared tool-catalogue status: 12 cross-runtime core tools + 21 Node-native tools are now under the shared `@builderforce/agent-tools` contract (33 total); ~6 remaining (`github_issue_workflow` + media `message`/`tts`/`canvas`/`image`/`browser`) need porting ŌĆö media first needs a `ToolResult.content` block extension (text-only `data` can't carry images/audio/MEDIA tokens) (updated 2026-06-13).** **Cross-runtime core (12), defined directly in [core-tools.ts](packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts)** and capability-gated/backed per surface: list_files, search_code, read_file, write_file, **edit_file** (cap `repo.edit`; cloud [read+commit] + Node [disk], NOT the container ŌĆö its image only commits whole files), delete_file, run_checks, run_command, **web_fetch** (cap `web`; Node-backed via global `fetch`+HTMLŌåÆtext), **web_search** (cap `web.search`; defined, no backend advertised yet), ask_human, finish. **Node-native (21), 2026-06-13:** code-intelligence (5) in [node-code-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-code-tools.ts) ŌĆö `git_history` (cap `shell`), `code_analysis`/`project_knowledge`/`codebase_search`/`codebase_semantic_search` (cap `repo.read`), read the working tree via `ctx.workspaceRoot`; orchestration/session (4) in [node-orchestration-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-orchestration-tools.ts) ŌĆö `orchestrate`/`agent_fleet`/`workflow_status` (cap `orchestrate`), `save_session_handoff` (cap `memory`); service/session (12) built by the **`buildNodeServiceTools(deps)` factory** (DI seam over a `NodeServiceToolDeps` bag) in [node-service-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-service-tools.ts) + co-located `build*ToolDef` exports in their `agents/tools/*` files ŌĆö `agents_list`/`sessions_list`/`sessions_history`/`sessions_spawn`/`session_status`/`subagents` (cap `orchestrate`), `sessions_send` (cap `message`), `gateway` (cap `process`), `nodes` (cap `orchestrate`), `cron` (cap `orchestrate`), `memory_search`/`memory_get` (cap `memory`, emitted only when config resolves). These reuse the existing TypeBox schema verbatim (TypeBox *is* JSON Schema) and share ONE body via an exported `run*()` that the pi wrapper also calls; `detailsData`/`nativeToolData` ([common.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/tools/common.ts)) bridge the legacy `AgentToolResult` to the native `ToolResult.data` (throw-safe). `NODE_SURFACE_CAPS` advertises `orchestrate`/`memory`/`message`. `buildNodeToolRegistry(deps?)` assembles core + code + orchestration + service; the `builderforce-local` engine wires it + threads `workspaceRoot`. Tested in [node-code-tools.test.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-code-tools.test.ts) + [node-registry.test.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-registry.test.ts). The legacy pi files still hold the `AgentTool` shape ONLY because the still-default pi loop consumes it ŌĆö deleted in cutover stage 3 (above). **Remaining (~6): `github_issue_workflow` (JSON, portable now); media `message`/`tts`/`canvas`/`image`/`browser`** ŌĆö these return content blocks (images/audio/MEDIA tokens) the text-only `ToolResult.data` can't carry, so they need a `ToolResult.content` extension to the shared contract + engine handling before porting (logged below).

- **Shared `ToolResult` is text/JSON-only (`data`) ŌĆö it cannot carry media (image/audio) content blocks, blocking native ports of `tts`/`canvas`/`image`/`browser`/`message`** ([tool.ts](packages/agent-tools/src/tool.ts) `ToolResult` has `data` + `control` but no `content`). The legacy pi tools return `{content:[...]}` (image blocks, `MEDIA:` tokens, `[[audio_as_voice]]`) the on-prem channel layer delivers. Fixing = add an optional `content?: ToolContentBlock[]` to `ToolResult`, have the engines (LocalAgentEngine sinks + cloud loop) surface it, then port the 5 media/channel tools via `buildNodeServiceTools(deps)`. Unblocks the final tool-layer (cutover stage 1) tools + true media parity on the native engine.

- **On-prem `ask_human` is NOT offered through the shared Node registry ŌĆö the Node `CapabilityProvider` does not advertise the `human` capability** ([node-capability-provider.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-capability-provider.ts) `NODE_SURFACE_CAPS` omits `human`; the legacy on-prem loop wires its own ask-human). So an agent on the `builderforce-local` engine cannot pause for a human via the shared `ask_human` tool. Fixing = add a `HumanCapability` concretion to the Node provider (CLI prompt / relay human-requests queue) and add `human` to `NODE_SURFACE_CAPS`, unblocking on-prem human-in-the-loop parity with cloud.

- **Newly added catalog model ids (openrouter free + paid + Cloudflare `@cf/...`) are unverified.** This pass added ~15 new entries to [api/src/application/llm/vendors/openrouter.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/openrouter.ts) (`openrouter/owl-alpha`, `deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash:free`, `arcee-ai/trinity-large-thinking:free`, `openai/gpt-oss-20b:free`, `meta-llama/llama-3-8b-instruct`, `google/gemma-3-4b-it`, `microsoft/phi-4`, `qwen/qwen3.5-9b`, `z-ai/glm-4-32b`, `openai/gpt-5-nano`, `openai/o4-mini`, `alibaba/qwen3.5-397b-a17b`) and one entry to [api/src/application/llm/vendors/cloudflare.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/cloudflare.ts) (`@cf/meta/llama-3-8b-instruct`). Operator gave the ids by hand without an `/v1/models` cross-check; wrong ids will surface as `404` from the upstream and the cascade will skip them (vendor cooldown drops them after 3 misses in 60s). Same drift risk as the existing NVIDIA NIM entry below. Fixing (curl `https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models` with the OpenRouter key and `https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/<id>/ai/models/search` with the Cloudflare token, reconcile each vendor's catalog against live ids ŌĆö remove or correct any 404'ing entries) unblocks: clean cascade ordering with no wasted attempts on phantom models.

- **NVIDIA NIM catalog model ids are wrong in production ŌĆö 404s observed live.** Re-confirms the existing entry below: in the 2026-05-23 `llm-b9a3db1b-...` trace, both `mistralai/mistral-large-3-675b-instruct-2512` (returned `408` after our timeout) and `nvidia/mistral-nemotron` (`404`) appeared in the cascade for a caller-pinned `anthropic/claude-3-haiku` request ŌĆö burning two attempts on doomed model ids. Compounds the "paid failover" bug closed in this pass because NVIDIA is the only non-OpenRouter vendor in the paid pool, so when the cascade falls through, it lands on the broken ids. Fixing (curl `https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1/models` with the API key, reconcile against [api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts) ŌĆö verified-id allowlist only, drop the inferred org-prefix entries) unblocks: paid cascade tail actually reaches working models when OpenRouter is saturated.

- **The standardized cloud coding default `minimaxai/minimax-m2.7` is operator-supplied and unverified against the live NIM catalog.** `CODING_DEFAULT_MODEL` resolves to `minimaxai/minimax-m2.7` ([api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts) ŌåÆ lead of `CODING_MODEL_POOL` in [LlmProxyService.ts](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts)) because M2.7 is FREE on NVIDIA NIM but PAID on OpenRouter. Reachability is **confirmed** ŌĆö `NVIDIA_API_KEY` is bound on the api worker (`wrangler secret list`, 2026-06-12), so the NIM default dispatches rather than no-key-skipping; `minimax/minimax-m2.5:free` (OpenRouter) sits immediately after as failover. **Still open:** the exact id strings for the NIM coding entries added by hand ŌĆö `minimaxai/minimax-m2.7` (the default) and `z-ai/glm-5.1` (a free coding-pool member) ŌĆö are not cross-checked against live `https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1/models` (the key value isn't retrievable via `wrangler secret list` and there's no local NVIDIA key to curl with) ŌĆö same drift risk as the NVIDIA NIM entry above; a wrong slug 404s and the cascade skips it (the default silently degrades to M2.5). Fixing (curl the NIM models endpoint with the bound key and confirm/correct each slug ŌĆö vendors may ship these under a different org prefix or version) unblocks: M2.7/GLM-5.1 actually serving instead of the cascade burning a doomed attempt.

- **Gateway-side strict-mode validation only fires when consumers send `response_format: { type: 'json_schema', strict: true }`.** Today consumers like hired.video do their own client-side Zod validation after the fact and never set `response_format` on the outbound request, so the gateway can't help them retry the chain on schema mismatches ŌĆö even though [jsonSchemaValidator.ts](api/src/application/llm/jsonSchemaValidator.ts) now supports it fully. Fixing (consumer-side migration: send `response_format: { type: 'json_schema', json_schema: { strict: true, schema } }` instead of post-call Zod) unblocks: cross-vendor retry on strict-schema failures, deletion of tenant-side retry loops, less wasted budget burning models that can't conform.

- **Epic decomposition foundation shipped; the agent reasoning step + board tree UI + fan-out routing are the residuals.** This pass built the task *type/hierarchy* data-model + API: migration [0112](api/migrations/0112_task_type_and_parent.sql) adds `task_type` (`task`|`epic` enum) + a nullable self-FK `parent_task_id` (ON DELETE SET NULL ŌåÆ deleting an Epic orphans, not cascade-deletes, its children) to [tasks](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts), with a matching `TaskType` enum + `taskType`/`parentTaskId`/`isEpic`/`isAssignedToAgent` on the [Task entity](api/src/domain/task/Task.ts) and a `reclassifyAsEpic()` behaviour (flips type + sheds the agent assignee, since an Epic is a planning container). [TaskService](api/src/application/task/TaskService.ts) now has an **on-assign hook** (`onAssignedToAgent`, fired from create *and* update whenever a plain task newly transitions into AGENT ownership) that runs an injectable [EpicDecomposer](api/src/application/task/EpicDecomposer.ts) and, when the verdict is "Epic", calls the public `decomposeEpic` server action to reclassifyŌåÆfan-out child tasks (each `parent_task_id`-linked, sequentially re-keyed, fanned out to the planned human/agent assignee). [TaskRepository](api/src/infrastructure/repositories/TaskRepository.ts) persists both columns + has `findChildren`; the board read path surfaces the tree via `taskType`/`parentTaskId` on every `GET /api/tasks` row plus new `GET /api/tasks/:id/tree` and `POST /api/tasks/:id/decompose` ([taskRoutes](api/src/presentation/routes/taskRoutes.ts)). Fan-out + reclassify is unit-tested ([epicDecomposition.test.ts](api/src/application/task/epicDecomposition.test.ts), 9 cases). **Residuals (deliberately scoped out):** (1) the `EpicDecomposer` is a **deterministic checklist-parsing heuristic** (`heuristicEpicDecomposer` ŌĆö markdown `- [ ]`/`-`/`1.` lines ŌåÆ children), a clearly-marked stand-in for the real BA-agent reasoning step; swap an LLM-backed `assess()` (e.g. an `ideProxy(env)` structured completion returning the same `DecompositionPlan` shape) in via the already-wired constructor injection. (2) **No board UI** renders the parent/child tree yet ŌĆö [TaskMgmtContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) still draws a flat status grid; children appear as standalone cards (data is there via the new fields, the nesting/expand UI is not). (3) Fan-out **assignee routing is pass-through** ŌĆö `decomposeEpic` writes whatever assignee the plan specifies but does NOT resolve a *role* ("give the QA subtask to the QA agent") nor dispatch the children through [SwimlaneCoordinator](api/src/application/swimlane/SwimlaneCoordinator.ts); newly-created children just land in the backlog. Fixing all three unblocks: agents acting as real planners/BAs end-to-end. Builds on the human+agent assignee foundation.

- **Routing pools are hand-maintained from a hardcoded vendor catalog that drifts from the live OpenRouter `/models` API.** The FREE/PRO/CODING pools derive from static `VendorModule.catalog` arrays ([vendors/*.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/)), edited by hand. This pass caught real drift by calling the live API: invented ids (`qwen/qwen3-coder-480b-a35b-instruct` as an OpenRouter id, a `deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash:free` that doesn't exist), AND missing current best coders (`qwen/qwen3.7-plus`, `xiaomi/mimo-v2.5` = Programming #1, `nex-agi/nex-n2-pro:free`, `nvidia/nemotron-3-ultra-550b-a55b:free`) ŌĆö now added/corrected. But the gateway ALREADY fetches the live catalog via [getCatalogCached](api/src/application/llm/modelCatalog.ts) for `/v1/catalog` (display only); routing ignores it. Fixing (derive the coding/free/paid pools ŌĆö or at least validate them ŌĆö from the cached live `/models` payload, filtering by `supported_parameters: tools` + a coding/programming tag, so a stale hardcoded id can never silently route to a 404 backstop again) unblocks: model selection that tracks OpenRouter's fast-moving free tier automatically instead of by manual catalog edits. Discovered when a cloud run fell to `gemini-2.5-flash-lite` because the hardcoded free coders were saturated/stale.

- **Drag-to-lane autonomous trigger uses the simple runtime executor, not the SwimlaneCoordinator ŌĆö so multi-agent stages / success policies / lane actions don't fire.** Fixed this pass: dropping a ticket into a lane now passes the lane's configured cloud agent (`decideLaneAutoRun`, gated by the lane's `auto`/`human` gate ŌĆö NOT the legacy `boards.autonomous` flag, which is always false ŌåÆ would have blocked every run) ŌåÆ `submitExecution` payload `cloudAgentRef`+`model`, so a "Coder Agent (V2)" lane actually runs AS that agent instead of the V1 gateway-default. BUT the path still goes `patchStatus ŌåÆ runtimeApi.submitExecution` (single cloud run), bypassing [SwimlaneCoordinator](api/src/application/swimlane/SwimlaneCoordinator.ts): only the FIRST cloud lane agent runs; a lane's `executionMode: 'parallel'` multi-agent fan-out, `successPolicy`/`successThreshold`, and `actionType` (advance/move_ticket/run_workflow) are ignored on a manual drag. Fixing (route lane-entry through the board coordinator's ticket-run start when the lane has >1 agent or a non-advance action) unblocks: full board automation semantics on drag, not just single-agent autorun. Discovered tracing why a dragged ticket ran as "BuilderForce Cloud (default)".

- **Lane agents with `runtime` host/local/remote aren't dispatched by the drag trigger ŌĆö only `runtime: 'cloud'`.** [decideLaneAutoRun](frontend/src/lib/laneAutoRun.ts) picks the first cloud agent; a lane configured only with a self-hosted/remote agent falls back to the legacy status auto-run (no agent pinned), so that host-run agent never executes on drag. Fixing (resolve a host/remote lane agent to an `agentHostId` or coordinator dispatch) unblocks: self-hosted lane agents triggering on drag, parity with cloud lane agents.

- **IDE file storage diverges between the worker and api backends (different buckets AND key layouts).** The frontend routes file reads/writes to the worker (`builderforce-storage`, key `{projectId}/ŌĆ”`, [worker/src/routes/files.ts](worker/src/routes/files.ts)) when `NEXT_PUBLIC_WORKER_URL` is set, else to the api (`builderforce-uploads`, key `ide/projects/{projectId}/ŌĆ”`, [ideRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts)). The two never share data. Server-side template seeding ([projectTemplate.ts](api/src/application/project/projectTemplate.ts)) writes only to the api bucket, so when the worker is the active backend a freshly-created project's seeded scaffold never appears (Run silently falls back to its in-memory defaults). The new repo-import sidesteps this by persisting through the same `saveFile` path the IDE reads from, but the underlying split remains a latent correctness hazard for any server-side write to project files. Fixing (one bucket + one key layout, or have the worker proxy the api's storage) unblocks: server-side seeding/writes that the IDE actually sees regardless of backend.

- **Cloud PRD generation + V1 workflow executor still dispatch on the fixed FREE pool.** Closing the cloud-coding-agent plan-routing gap routed the durable/container *tool loops* through `llmProxyForPlan(env, effectivePlan, premiumOverride)`, but the one-shot PRD generator ([taskPrd.ts](api/src/application/prd/taskPrd.ts) `ideProxy(env)`) and the V1 workflow executor ([workflow/cloudExecutor.ts](api/src/application/workflow/cloudExecutor.ts) `ideProxy(env)`) still use the free pool. Low impact (PRD gen is a cheap structured-doc completion free models handle fine; V1 workflows are the legacy engine), so deliberately left on free. Fixing (thread the run's `effectivePlan`/`premiumOverride` ŌĆö already resolved once per run ŌĆö into these two callers via `llmProxyForPlan`) unblocks: a Pro tenant's PRD/V1-workflow steps also running on premium models, fully consistent with the coding loop.

- **The core app component classes (`.btn` family, `.input`, `.label`, `.page-header`, `.card-header`, `.card-title`, `.modal-title`, base `.badge`, base `.empty-state`) were referenced in 145+ call-sites across 26 files but were never defined in any loaded stylesheet ŌĆö now fixed, so spot-check the wider app.** Tailwind ships `@tailwind components` with an empty `plugins: []` ([frontend/tailwind.config.js](frontend/tailwind.config.js)) and the only stylesheet ([frontend/src/app/globals.css](frontend/src/app/globals.css)) defined only the *variant* leaves (`.page-title`, `.card`, `.badge-green`, `.empty-state-title`, ŌĆ”) ŌĆö so every page using bare `.btn`/`.input`/`.page-header` fell back to native chrome or stacked layout, which is why only `/prompts` (self-contained inline styles) looked finished. This pass added the missing base classes to globals.css matched to the `/prompts` aesthetic. **Deferred:** the fix lights up chrome on many pages beyond the four normalized here (admin, marketplace, models, settings, workforce sub-views, ArtifactAssigner, ŌĆ”) that were silently relying on the same undefined classes; they should be visually spot-checked for any page that had hand-tuned around the missing styles. Fixing (a quick visual sweep of `.btn`/`.input`/`.empty-state` consumers) unblocks: confidence the design-system completion didn't regress a page that compensated for the gap.

- **Marketplace pages aren't fully converged: Prompts keeps a local `card` style const and a different create-UX pattern from Skills/Personas/Content.** This pass unified headers, tab bars, search/filter placement, badges, and buttons across `/content-manager`, `/skills`, `/personas`, `/prompts` onto the shared classes, but two residuals remain: (1) [prompts/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/prompts/page.tsx) still renders cards + detail-drawer surfaces via a local `card` CSSProperties const (padding 16 / `--bg-base`) instead of the shared `.card` class (padding 20 / `--card`), so prompt cards sit slightly tighter on a different surface token; (2) Prompts uses an inline expanding `CreatePromptForm` while the other three use a centered `.modal-overlay` create dialog. Both deferred to avoid restyling the prompts grid/detail and to keep a product decision (inline vs modal create) explicit. Fixing unblocks: pixel-identical card chrome and one canonical create pattern across all four library pages.

- **Brain "capture execution" trace is in-memory per session ŌĆö it doesn't persist across reload.** This pass added a Brain-side triage capture (the `Ō¦ē` button beside `+ New` in both BrainPanel headers): [useBrainConversation.ts](brain-embedded/src/useBrainConversation.ts) records a per-chat `BrainTraceEvent[]` (LLM steps, full tool chain with args/results/timing, intermediate assistant messages, and errors ŌĆö thrown tool errors are now fed back as `{ok:false}` AND traced) and `buildTriageReport()` ([brainTriage.ts](brain-embedded/src/brainTriage.ts)) assembles the same errors-first ŌåÆ trace ŌåÆ logs ŌåÆ transcript report the host/cloud Logs view emits. **Residual (deliberate, mirrors `transcriptRef`):** the trace lives only in a `useRef` Map for the session, so a page reload (or capturing a chat from a prior session) yields only the steps that ran since mount ŌĆö the persisted chat tables have no tool columns. Fixing (persist trace events to a `brain_chat_trace` table written alongside the final-assistant message, and rehydrate on chat load) unblocks: capturing a complete report for any historical Brain run, not just the live session.

- **A cloud coding run that floors onto a non-coder backstop now SAYS so on the timeline, but is not aborted/escalated ŌĆö and the rationale event is durable-loop-only.** This pass made model selection legible in the execution triage (the #1 unanswered question on exec #59: dispatched `gateway-default`, silently floored onto the `gemini-2.5-flash-lite` backstop, spun 7 steps, shipped nothing): `runCloudToolLoop` now emits a run-start `model.select` event (requested model, strict-pin vs soft-seed, the seed + whether it's a curated coder, the plan's reachable coders) and the existing `coding_model_degraded` event ([cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts) `emitModelSelection`/`emitCodingModelDegraded`) now spells out cause (curated coders unreachable: vendor key unbound / cooled down / outage) AND consequence (backstop generalist loops on search, finishes with no edits). **Residuals (deliberately scoped out):** (1) **Observability only ŌĆö no policy change.** A degraded run still proceeds and burns its full step budget producing nothing; it is flagged, not stopped. A Coder Agent that resolves to a non-coder backstop arguably should hard-fail fast (or retry on a different reachable coder) rather than spin ŌĆö needs a product decision on abort-vs-warn. (2) The `model.select` rationale fires from the durable loop only; the long-lived **Container** executor ([handleContainerOp](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)) picks per-op with no run-start hook, so a container-surface run gets the `coding_model_degraded` *outcome* event but not the up-front selection rationale. (3) The dispatch event ([runtimeRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) still logs the opaque `gateway-default` label ŌĆö now superseded by `model.select` but left in place. Fixing all three unblocks: degraded coding runs that fail fast instead of wasting budget, and uniform selection telemetry across both cloud executors. Builds directly on entry [1247] (stale/saturated hardcoded coders ŌåÆ fell to gemini-2.5-flash-lite).

- **Subdomain hosting ships static-only and behind the path form ŌĆö the wildcard DNS/route + container web-serving are unprovisioned.** This pass added DesignerŌåÆsubdomain publishing: migration [0121](api/migrations/0121_project_sites.sql) (`project_sites`), an in-browser build-capture (`handlePublishBuild` mountsŌåÆ`npm run build`ŌåÆ`readDirRecursive('dist')` in [IDENew.tsx](frontend/src/components/IDENew.tsx) via [useWebContainer](frontend/src/hooks/useWebContainer.ts)), a multipart publish endpoint + cached subdomainŌåÆsite lookup ([ideRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts) `POST /projects/:id/publish`, [siteHosting.ts](api/src/application/ide/siteHosting.ts)), a public R2 server ([sitesRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/sitesRoutes.ts)), and the [SitePublishPanel](frontend/src/components/SitePublishPanel.tsx). **Residuals (deliberately scoped out):** (1) **Wildcard hosting is wired but needs the DNS record + a deploy.** The Worker route `*.apps.builderforce.ai/*` is now in [api/wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml) and a Host-serving middleware in [index.ts](api/src/index.ts) (`tryServeHostedSite`) serves any path on a hosting subdomain from R2; `AUTH_CACHE_KV` is already bound. **Still required:** (a) a proxied wildcard DNS record `*.apps ŌåÆ AAAA 100:: (proxied)` ŌĆö the local wrangler token has only `zone:read`, not `dns_records:edit`, so create it via the dashboard or a DNS-scoped token (`curl -X POST https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/zones/<ZONE_ID>/dns_records -H "Authorization: Bearer <DNS_EDIT_TOKEN>" -H 'Content-Type: application/json' --data '{"type":"AAAA","name":"*.apps","content":"100::","proxied":true}'`); (b) `wrangler deploy` (currently blocked locally only because the `[[containers]]` image build needs Docker running). **UPDATE 2026-06-22 (diag of `rumbledating.apps.builderforce.ai` not loading):** (a) and (b) are DONE ŌĆö the wildcard `*.apps` DNS record now resolves to the Cloudflare edge and the path form serves through the deployed worker (`GET /api/sites/rumbledating/` ŌåÆ 200). The remaining blocker was **TLS**: a host-based request to `<sub>.apps.builderforce.ai` failed the handshake (`SEC_E_ILLEGAL_MESSAGE`, curl http_code 000) because Cloudflare **Universal SSL covers only the apex + the single-label wildcard `*.builderforce.ai`, NOT the second-level wildcard `*.apps.builderforce.ai`**. **RESOLVED 2026-06-22 (operator decision: no paid ACM):** moved hosting from `*.apps.builderforce.ai` to the single-label apex **`<sub>.builderforce.ai`**, which the FREE Universal SSL `*.builderforce.ai` cert already covers ŌĆö zero TLS cost. Code: `HOSTING_APEX='builderforce.ai'` + reserved-label hardening in [siteHosting.ts](api/src/application/ide/siteHosting.ts) (`subdomainFromHost` now returns null for `RESERVED_SUBDOMAINS` so the shared apex doesn't 404 `api`/`www`/etc.), worker route `*.builderforce.ai/*` in [wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml), comments synced across index.ts/sitesRoutes.ts/schema.ts/frontend, unit test [siteHosting.test.ts](api/src/application/ide/siteHosting.test.ts). **Operator action still required to go live:** (i) add a proxied wildcard DNS record `* ŌåÆ AAAA 100:: (proxied)` on the zone (specific api/www records take precedence); (ii) `wrangler deploy`; (iii) existing sites (e.g. rumbledating) must **Re-publish** to rebuild with the relative asset base. **Greedy-route caution:** `*.builderforce.ai/*` is broad ŌĆö any platform subdomain that should serve elsewhere MUST keep a more-specific route/binding OR be in `RESERVED_SUBDOMAINS`; an unlisted, unrouted platform subdomain would now hit this worker and 404. Until deploy, sites remain reachable via the path form `/api/sites/<sub>/...` (wired + working, surfaced as "preview" in the panel). (2) **Container mode is schema-only** ŌĆö `project_sites.mode='container'` exists but the V2 Cloudflare Container serves no HTTP; long-lived web-serving (SSR/APIs) is a later phase. (3) **Build-default parity** ŌĆö `handlePublishBuild` only injects a default `package.json`; unlike `handleRun` it doesn't backfill index.html/main.jsx/index.css/vite.config, so a project missing those (and never Run) can fail the build. (4) **Orphaned R2 on project delete** ŌĆö `project_sites` cascades on `projects` delete (FK) but the `sites/<sub>/...` R2 objects are not swept, leaking storage; add an on-delete R2 prefix purge. (5) **Asset-base fix (2026-06-22) ŌĆö relative-base build, with two follow-ons.** `handlePublishBuild` now builds with `npm run build -- --base=./` ([IDENew.tsx](frontend/src/components/IDENew.tsx)) so Vite emits relative asset URLs that resolve under BOTH the host form (`<sub>.apps.builderforce.ai/`) and the path form (`/api/sites/<sub>/`). Was the cause of the path-form preview loading blank with `/assets/*.js|.css` 404s (root-absolute URLs miss the `/api/sites/<sub>/` prefix). Follow-ons: (a) **already-published sites must Re-publish** to pick up the relative build ŌĆö old R2 artifacts still carry absolute URLs; (b) **deep multi-segment SPA routes still break with relative base** ŌĆö on reload of `/foo/bar`, `./assets` resolves against `/foo/` not the root; an SSR-less SPA served from a path prefix can't have it both ways without a serve-time `<base href>` inject keyed to the serving prefix (host vs path differ), so left as a known static-SPA limitation; (c) **`--base=./` assumes a Vite build** ŌĆö it's appended to `npm run build`, so a non-Vite or multi-command build script ending in a non-Vite tool would mis-receive the flag (Designer scaffold defaults to `vite build`, so the common case is covered). Fixing all unblocks: real `<sub>.apps.builderforce.ai` hosting (static now, container later) with assets that load under either addressing mode and no orphaned assets.

- **Vision image input ships inline-data-URL-first; the signed-URL fallback needs `JWT_SECRET` and the gateway picks the vision model by shape, not a hard pin.** This pass wired uploaded/pasted/dropped images into OpenAI `image_url` content parts so the model actually sees them (was previously flattened to a markdown link): [ChatInput.tsx](frontend/src/components/ChatInput.tsx) paste/drop ŌåÆ [useBrainConversation](brain-embedded/src/useBrainConversation.ts) builds `ContentPart[]` from a downscaled data URL ([imagePrep.ts](brain-embedded/src/imagePrep.ts)), falling back to a signed public URL ([brainFilesRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/brainFilesRoutes.ts) + [uploadSign.ts](api/src/infrastructure/auth/uploadSign.ts)) for oversize images. The gateway already routes `image_url` requests to a vision model via `reorderPoolByShape`. **Residuals:** (1) the signed-URL path no-ops to the text link when `JWT_SECRET` is unbound (graceful, but silent); (2) downscaling targets ~1568px/3.5MB so it covers ~all real images, but a pathological one still degrades to text; (3) the Brain sends no explicit vision-model hint ŌĆö it relies on the gateway's shape reorder + cross-vendor recovery, so a non-vision caller-pinned model would burn one attempt before failover. Fixing unblocks: guaranteed vision routing + a louder signal when signing is unconfigured.

- **Cloud human-in-the-loop SHIPPED for the durable/Worker surfaces ŌĆö residuals are the container surface, the chip-resume glyph, and unanswered-question lifecycle.** A blocked cloud agent can now ask instead of failing silently: new `ask_human` tool ([cloudAgentTools.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentTools.ts)) ŌåÆ records a `question` approval scoped to the run (`execution_id`/`cloud_agent_ref`, migration 0120) into the SAME human-requests queue + `HumanRequestsView` self-hosted agents use, fans out Slack+email via the shared [approvalNotifier.ts](api/src/application/approval/approvalNotifier.ts) (extracted from the approval route, now used by both), parks the run in the new `paused` execution state (amber "needs attention" chip on the board), and resumes when a human answers: `PATCH /api/approvals/:id` ŌåÆ [executionResume.ts](api/src/application/runtime/executionResume.ts) delivers the answer as a steer and wakes the durable runner via a new `CloudRunnerDO` `/resume` (the loop drains the answer on its next tick). **Residuals (deliberately scoped out):** (1) **Container surface** ([handleContainerOp](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)) is NOT wired ŌĆö it picks per-op with no run-start/pause hook, so `ask_human` is intentionally absent from `CONTAINER_AGENT_TOOLS` (asserted in [cloudAgentHumanInLoop.test.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentHumanInLoop.test.ts)); since the container falls back to the DO today this is latent, but a true long-lived container needs its own pause/resume op. (2) The board/chip **`resume` play-glyph re-runs a fresh execution** rather than calling a dedicated resume-execution endpoint ŌĆö true resume is the answer path; the glyph is a secondary nudge. (3) The **Output "Send" box on a `paused` run** doesn't resume (it follows the terminal/steer branch); the canonical answer channel is the human-requests queue. (4) **No timeout/auto-fail for an unanswered cloud question** ŌĆö a `paused` run waits indefinitely (intended for HITL, but a cancel-while-paused leaves the DO cursor + a `pending` approval dangling, since cloud questions set no `expiresAt`). (5) **Task isn't routed to a `needs_attention` lane on pause** ŌĆö only the amber chip signals it; wiring `paused`ŌåÆlane move would close the exec #69 ask fully. Fixing these unblocks: HITL parity across all cloud surfaces + a self-cleaning paused-run lifecycle. Builds on the model-selection observability entry above (same "silent no-output run" failure class, exec #59/#69).

- **NVIDIA NIM catalog model ids are partially unverified.** [api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/nvidia.ts) registers 11 free models against `https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1/chat/completions`.
