- **Cloud Done-finalize doesn't emit a `pr_opened` tool-audit event, and the no-existing-PR guard is a read-time check (narrow double-PR race).** This pass closed the host/cloud finalize-parity gap: [dispatchTaskFinalize](api/src/presentation/routes/taskRoutes.ts) now opens a PR server-side via [openTaskPullRequest](api/src/application/repos/openTaskPullRequest.ts) when a *cloud*-assigned task hits Done with a pushed `gitBranch` and no `githubPrUrl` yet. Two residuals: (1) unlike the inline run-end finalize in [runCloudToolLoop](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) (which calls `recordCloudToolEvent` with a `pr_opened`/`merge_to_main` event), the Done-transition path records only the `pull_requests` row + task `githubPrUrl` ŌĆö so the Observability timeline shows no `pr_opened` event for a manually-completed cloud ticket. (2) The `!githubPrUrl` guard reads task state at Done-time; if an execution's inline finalize is opening a PR at the same instant a human drags the card to Done, both can fire before either writes `githubPrUrl` ŌåÆ a duplicate PR. Both are narrow (the common path is execution-opens-PR-then-auto-Done). **Investigated 2026-06-13 ŌĆö needs two prerequisites, not a drop-in:** (1) the uniform-emit can't just call [recordCloudToolEvent](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts) from `openTaskPullRequest` because that helper requires a non-optional `executionId` and writes an *execution-scoped* row (`sessionKey: exec:<id>`); the Done-finalize path is *task-scoped* with no execution, so a uniform `pr_opened` needs a task-scoped audit channel (nullable `executionId` + `sessionKey: task:<id>`) AND a check that the Observability timeline read path renders execution-less events (else the event is written but invisible). (2) The race-free guard needs an atomic claim *before* the external PR-create call (the URL isn't known until after, so a conditional update on `githubPrUrl` can't claim pre-creation) ŌĆö i.e. a new nullable `tasks.pr_opening_at` claim column set via `UPDATE ŌĆ” WHERE id=? AND pr_opening_at IS NULL AND github_pr_url IS NULL` (a migration, hence live-DB-apply gated), rolled back on PR-create failure. Fixing both unblocks: uniform cloud PR observability + race-free single-PR finalize.

- **Changes-tab Monaco diff viewer reads only the cloud ticket branch `builderforce/task-<id>`; on-prem custom-branch runs show "No content found."** This pass added a [FileChangeViewer](frontend/src/components/agent/FileChangeViewer.tsx) that fetches a changed file's current+base contents via the new `GET /api/runtime/tasks/:taskId/file-content` route ([runtimeRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) and renders the diff in Monaco (the same editor the IDE uses). The route resolves the branch via [resolveTicketRepoContext](api/src/application/repos/commitFileAsPendingChange.ts), which hardcodes `builderforce/task-<taskId>` ŌĆö correct for cloud V2 runs (same resolver the cloud `commitAgentFile`/`write_file` path commits through), but on-prem runs and any task with an explicit [tasks.branchName](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) (migration 0091; [prDispatch.buildBranchName](api/src/application/repos/prDispatch.ts) emits `task/<slug>` or the explicit name) commit to a *different* branch, so the viewer reads the wrong ref and degrades to "No content found." Fixing (thread `tasks.branchName` into `resolveTicketRepoContext` and have both the read path and `commitAgentFile` honor it, so cloud + on-prem + custom-branch all converge on one branch source of truth) unblocks: the diff viewer working for every execution path, not just default-branch cloud runs. Same hardcoded-branch root cause as the cloud commit path, so fix them together.

- **Workforce Teams drive assignee scoping; lane-agent picker scoping is the remaining edge.** Teams shipped end-to-end: migration [0114](api/migrations/0114_workforce_teams.sql) (`teams` + polymorphic `team_members` [`human`|`cloud_agent`|`host_agent`, mirroring the task-assignee identity] + `team_projects` M:N), [teamRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/teamRoutes.ts) CRUD/members/projects + cached `GET /by-project/:projectId` and `GET /by-project/:projectId/workforce` (MANAGER+), [lib/teams.ts](frontend/src/lib/teams.ts), the [TeamsView](frontend/src/components/teams/TeamsView.tsx) Workforce tab, and the Teams tab in the [Board-config panel](frontend/src/components/board/BoardConfigPanel.tsx) (assigns teams to a board's project). **Now wired into assignee resolution:** the manual task assignee picker ([TaskMgmtContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) ŌĆö create dialog + drawer) filters its human/cloud-agent/host options to the project's assigned-team members when any team is assigned (falls back to the full tenant roster otherwise); the auto-assign recommender ([assigneeRecommender.ts](api/src/application/metrics/assigneeRecommender.ts) `loadProjectTeamMembers`, shared with the picker endpoint) already scopes the same way. **Residuals:** (1) the **board lane-agent picker** ([BoardConfigPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/board/BoardConfigPanel.tsx) `AgentList` ŌåÆ `loadAgentPool`) is NOT team-scoped ŌĆö it uses the tenant-wide pool whose identity space (`workforce`/`registered` agents from `/api/agents`) doesn't line up 1:1 with `team_members` (`cloud_agent`=ide_agents.id / `host_agent`=agent_hosts.id), so a clean filter needs the pool reconciled to the team-member id spaces first; `SwimlaneCoordinator` dispatch stays correctly agnostic (it runs the explicitly-configured lane agent). (2) The **all-projects board view** (`TaskMgmtContent` with no `projectId`) can't scope the per-task picker to each task's own project ŌĆö it stays tenant-wide there; only the single-project board scopes. (3) `team_members.member_name` is denormalized and only refreshed on (re-)add, so renaming a user/agent/host drifts the team's stored label until re-added (the picker dodges this by filtering live lists, but the TeamsView roster still shows the stale name). (4) The member picker's agent pool is owned cloud agents (`/api/workforce/agents/mine`) + remote hosts only; marketplace-*hired* agents (`/agents/purchased`) are not offered.

- **"V2 Cloud Agent (Node/Container)" real Cloudflare Container is BUILT ŌĆö needs deploy + Containers-enabled account, and has two known bounds.** The `container` surface now runs on a real long-lived Cloudflare Container ([AgentContainerDO](api/src/infrastructure/relay/AgentContainerDO.ts) via the `[[containers]]` block in [wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml), image [api/container/](api/container/server.mjs)). The container clones the repo to disk, runs the agent loop in one persistent process with a REAL shell (`run_command` for build/type-check/lint/test), and delegates every LLM step / commit / PR finalize back to the Worker's `/internal/container-op` endpoint (authenticated by a per-run HMAC token, [containerRunToken.ts](api/src/application/runtime/containerRunToken.ts)) so metering/commit/finalize stay single-impl (the finalize block was extracted to the shared `finalizeCloudRun`). Dispatch routes `container`-surface V2 runs to it and degrades to the durable DO only when the binding is absent or the container can't start. **Remaining:** (1) **deploy** ŌĆö needs a Workers Paid plan with Containers enabled and a `wrangler deploy` that builds `api/container/Dockerfile`; not yet built/pushed from this environment (no Docker/CF here), so end-to-end is unverified. (2) **inactivity bound** ŌĆö `sleepAfter` is 20m and the loop's outbound calls don't renew the Container activity timer, so a single run that exceeds ~20m of wall-clock could be stopped mid-flight; raise `sleepAfter` or add a keep-alive ping for very-long tasks. (3) **clone token in run spec** ŌĆö the Worker passes a tokened `x-access-token` git URL to the container so its shell can clone; it's short-lived and internal, but is a wider exposure than the DO loop (which commits via the GitHub API and never hands out a token) ŌĆö consider a scoped git-proxy for the container instead. (4) **non-GitHub providers** ŌĆö the tokened clone URL is built only for `provider.startsWith('github')`; GitLab/others run reasoning+commit-only (no local clone, so `run_command` returns "no repo"). Also: the agent picker ([RunAgentControl.tsx](frontend/src/components/task/RunAgentControl.tsx)) doesn't label which of the three cloud types (V1 / V2-Durable / V2-Container) an agent is, so users can't tell the surface at selection time (user opted to defer the picker chip).

- **V2 cloud agents run fully in the cloud (all Cloudflare); the `durable` (CloudRunnerDO) executor is built ŌĆö needs deploy verification.** A V2 cloud agent picks a `runtime_surface` at creation (migration 0105 on `ide_agents`; selector in [CloudAgentFormFields](frontend/src/components/workforce/CloudAgentFormFields.tsx); resolved in `resolveCloudAgent`; routed via [cloudDispatch.resolveCloudSurface](api/src/application/runtime/cloudDispatch.ts)). Both surfaces execute **in the cloud, on Cloudflare** (no local/hybrid/Fly.io): **`durable`** = [CloudRunnerDO](api/src/infrastructure/relay/CloudRunnerDO.ts), a Durable Object running the cloud agent loop ONE LLM step per `alarm()` tick with conversation state persisted in DO storage ŌĆö fresh CPU/subrequest budget per tick, so it survives the ~30s `waitUntil` wall and runs to completion (mirrors [AnalysisRunnerDO](api/src/infrastructure/relay/AnalysisRunnerDO.ts)). Built this pass: `CLOUD_RUNNER` binding (env.ts + wrangler.toml) + `new_sqlite_classes=["CloudRunnerDO"]` migration (tag v5) + export in index.ts; `dispatchAndQueue` kicks off the DO (interim `runCloudExecution` Worker loop is the fallback when the binding is absent); `runCloudToolLoop` parameterized for per-tick resume (Worker path behavior preserved by defaults); orphan ceiling is now a **heartbeat** ŌĆö cloud runs measured from `updated_at` (bumped each tick) in both [RuntimeService.isOrphaned](api/src/application/runtime/RuntimeService.ts) and the [reaper](api/src/application/runtime/staleExecutionReaper.ts). **`container`** = a long-lived **Cloudflare Container** runtime (for very long/continuous tasks) ŌĆö dispatched to an online runtime via the relay, and **gracefully falls back to the durable DO** (recorded as a `runtime.fallback` event) when none is online, so it never dies. The Fly.io `agent-runtime/fly.toml` was an unused orphan (wired into no CI/deploy) and was deleted ŌĆö the stack is Cloudflare-only. REMAINING: cannot verify DO/alarm behavior locally ŌĆö verify on deploy that a durable V2 run ticks to completion + PR/merge; the actual **Cloudflare Container** executor for the `container` surface is a future build (today it falls back to the DO); CloudRunnerDO notifications are skipped (UI polls) so live streaming is poll-only for durable runs.

- **Workforce member metrics + DORA + planner consumption + Calendar sync shipped end-to-end (backend + frontend, migrations live on Neon); only operator-config remains.** The metrics keystone: member capability/availability **profiles** (migration [0116](api/migrations/0116_member_profiles.sql) `member_profiles`), an append-only **task_status_transitions** log + `tasks.completed_at`/`last_worked_at`/`redo_count`/`reopen_count` (migration [0117](api/migrations/0117_task_status_transitions.sql)), and **member_metrics_period + deployment_events** (migration [0118](api/migrations/0118_member_metrics_dora.sql)) feeding [workforceMetrics.ts](api/src/application/metrics/workforceMetrics.ts) behind `GET/PUT /api/members/*` ([memberRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/memberRoutes.ts)). Transition recording fires from the agent-execution path ([RuntimeService](api/src/application/runtime/RuntimeService.ts) `onTaskStatusSync` ŌåÆ [syncExecutionTaskLifecycle](api/src/application/task/taskLifecycle.ts)) + the dequeue claim + the human PATCH, and a terminal run stamps the true work-stopped signal `tasks.last_worked_at`; **DORA deployment_events auto-produced** at the merge chokepoint ([recordPullRequestRow.ts](api/src/application/repos/recordPullRequestRow.ts) ŌĆö every PR merge writes a `success` deploy; post-merge CI `failure` flips `is_failure`, a later `success` stamps `restored_at` for MTTR); **planner consumption** is live via [assigneeRecommender.ts](api/src/application/metrics/assigneeRecommender.ts) (ranks by availability + spare WIP + skill match + ramp) behind `GET /api/members/recommend`, injected into the Epic fan-out; **frontend** ships the Performance tab ([WorkforceMetricsContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/workforce/WorkforceMetricsContent.tsx)) + capability/availability editor ([MemberProfileEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/workforce/MemberProfileEditor.tsx)). **Google Calendar sync built** (migration [0122](api/migrations/0122_google_calendar_provider.sql) adds the `google_calendar` provider; [googleCalendarSync.ts](api/src/application/integrations/googleCalendarSync.ts) overlays busyŌåÆavailability + eventsŌåÆPTO onto profiles via the existing integration-credentials framework; `POST /api/members/:kind/:ref/calendar-sync` + a "Sync from Google Calendar" button; AES-GCM credential crypto extracted to the shared [credentialCrypto.ts](api/src/application/integrations/credentialCrypto.ts)). **Migrations 0116ŌĆō0118 + 0122 applied to the live Neon DB and verified idempotent.** **Operator-config remaining (not code gaps):** (1) to *use* Calendar sync a tenant must connect a `google_calendar` integration credential and (for token refresh) set `GOOGLE_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID`/`GOOGLE_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET`; the per-member calendar id defaults to the user's email, so reading other users' calendars needs Workspace domain-wide read or per-user consent. **Minor code follow-ups:** the merge-path deployment write has no `env` to bump the workforce-metrics cache version (a fresh DORA read can lag up to the token TTL / next status write); the Epic fan-out recommender ranks on capacity/availability only (no per-child skill hint passed yet).

- **No pause/resume execution lifecycle ŌĆö the chip's `resume` (play) affordance is unreachable.** The execution chip ([ExecutionChip.tsx](frontend/src/components/agent/ExecutionChip.tsx)) re-runs failed/cancelled executions and is wired to show a play/resume glyph for a `paused` status via the shared [rerunAffordance](frontend/src/components/board/AgentChip.tsx), but the backend `execution_status` enum ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)) has only `pending|submitted|running|completed|failed|cancelled` ŌĆö there is no `paused` state, nor a pause/resume endpoint or a way to checkpoint+resume a cloud run mid-loop. So the `resume` branch never renders today. Also note: "re-run" creates a *new* execution that re-submits the task (it does not continue the old run's context/partial work ŌĆö for cloud runs it re-plans from the PRD and operates on the same ticket branch). Fixing (add a `paused` status + `POST /executions/:id/pause|resume`, persist enough run state to continue, and surface it through the existing chip affordance) unblocks: pausing a long/expensive run and continuing it instead of restarting from scratch.

- **Host-run terminal failures show on the Timeline but not the Log view.** This pass made every terminal failure (orphan-reap, FAILED transition, stale-run reaper) emit a `run.failed` tool-audit event ([recordRunFailureEvent.ts](api/src/application/runtime/recordRunFailureEvent.ts)), so for **cloud** runs the error now appears in both the Logs and Timeline tabs (both derive from `tool_audit_events`). For **self-hosted host** runs the Timeline picks it up (it reads host `tool_audit_events` via `eventsByHost`), but the **Log view** is sourced only from the host's live WebSocket relay stream + cloud-derived lines ([ObservabilityContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/ObservabilityContent.tsx) `cloudLogLines`), so a host that crashed/disconnected before the failure was reaped will not show the `run.failed` line in its Log tab (the host is offline ŌåÆ no WS). Fixing (fold `eventsByHost` error events into the derived log lines, or backfill the host log pane from `tool_audit_events` when the WS is disconnected) unblocks: parity so host failures surface in the Log tab too, not just the Timeline.

- **[PR CREATE + MERGE + CORE DETAIL now multi-provider 2026-06-13 ŌĆö needs live-provider validation + rich-detail parity] In-product PR lifecycle.** The full non-GitHub PR loop now works for **GitHub, GitLab, and Bitbucket Cloud**: [createPullRequest.ts](api/src/application/repos/createPullRequest.ts) (pure `buildCreatePrRequest`: GitHub `POST /pulls` head/base; GitLab `POST /merge_requests` source/target_branch; Bitbucket `POST /pullrequests` nested branch refs) ŌåÆ [mergePullRequest.ts](api/src/application/repos/mergePullRequest.ts) (pure `buildMergeRequest`: GitHub `PUT /pulls/:n/merge`+merge_method; GitLab `PUT /merge_requests/:iid/merge`+squash; Bitbucket `POST /pullrequests/:id/merge`+merge_strategy) ŌåÆ [getPullRequestDetail.ts](api/src/application/repos/getPullRequestDetail.ts) (core `state`/`merged` all three; GitLab adds mergeable + head-pipeline CI). `buildGitApiBaseUrl` maps GitLab `/api/v4` + Bitbucket Cloud `/2.0`; all request construction is unit-tested. Routes are reachable (no provider gate); `unsupported`ŌåÆ501 only for unknown providers / Bitbucket **Server**. **Residual:** (a) **live-provider validation** ŌĆö request shapes are doc-derived + unit-tested but not yet run against real GitLab/Bitbucket creds; auth is `Bearer <token>` (modern GitLab PATs + Bitbucket Cloud access tokens ŌĆö confirm vs an app-password if used). PR create is now idempotent on all three (a conflict resolves to the existing open PR/MR via `buildFindOpenPrUrl`, +unit-tested). (b) **rich-detail parity** ŌĆö Bitbucket detail is state/merged only (no diffstat/build-statuses); GitLab lacks per-file additions/deletions (needs `/changes`). Fixing unblocks: verified non-GitHub PR createŌåÆmerge + full diff/CI detail parity.

- **All three providers now cover the cloud-agent repo loop; only Bitbucket code-search + live-validation remain.** As of 2026-06-13 GitHub, GitLab, AND Bitbucket Cloud have read (`readRepoFile`/`listRepoFiles`/`listBranchDiff`), write (`commitFileToRepo`/`deleteFileFromRepo`), and PR lifecycle (`createPullRequest`/`mergePullRequest`/`getPullRequestDetail`) ŌĆö all additive + unit-tested (Bitbucket write via the form-encoded `/src` API: branch forked off the base commit `hash`, deletion via the `files` field; branch diff via `/diffstat`). **Residual:** (a) **Bitbucket code search** ŌĆö only GitHub + GitLab implement `searchRepoCode`; Bitbucket's is workspace-scoped (`/workspaces/:ws/search/code`, not repo-scoped) and Premium-gated, so it's deferred. (b) **live-provider validation** ŌĆö the GitLab/Bitbucket request construction is doc-derived + unit-tested but not yet exercised against real GitLab/Bitbucket creds (auth `Bearer <token>`; confirm Bitbucket app-password vs access-token). (c) minor: GitLab/Bitbucket `commitUrl` is returned `null` (their write responses carry no html_url; a follow-up commit lookup would populate it). Fixing unblocks: Bitbucket code search + verified non-GitHub repo operations.

- **The agentHost PR-dispatch path still inserts a placeholder `pull_requests` row (null number) before the host calls back ŌĆö minor residual.** The user-facing bug (a stale numberless placeholder surfacing over a real PR in `GET /tasks/:taskId/pull-request`) is FIXED [1280]: the GET now orders `number IS NOT NULL DESC, createdAt DESC`, and the merge route already 409s a null number. Residual cleanliness only: [RepoService.dispatchPrCreation](api/src/application/repos/RepoService.ts) could upsert on `(task, branch)` instead of insert so a never-arriving callback leaves no orphan row at all (cosmetic ŌĆö nothing surfaces it now).

- **Post-merge build validation + auto-fix is GitHub-Actions-only and reuses the merged ticket branch.** This pass added: record `merge_sha` on the PR at every merge site; correlate the deploy-branch CI build back to the task by that SHA ([ingestRepoCiEvent.ts](api/src/application/ci/ingestRepoCiEvent.ts)); on failure, fetch the failed jobs/steps ([fetchBuildError.ts](api/src/application/ci/fetchBuildError.ts)) and auto-dispatch a fix run (capped at `MAX_AUTOFIX_ATTEMPTS=2` per task via `autofix.dispatch` telemetry count) through the new context-free `dispatchCloudRunForTask`. Remaining gaps: (a) the step-level error fetch only works for **GitHub Actions** (`workflow_run` ŌåÆ jobs API); Cloudflare Pages / `deployment_status` / `check_suite` events record the pass/fail status + run URL but no failed-step detail, so a fix run on those gets a URL-only error summary. (b) The fix run reuses the SAME `builderforce/task-<id>` branch (already merged) rather than a fresh `-fix-<n>` branch ŌĆö the new PR shows only the post-merge diff (works), but the branch history is a bit unclean and the CI-correlation regex assumes one branch per task. (c) `build_status` only populates for PRs whose merge we recorded a `merge_sha` for ŌĆö PRs merged before this pass (or merged directly on the provider) won't validate. (d) Full step LOGS (the actual error text) are a zip we don't unpack in the Worker ŌĆö the agent gets job/step names, not the stack trace; piping a trimmed log tail would improve fix quality. Fixing unblocks: build validation for non-GitHub-Actions CI, cleaner fix branches, and richer fix prompts.

- **No pre-`finish` completeness/self-review loop for cloud agents ŌĆö the prompt is the only guard against premature finish.** Execution #20 had the V2 cloud agent write a single stub file then call `finish`. This pass tightened the system prompt + `finish` tool description ([runtimeRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) to forbid finishing with stubs/unimplemented requirements, and removed the auto-merge so an incomplete run now lands in an OPEN PR for human review instead of on `main` (the real safety net). But there is no programmatic check that the deliverables are complete before `finish` is honored (e.g. a reviewer pass, a "no TODO/placeholder" lint, or PRD-requirement coverage). Fixing (a self-review step that re-prompts the agent to verify each PRD requirement is met before accepting `finish`, or a cheap static placeholder scan that rejects `finish` and continues the loop) unblocks: cloud runs that reliably produce complete changes, not scaffolds. Deferred as a larger per-run-token investment.

- **The serverless durable executor has no real V2 (Claude Agent SDK) engine ŌĆö a V2 agent with no live runtime now FAILS LOUDLY instead of silently running gemini.** Root cause of the reported "I kicked off Coder Agent V2 and the logs show BuilderForce Cloud (default)" (execution #26): the durable Worker loop ([runCloudToolLoop](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) only ever calls `ideProxy().complete()` with the gateway-default model + a 4-tool set and never branches on `engine`, while `dispatchAndQueue`/`startDispatchedExecution` forwarded `agent.engine` only to the *host* dispatch message, never to `CloudRunnerDO`/the Worker fallback. So any V2 agent that landed on the durable surface (its `container` runtime offline, or `runtime_surface:'durable'`) ran the V1 gemini tool-loop and ŌĆö when no `cloudAgentRef` reached the API ŌĆö was attributed to the `__default__` bucket. **Fixed this pass:** (a) frontend [RunAgentControl](frontend/src/components/task/RunAgentControl.tsx) now takes `cloudAgentRef` straight from the selected target string, not only from the loaded pool, so a selected agent's identity is never lost; (b) `startDispatchedExecution` now refuses the durable fallback for any `engine !== 'builderforce-v1'`, recording an attributed `runtime.unavailable` event + FAILED status ([failCloudEngineUnavailable](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) telling the user to bring an agent-runtime host / Container online. **Still missing:** an actual serverless V2 executor ŌĆö i.e. drive the Claude Agent SDK loop from the durable surface via the gateway `/llm/v1/messages` bridge (with the V2 toolset), so a V2 agent can run cloud-only without a self-hosted runtime. Until then V2 strictly requires a long-lived runtime. Fixing unblocks: V2 agents runnable on the serverless surface instead of only failing when no runtime is online. Ties to PRD 09 engine-parity gaps.

- **Cloud loop has no code execution, so verification is CI-only ŌĆö now made honest, not fabricated.** Execution #26 also exposed that the agent invented a `run_code` tool (got `unknown tool 'run_code'`), then declared *"I am confident the typecheck will now pass"* and opened a PR without running anything. The Worker executor has no shell and cannot run builds/tests. **Mitigated this pass:** a defined `run_checks` tool that honestly states checks run in CI on the PR; a system-prompt clause forbidding any claim that a check passed; an [assertsUnrunVerification](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) honesty gate that blocks a `finish` summary asserting a check passed (once) to force an honest restatement; and an always-on "ŌÜĀ Not verified in-agent" annotation on both the opened PR body and the run output. **Still heuristic:** the gate is a narrow regex (clear fabrications only); borderline "should resolve the errors" phrasing isn't blocked (the annotation covers it). A structured `finish({ verified: false })` contract + the green-gate (`CLOUD_AUTOMERGE_REQUIRE_GREEN`) are the durable fixes. Fixing unblocks: cloud PRs that never present unrun checks as passing.

- **Execution #26 likely opened an INVALID fix (PR #12 on Fix-Faster-LLC/hired.video) ŌĆö repo-state cleanup, not code.** The gemini fallback added `.ts` extensions to relative imports in `api/src/db/schema/localizations.ts`. TypeScript NodeNext/ESM requires `.js` specifiers even for `.ts` sources (`allowImportingTsExtensions` is editor-only), so the change probably does not compile ŌĆö and nothing verified it (see above). The PR should be closed or corrected; this is operator repo state outside this workspace. Fixing unblocks: not shipping a non-compiling change merged on the agent's unverified word.

- **[ANALYZED 2026-06-13 ŌĆö likely-correct failover, not drift; needs exec-#26 trace to close] Gateway model-id prefix `googleai/gemini-2.5-flash-lite` (step 0) vs `google/gemini-2.5-flash-lite` (steps 1+) within one run.** Re-analysis: `googleai/*` (direct Google AI, [vendors/googleai.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/googleai.ts), in `PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS` [LlmProxyService.ts](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts)) and `google/*` (Google **via OpenRouter**) are TWO DISTINCT upstream vendors. `vendorForModel()` ([vendors/registry.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/registry.ts)) already keys cooldown + cost to the correct separate vendor for each prefix, so the "split accounting" is *correct* (two real upstreams), and force-normalizing the prefix would WRONGLY merge them. The per-step prefix change is the cascade failing over between the two Google routes ŌĆö expected behavior ŌĆö UNLESS the run had a strict model pin that a later step violated. Closing requires the execution-#26 `llm.complete` trace (operator/data-gated) to confirm pin-vs-failover; no code change is warranted under the failover reading. Fixing the pin path (if confirmed) unblocks: strict-pinned runs never silently swapping Google upstreams mid-run.

- **Card/List `ViewToggle` rollout skipped a few non-tabular / delegated surfaces.** This pass added the shared [ViewToggle](frontend/src/components/ViewToggle.tsx) + [dataTableStyles](frontend/src/components/dataTableStyles.ts) to all primary data-list pages (projects, dashboard, content-manager, prompts, workforce, members, api-keys, logs, approvals, admin users/tenants, llm-traces, marketplace, skills, personas, contributors, shoutouts, showcase, integrations, agent skills). **Not converted:** (a) [chats/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/chats/page.tsx) ŌĆö the conversation sidebar is a messaging UI, not a tabular record set, so a List view was judged inapplicable; (b) [settings/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/settings/page.tsx) Connected Accounts / Active Sessions / Admin Access sections ŌĆö still card-only with no toggle; (c) the **assigned** tab on skills/personas, which delegates to `SkillAssignmentsContent` / `PersonaAssignmentsContent` ŌĆö the `ViewToggle` is hidden there and those child components have no table view; (d) [TaskMgmtContent](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) keeps its own **Board/List** switch (not relabeled to Card/List) since it already offers dual views. Fixing (decide whether settings sections + the assigned tabs warrant a list view, and whether TaskMgmt's Board/List should be unified under the shared `ViewToggle` vocabulary) unblocks: fully uniform view-switching vocabulary across every surface.

- **Agent card/badge/price/skill rendering was consolidated; the non-agent marketplace listings and the table chrome were not.** This pass extracted shared agent primitives ŌĆö [AgentCard](frontend/src/components/workforce/AgentCard.tsx) (owned/purchased/marketplace variants), [AgentOwnerActions](frontend/src/components/workforce/AgentOwnerActions.tsx), [AgentTypePill](frontend/src/components/AgentTypePill.tsx), [StatusBadge](frontend/src/components/StatusBadge.tsx) (+ `.badge-muted` in [globals.css](frontend/src/app/globals.css)), [SkillTags](frontend/src/components/SkillTags.tsx), [formatAgentPrice](frontend/src/lib/agentPresentation.ts) ŌĆö and rewired [WorkforceAgents](frontend/src/components/workforce/WorkforceAgents.tsx) (card + list) and the marketplace workforce section onto them. **Still duplicated:** (a) the marketplace **main listings** (personas/skills/content) in [marketplace/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/marketplace/page.tsx) re-inline their own price formatting, type badges, and tag-pill slicing ŌĆö `formatAgentPrice`/`SkillTags` are agent-typed but the same rules apply to artifacts; (b) there is still no shared `<DataTable columns rows />` ŌĆö every list view (marketplace ├Ś2, showcase, integrations, skills, WorkforceAgents) hand-writes its own `<thead>/<tbody>` against [dataTableStyles](frontend/src/components/dataTableStyles.ts). Fixing (generalize the price/tag helpers to an artifact-agnostic shape and introduce a `DataTable` that owns thead/tbody) unblocks: one row-rendering path for every collection page, not just agents.

- **No `GOOGLE_API_KEY` (nor `NVIDIA`/`CEREBRAS`/`OLLAMA`/`CLOUDFLARE` keys) bound in production ŌĆö the cascade is OpenRouter-only.** [wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml) documents only `OPENROUTER_API_KEY` + `_PRO` as secrets. Consequence: the two `googleai/*` entries in [`PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS`](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) are always skipped (key-unbound), every non-OpenRouter free model in the pool is dead weight, and the *only* paid safety net is OpenRouter-routed Gemini ŌĆö a single upstream with no vendor diversity. The new guaranteed backstop (`GUARANTEED_BACKSTOP_MODEL`, this pass) leans entirely on `OPENROUTER_API_KEY_PRO` having credit; if that key lacks paid balance the backstop 402s and the request still hard-fails. Fixing (`wrangler secret put GOOGLE_API_KEY` so direct Gemini becomes a vendor-diverse backstop, confirm `OPENROUTER_API_KEY_PRO` is a credited key, and document the optional free-vendor keys) unblocks: real multi-vendor failover instead of a single-upstream dependency, and a backstop that can't 402.

- **LLM trace capture is wired for the gateway chat route and IDE chat, but not brain / dataset-gen / agent-inference callers.** [traceLogger.logTrace](api/src/application/llm/traceLogger.ts) is invoked from [llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts) (`/v1/chat/completions`) and [ideAiRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideAiRoutes.ts) (`/api/ai/chat`). Other internal `ideProxy(...).complete()` callers ŌĆö [BrainService](api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts), the workforce agent inference endpoint, dataset generation, and `/v1/images/generations` in [llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts) ŌĆö still pass through the proxy (so a `traceId` is minted and the cooldown/failover path runs) but never call `logTrace`, so those calls are invisible in the superadmin trace view. Fixing (thread `newTraceId()` + `logTrace` through each remaining caller with the right `surface` label ŌĆö `brain` / `agent` / `dataset-gen` / `image`) unblocks: full-surface diagnostic coverage, not just the public gateway.

- **A cloud run still targets exactly ONE repo ŌĆö no multi-repo *spanning* for a task whose change crosses repositories.** Run-time repo *selection* shipped (a task pins `tasks.explicit_repo_id` via [migration 0110](api/migrations/0110_task_explicit_repo.sql); [resolveDefaultRepoForTask](api/src/application/repos/resolveDefaultRepo.ts) now delegates to the pure [resolveRepoForTask](api/src/application/repos/resolveRepo.ts) ŌĆö explicit pin ŌåÆ inferred-by-matchHints ŌåÆ single default, falling back to the legacy default/most-recent pick so nothing regresses; the [RunAgentControl](frontend/src/components/task/RunAgentControl.tsx) picker, shown when a project has >1 repo, sends `repoId` in the run payload, validated + stamped at dispatch so the run/finalize/CI/PRD all use the same repo). The picker's repo list is served through the read-through cache (`project-repos:<tenant>:<project>`, invalidated on every repo CRUD route). **Still open:** a single run cannot edit MULTIPLE repos at once ŌĆö the ticket model is one branch (`builderforce/task-<id>`) ŌåÆ one PR ŌåÆ one repo, so a task that legitimately spans repos (e.g. shared types in repo A + consumer in repo B) needs N branches/PRs and a loop that resolves a repo per file/sub-task. Fixing (a per-task repo *set* with a branch+PR per repo, and a loop that routes each write to the right repo via matchHints/pathGlobs) unblocks: cross-repo changes in one run. Lower priority ŌĆö the common case (wrong single repo bound) is now fixed by selection. Related to the "happy-path validated" (PRD 09) entry above.

- **CI/deploy auto-merge: the safety follow-ups remaining after this pass.** The build/deploy feedback loop now exists ŌĆö [githubWebhookRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/githubWebhookRoutes.ts) ingests `check_suite`/`check_run`/`workflow_run`/`deployment_status`/`status` and [ingestRepoCiEvent](api/src/application/ci/ingestRepoCiEvent.ts) correlates them to the task's latest execution and records a `ci.*`/`deploy.status` `tool_audit_event` (visible on the run's Logs/Timeline). An opt-in **merge-only-on-green** gate (`CLOUD_AUTOMERGE_REQUIRE_GREEN`, [cloudAutoMergeRequiresGreen](api/src/application/repos/mergeBranchToBase.ts)) defers the immediate merge to a green CI/deploy webhook. **Still open:** (a) requires the *target* repo to have a webhook ŌåÆ `/api/webhooks/github` with those events + `GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET` set (no auto-provisioning); (b) a **failed** deploy is recorded but only surfaces in Logs/Timeline ŌĆö there's no task-card badge or `needs_attention` flag (would need a status column on the task/execution); (c) when the gate is on and no CI ever runs, the ticket branch is left open and never merges (no timeout/fallback). Fixing unblocks: a hard failure signal on the board, not just in the timeline. Ties to PRD 09 GAP-W6.

- **V1 cloud loop still auto-merges UNVERIFIED code when the green-gate is off (the operator default).** With `CLOUD_AUTOMERGE_REQUIRE_GREEN` unset, the shell-less V1 loop merges best-effort edits straight to the deploy branch without compiling/testing. The opt-in gate (above) is the mitigation; routing test-gated tasks to V2 (which has Bash) is the other. Fixing (make the green-gate the default once the webhook is provisioned everywhere, or add a provider-side "trigger CI + poll" pre-merge check) unblocks: no unverified code reaching `main` by default.

- **Host-scoped Logs/Timeline aren't execution-filtered, so a V2/host run's panel shows ALL the host's events, not just the selected run.** V2 telemetry now persists with `execution_id` (the cloud `/agents/:ref/tool-audit?executionId=` path filters precisely), but the host path `GET /api/agent-hosts/:id/tool-audit` ([agentHostRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/agentHostRoutes.ts)) only filters by `runId`/`sessionKey`, and the panel uses host scope (not the executionId-filtered cloud path) when `execution.agentHostId` is set. So a V2 run's Logs/Timeline include the host's other runs. Fixing (add an `executionId` filter to the host tool-audit GET + have the panel use it for host scope, or route the panel's per-execution Logs/Timeline through the execution-scoped cloud endpoint regardless of host vs cloud) unblocks: per-execution precision for V2/host runs to match V1.

- **[TOKENS FIXED 2026-06-13] Streaming traces ŌĆö response-body capture is the remaining half.** Token back-fill DONE [1298]: the gateway chat stream's `onUsage` callback now calls `backfillTraceUsage` ([traceLogger.ts](api/src/application/llm/traceLogger.ts)) ŌåÆ `UPDATE llm_traces SET prompt/completion/total_tokens WHERE trace_id`, so a streamed trace shows real token counts instead of 0 (was logged up-front at 0). **Residual:** the completion `response_body` is still null for streams ŌĆö capturing it needs tee-ing the stream into a buffer (the higher-risk half; tokens were the higher-value one). Also `ideAiRoutes.ts` streams aren't back-filled yet (only the gateway chat path). Fixing the body-tee unblocks: full streamed-call diagnostics.

- **Project Calendar/Gantt views are read-only and derive deadlines from tasks ŌĆö no in-view editing and no project-level date column.** This pass added Calendar + Gantt view modes to the projects page ([ProjectCalendar](frontend/src/components/ProjectCalendar.tsx), [ProjectGantt](frontend/src/components/ProjectGantt.tsx), shared [projectSchedule.ts](frontend/src/lib/projectSchedule.ts)/[ScheduleLegend](frontend/src/components/ScheduleLegend.tsx)), wired through the now-generic [ViewToggle](frontend/src/components/ViewToggle.tsx). A project has no date column of its own, so [GET /api/projects](api/src/presentation/routes/projectRoutes.ts) derives `startDate` (min task start, falling back to min due) and `dueDate` (max task due) by aggregating non-archived `tasks` rows. **Scope cuts:** (a) the views are display-only ŌĆö there's no drag-to-reschedule or click-to-set-deadline, so changing a timeline still means editing individual task dates in the task UI; (b) the derived range recomputes on every list fetch with a `min/max ... group by project_id` aggregate that is NOT run through the read-through cache (`getOrSetCached`) the perf rule mandates ŌĆö at high project/task counts this is an uncached fan-over-tasks scan on the hot `/api/projects` path; (c) the Calendar plots only the deadline (`dueDate`) as a single-day pill and does not render multi-day spans across the grid the way the Gantt does. Fixing (cache the per-project date aggregate keyed by a tenant task-version token invalidated on task write; add an editable mode that PATCHes task dates from the timeline; optionally a true project-level milestone/deadline column) unblocks: cached timeline reads, in-place rescheduling, and a project-owned deadline independent of task data. The View-Toggle vocabulary note (TaskMgmt's Board/List) in the rollout entry above also now applies to these two new modes.

- **Agent-host liveness depends on the 5-min heartbeat; the relay DO / WS path does not refresh `lastSeenAt` on its own.** The online-status fix ([onlineStatus.ts](api/src/domain/agentHost/onlineStatus.ts)) treats a host with a stale `lastSeenAt` (>15 min) as OFFLINE even while its socket is up, so liveness now hinges entirely on the periodic HTTP heartbeat landing. This pass found the agent-runtime relay ([builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts)) targets `/api/agentNodes/:id/{upstream,heartbeat,assignment-context}`, a path the worker never mounted (only `/api/agent-hosts` + the `/api/claws` alias) ŌĆö so the heartbeat was 404ing and `lastSeenAt` only moved on (re)connect. Mitigated this pass by adding an `/api/agentNodes` back-compat route mount in [index.ts](api/src/index.ts) so heartbeats now land. **Still open:** (a) the runtime/worker naming is now triplicated (`claws`/`agent-hosts`/`agentNodes`) and should converge on one ŌĆö repoint the runtime to `/api/agent-hosts` and drop both aliases; (b) the WS `/upstream` handler ([agentHostRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/agentHostRoutes.ts)) sets `lastSeenAt` only at connect, and the [AgentHostRelayDO](api/src/infrastructure/relay/AgentHostRelayDO.ts) never bumps it ŌĆö add a periodic `lastSeenAt` touch on the live socket as defense-in-depth so a host stays ONLINE even if the HTTP heartbeat is blocked. Fixing unblocks: liveness that doesn't silently depend on one easily-misrouted heartbeat call.

- **Gateway prompt caching covers the Anthropic family only ŌĆö Gemini relies on implicit caching, no explicit breakpoints.** [promptCaching.ts `modelSupportsExplicitCaching`](api/src/application/llm/promptCaching.ts) deliberately gates to `anthropic/*` / `claude` ids (the only OpenRouter upstreams that *require* an explicit marker and are known to honour it without a 400). `google/*` (via OpenRouter) and the direct `googleai` vendor cache implicitly above the model minimum, so they get *some* caching for free ŌĆö but explicit breakpoints would give tunable placement and a higher hit rate on long stable prefixes. Held back to avoid 400s on providers that reject the unknown `cache_control` field. Fixing (extend the gate + a per-vendor allowlist once Gemini-via-OpenRouter explicit-cache behaviour is confirmed against a live call) unblocks: tunable Gemini prompt caching, not just whatever the provider caches implicitly.

- **Cloud Worker agent toolset is minimal (write_file/finish) and V1 self-hosted (pi) tool events may still be relay-only.** This pass made both cloud engines genuinely *execute tools*: [runCloudExecution](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) now runs a real tool loop ([runCloudToolLoop](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts), up to 6 steps) where the model calls provider-API-backed tools ŌĆö `write_file` commits to the ticket branch as a pending change ([commitFileAsPendingChange.ts](api/src/application/repos/commitFileAsPendingChange.ts) ŌåÆ opens a PR) and `finish` ends the run ŌĆö emitting an `llm.complete` + per-tool event each step (migration 0092 columns). V2's agent-runtime SDK loop now *persists* its tool calls too: [builderforce-relay.ts `persistToolAudit`](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts) POSTs each `onToolUse` to the agent-host tool-audit ingest (Bearer agent-host key) instead of live-relay-only. **Residual:** (a) the Worker toolset has only `write_file`/`finish` ŌĆö no `read_file`/`search`/`run_tests`/`apply_patch`, so the cloud Worker agent can write but not inspect the repo or self-verify; richer tools need a read path through the provider contents API. (b) The V1 self-hosted **pi** coding loop's tool calls are not confirmed to flow through `persistToolAudit`/the ingest ŌĆö only V2's `onToolUse` was wired this pass; verify whether pi emits `tool.audit` only over the relay (live, non-durable) and wire it the same way if so. Fixing unblocks: cloud agents that can read+verify their own work, and durable timelines for V1 self-hosted runs.

- **Cloud log view is polled, not streamed.** Cloud agents have no live relay socket, so the unified Log view derives cloud log lines from polled tool-audit telemetry with a manual "Refresh cloud" button ([ObservabilityContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/ObservabilityContent.tsx)) rather than a live tail. Self-hosted hosts still stream live over the relay WS. Fixing (a per-execution cloud log stream ŌĆö the cloud equivalent of `logs.subscribe`, e.g. an SSE/WS tail of the execution's events) unblocks: live cloud logs without a refresh button. (Note: `/timeline` now renders the D3 [ExecutionTimelineChart](frontend/src/components/ExecutionTimelineChart.tsx) via `ObservabilityContent` and is the intended timeline visual; the sidebar links `/observability`, which holds the same chart behind the Log/Timeline toggle.)

- **builderforce-memory's `CachingBridge`/`ResponseCache` (response-level cache) is still unused by the gateway and agent-runtime ŌĆö separate mechanism from this pass's prompt caching.** This pass added Anthropic *prompt* caching (provider-side prefix reuse, billed at ~0.1x). It does **not** touch [builderforce-memory's CachingBridge / ResponseCache](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory/src/bridges/CachingBridge.ts) (an SSM-embedding-keyed response cache that returns a stored completion without an upstream call at all). The two are complementary: prompt caching discounts the input of calls that still happen; response caching elides the call entirely on a semantic hit. Fixing (wire `CachingBridge`/`ResponseCache` into the gateway read path for idempotent/low-temperature `useCase`s, with the same version-token invalidation the project's read-through cache uses) unblocks: zero-cost responses on repeated/near-duplicate prompts, on top of the per-call prompt-cache discount.

- **Deployed Cloudflare Pages output drifted ~2.5 months stale, silently shipping the pre-COOP/COEP `_headers` and pre-fix IDE bundle.** Observed 2026-06-05: `.vercel/output/static/_headers` was dated 2026-03-16 (containing only the next-on-pages autogenerated immutable-cache block, **no `Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy`/`Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy`**) while `public/_headers` + the IDE components were dated 2026-06-02. Result on the live site: `/ide` is not cross-origin isolated ŌåÆ `self.crossOriginIsolated === false` ŌåÆ WebContainer "Run" fails to boot ("WC error"), **and** the stale JS bundle predates the June-2 Designer editor fixes (file-click not switching content, `package.json` getting CSS written into it). Root process gap: nothing guarantees a `cf-build` + redeploy after `public/_headers` or IDE source changes ŌĆö the deploy artifact can lag source indefinitely with no alarm. Fixing (a CI deploy job that always rebuilds from source on merge to main, plus a post-build assertion that `.vercel/output/static/_headers` contains both COOP `same-origin` and COEP `credentialless` before publishing) unblocks: the live `/ide` matching source, and WebContainer Run never silently dying on a header regression. Immediate remediation for this incident: run `npm run cf-build` and redeploy.

- ~~**The `/v1/usage` gateway endpoint still can't split usage by source (cloud/on-prem/web) ŌĆö only `/api/dashboard/usage` can.**~~ **Ō£ģ RESOLVED 2026-06-21.** `/v1/usage` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) now returns a `bySource` aggregate (requests + prompt/completion/total tokens grouped by cloud/on-prem/web). The classifier was extracted from `dashboardRoutes.ts` into a shared [usageSource.ts](api/src/application/llm/usageSource.ts) (`USAGE_KIND`) and is now the ONE definition both surfaces consume (DRY) ŌĆö the dashboard imports it instead of its former local copy, so `/v1/usage` and `/api/dashboard/usage` can never disagree on the split. api 1141 tests green. (Cost-millicents sum on `/v1/usage` intentionally left to the dashboard, which is the cost surface; the source split ŌĆö the actual gap ŌĆö is closed.)

- **[DONE 2026-06-18] agent-runtime loads the SSM memory hippocampus in production.** `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory`(+`-engine`)`@^2026.6.20` added to [agent-runtime/package.json](agent-runtime/package.json) `optionalDependencies`; [ssm-memory-service.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/ssm-memory-service.ts) dynamically imports it (guarded), `server-startup` boots `initSsmMemoryService`, the orchestrator injects `recallSimilar` into task prompts, and `KnowledgeLoopService` remembers/learns per run. The 48h `pnpm.minimumReleaseAge` cooldown (which refuses freshly-published versions) was bypassed for FIRST-PARTY packages only via `minimumReleaseAgeExclude` ŌĆö the guard still applies to all third-party deps. Verified: recall/remember loads + works in the agent-runtime env; install resolves `2026.6.20`, lockfile committed.

- **Fully configurable boards rely on free-form `tasks.status` strings keyed to swimlanes ŌĆö no referential integrity links a task's status to a lane.** `tasks.status` is now a `varchar` (migration [0076](api/migrations/0076_task_status_freeform.sql), [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)) and the board columns are the project's swimlanes ([boardColumns](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) + [LanesTab](frontend/src/components/board/BoardConfigPanel.tsx)), seeded from [defaultSwimlanes.ts](api/src/application/swimlane/defaultSwimlanes.ts). The coupling is now by string convention only (`task.status === swimlane.key`), with no FK: (a) **deleting/renaming a lane key orphans tasks** holding the old key ŌĆö they surface in an auto-appended fallback column (`boardColumns` orphan pass) but there's no migration to move them onto a surviving lane; (b) the same status string can mean different columns in different projects, and there's no per-project uniqueness enforcement on `swimlane.key`; (c) automation still keys off the canonical strings (`RuntimeService` sets `in_progress`/`in_review`/`done`; auto-submit fires on `todo`/`in_progress`), so a board that renames/removes those lane keys silently loses that automation. Fixing (a real `swimlane_id` FK on `tasks` with `ON DELETE SET NULL` + a lane-merge/reassign flow on delete, and moving automation triggers onto a per-lane flag instead of hard-coded status strings) unblocks: referential safety for configurable boards and automation that follows user-defined lanes instead of the canonical seven.

- **Board agent-status chips are a load-time snapshot, not live.** The running-agent chip on each task card/row ([TaskMgmtContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) `latestExecByTask`, fed by `runtimeApi.listRecent()`) is fetched once in `load()` and only refreshes on a full board reload (status change, task CRUD). A task whose agent transitions runningŌåÆcompleted while the board sits open keeps showing the stale status until the next reload. The drawer's Agent tab is live per-execution, but the board overview is not. **The new swimlane dispatch-status chips on lane headers share this limitation:** `latestDispatchByAssignment` (fed by `boardsApi.dispatches(boardId)`) is fetched once per board-view mount with no polling, so a dispatch transitioning pendingŌåÆrunningŌåÆcompleted while the board sits open shows stale status until a remount. Fixing (poll both `runtimeApi.listRecent()` and `boardsApi.dispatches()` on an interval while any task/dispatch is active, or subscribe to the existing `/api/runtime/executions/:id/stream` SSE plus a new dispatch-status stream for visible active lanes) unblocks: accurate at-a-glance agent status without manually reloading.

- **Swimlane agent assignments still write to `swimlane_agent_assignments`, not the canonical `agent_assignments` (0082).** This pass made the assign-agent form pick a registered/workforce agent from the project registry ([projectAgents.list](frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts) ŌåÆ [AgentList](frontend/src/components/board/BoardConfigPanel.tsx)), resolving its runtime/host/model at write time via [resolveAssignedAgent.ts](api/src/application/swimlane/resolveAssignedAgent.ts) and storing `agent_kind`/`agent_ref` alongside the resolved `role/runtime/target/model` on `swimlane_agent_assignments` (migration [0084](api/migrations/0084_swimlane_actions.sql)). The canonical [agent_assignments](api/migrations/0082_agent_assignments.sql) table (`scope='swimlane'`), explicitly built to *replace* this per-lane assignment model, is still unused for swimlanes ŌĆö so there are now two assignment stores. Fixing (migrate the swimlane dispatch pipeline ŌĆö [compileStage](api/src/application/swimlane/compileStage.ts) + [DrizzleCoordinatorStore.listAssignments](api/src/application/swimlane/DrizzleCoordinatorStore.ts) ŌĆö onto `agent_assignments`, backfill, and drop `swimlane_agent_assignments`) unblocks: one assignment model across project/workflow/swimlane.

- **Legal documents render with chat-message typography.** The new shared [LegalDocPreview](frontend/src/components/admin/LegalDocPreview.tsx) control (used by the admin legal tab, the editor drawer preview, and the public footer modal) renders Markdown through [ChatMessageContent](frontend/src/components/ChatMessageContent.tsx) ŌĆö a renderer tuned for chat bubbles (0.82rem body text, uppercase code-fence chrome with a "Copy" button). The three previews are now consistent with each other and with the live footer modal, but the typography is sub-optimal for long-form legal prose. Fixing (give `LegalDocPreview` its own document-scale Markdown component map ŌĆö larger body/heading sizes, prose line-length ŌĆö instead of delegating to the chat renderer) unblocks: legal docs that read like documents rather than chat transcripts, without re-diverging the three call sites.

- **[MOSTLY CLOSED 2026-06-13] Legal-doc content ŌĆö write-normalization done; only the historical backfill remains.** New docs are now normalized on WRITE: `LegalEditorDrawer.handleSave` runs `unwrapMarkdownFence(content)` before `publishLegal`/`amendLegal` [1328], so the stored value is clean for every consumer (API/exports/Copy), not just the React render path (which still unwraps idempotently). **Residual (operator):** a one-off backfill of pre-existing rows written before this change ŌĆö until then the render-time unwrap stays as the safety net (can't be retired yet). No code change available for the backfill without live-DB access.

- **Token-cost enhancement: agent-runtime has the SSM hippocampus wired but no InferenceRouter offload.** [agent-runtime/src/infra/ssm-memory-service.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/ssm-memory-service.ts) loads `@builderforce/memory` and exposes `recallSimilar()`/`learn()`, and the local amygdala (Qwen3-0.6B) already does simple/complex triage ([builderforcellm-local-stream.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforcellm-local-stream.ts)) ŌĆö so this is an *enhancement*, not a bug. The library's `InferenceRouter` (perplexity/length/complexity ŌåÆ SSM-vs-cortex) could short-circuit cheap/repeated queries to the local SSM before paying the cortex, on top of the existing triage. Unblocks: further cortex-call avoidance.

- **Token-cost enhancement: agent-runtime compaction is reactive, not proactive.** [agent-runtime/src/agents/compaction.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/compaction.ts) has the machinery (`estimateMessagesTokens`, `chunkMessagesByMaxTokens`, `stripToolResultDetails`) but it only fires on context overflow; the tool loop in [builderforcellm-local-stream.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforcellm-local-stream.ts) resends the full growing message list every round. Summarizing completed sub-tasks after N tool rounds (using the hippocampus to distill) rather than waiting for window overflow would cut ~20ŌĆō30% per-turn on long tool-heavy runs.

- **Semantic cache (2026-06-06): the agent cortex call is not yet wrapped, so the agent isn't saving tokens yet.** The `@builderforce/memory` `SemanticCache` (L1 on-device SSM embeddings + L2 gateway) is fully built and wired into [`SsmMemoryService`](agent-runtime/src/infra/ssm-memory-service.ts) (public `semanticCache` field + `getCachedOrGenerate`, 3 tests green), and the shared L2 endpoint ships at [`/v1/semantic-cache`](api/src/presentation/routes/semanticCacheRoutes.ts) (6 tests green). **Not yet done:** the cortex seam [`callExecutionLlm`](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforcellm-local-stream.ts) (called at the code/fix/direct passes) does not consult the cache. Wiring it needs the cache threaded down ŌĆö `runBuilderForceAgentsLlmLocalRequest(request)` takes only `request`, so add `semanticCache?` to `BuilderForceAgentsLlmLocalRunRequest` and populate it from the `SsmMemoryService`-owning caller ŌĆö plus nullable-result handling (do **lookup-first / store-only-on-non-null** via `service.semanticCache.lookup`/`.store`, not `getOrGenerate`, since the provider loop can return `null`) and a query derived from the last user message. Needs live agent verification. Fixing turns the built capability into actual agent-side token savings.

- **[DONE 2026-06-18] Active cross-run memory tools for Node agents.** The declared-but-unused `memory` capability is completed: `@builderforce/agent-tools` now ships `memory_recall`/`memory_remember` `ToolDefinition`s (`requires: ["memory"]`, in `CORE_TOOLS`); on-prem [agent-runtime/src/agents/memory-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/memory-tools.ts) backs `memory` with the in-process SSM service (`getSsmMemoryService`) and folds the tools into every run via [coding-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/coding-tools.ts) (self-gating ŌåÆ `[]` when the layer is absent). So on-prem + cloud-container (Node) agents can ACTIVELY recall/remember mid-run, not just the passive `recallSimilar` injection. Additive + capability-gated, so Worker/Container surfaces (which don't advertise `memory` in `CLOUD_SURFACE_CAPS`/`CONTAINER_SURFACE_CAPS`) filter them out ŌĆö agent-tools, agent-runtime (tsgo), and api (tsc) all 0 errors; 7 vitest cases.
- **[DONE 2026-06-18] Server-side semantic cache wired into the cortex call.** `SsmMemoryService.getCachedOrGenerate` was dead (only its own test). [builderforcellm-local-stream.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforcellm-local-stream.ts) now fronts the cortex provider cascade (`callExecutionLlm` ŌåÆ `runProviderCascade`) with it, so a semantically-repeated prompt returns a prior answer (L1 on-device SSM embeddings, optional L2 gateway) instead of re-billing the frontier model. Memoised generator (no double-cascade on the cache's degrade path) + a sentinel so total provider failure returns null without caching an empty answer; degrades to a direct cascade when the memory layer is absent.
- **[DONE 2026-06-18] Worker/DO active memory ŌĆö Postgres-backed.** `'memory'` added to `CLOUD_SURFACE_CAPS` ([cloudAgentTools.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentTools.ts)) + `memory:` wired into `buildCloudProvider` ([cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)) via [cloudMemory.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudMemory.ts) ŌĆö the Worker-safe twin of the on-prem SSM store: migration 0200 + schema `agent_memory` (tenant-scoped keyŌåÆfact, unique `(tenant_id,key)` upsert), lexical (ILIKE) recall served through `getOrSetCached` with a per-tenant version token bumped on write. All errors degrade to `{ok:false}` so a pre-migration table never breaks a run; activates when migration 0200 deploys. tsc + schema-drift + migration-sequence checks pass; mock-db unit tests. Container surface intentionally omitted (its image loop would need the handler). 
- **[DONE 2026-06-20] Web (browser) `SemanticCache` (L1).** [semantic-cache.ts](frontend/src/lib/semantic-cache.ts) fronts the cloud-inference path (`ExternalLLMProvider.generate/stream` in [model-provider.ts](frontend/src/lib/model-provider.ts)) with a read-through `SemanticCache` backed by an on-device WebGPU SSM embedder (`SSM.create` ŌåÆ `runtime.embed`), loaded via dynamic `import()` (out of the main bundle). Gracefully `null` when WebGPU/assets are absent ŌåÆ falls through to the network; `runThroughCache` is pure/DI (4 vitest cases). WebGPU gate shared via `hasWebGPU()` (DRY). frontend tsc 0 errors. Browser smoke-test (WebGPU + COOP/COEP + deployed `/vocab.json` assets) is the remaining live validation. **Scope-cut (logged):** (a) **L2 not wired** ŌĆö only L1 (in-session vector list) is active; the cross-surface win (a web cache hit reused by an agent and vice-versa) needs `FetchSemanticCacheBackend` pointed at a gateway semantic-cache HTTP endpoint + tenant token (no such endpoint exists yet ŌĆö `SsmMemoryService`'s L2 hook is the server twin). (b) **Possible double model-load** ŌĆö the cache builds its own `SSMRuntime` session separate from `MambaModelProvider`'s engine model; harmless today (local vs cloud providers rarely both active) but a shared on-device runtime would save memory when they are.

- **Gateway semantic-cache L2 is KV brute-force, not a vector index.** [`semanticCache.ts`](api/src/application/llm/semanticCache.ts) keeps a bounded (200-entry) per-tenant+namespace list in `SEMANTIC_CACHE_KV` and brute-forces cosine on lookup ŌĆö fine at that bound, but it caps recall and won't scale to large tenants. Upgrade path: a Cloudflare **Vectorize** index keyed per tenant/namespace (ANN lookup, no 200-entry cap), keeping the same `/v1/semantic-cache` wire contract so clients don't change. Also: `SEMANTIC_CACHE_KV` must be provisioned + bound in `wrangler.toml` (unbound today ŌåÆ the endpoint degrades to miss/no-op and clients run L1-only). Fixing unblocks production-scale shared caching.

- **Per-agent cron is now storable + scoped in the UI, but the cron poller doesn't route a fired job to that agent yet.** This pass added `cron_jobs.project_agent_id` ([migration 0081](api/migrations/0081_cron_per_project_agent.sql) + [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)), threaded it through the cron GET/POST ([agentHostRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/agentHostRoutes.ts) ŌĆö `projectAgentId` numeric=agent, `none`=project-wide/NULL), `cronApi` ([builderforceApi.ts](frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts)), and `CronJobsContent` ŌåÆ so the Agent/Capabilities tab shows project-wide schedules under "Project-wide" and per-agent schedules under each selected agent. **Still open:** the cron executor still fires on the project's `assignedAgentHostId` and the poller ignores `project_agent_id` when dispatching ŌĆö so a per-agent schedule is correctly *stored/scoped* but the fired run is not yet directed to that specific agent's duty/runtime. Fixing (have the cron poller pass `project_agent_id` into the dispatched task ŌåÆ resolve that agent's runtime/assignment) unblocks: a per-agent schedule actually executing *as* that agent.

- **CANONICAL AGENT MODEL (stated 2026-06-06) ŌĆö foundation + assignment UI built; runtime-consumption + legacy migration remain.** Target: an agent registered ONCE (tenant-scoped) is *assigned* to platform aspects ŌĆö Project, Workflows (execute under a project OR globally), Architecture analysis, Security, Swimlanes, AI Brain (switch to a chosen Agent **or** Persona); cron per-project AND per-agent. **BUILT this pass:** the single polymorphic store ŌĆö [migration 0082](api/migrations/0082_agent_assignments.sql) + `agentAssignments` ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)) keyed by `(agentKind, agentRef, scope Ōłł project|workflow|architecture|security|swimlane|brain|global, scopeId, executionScope Ōłł project|global)`; [AgentAssignmentService](api/src/application/agent/AgentAssignmentService.ts) (read-through cached, invalidate-on-write) + cached routes [/api/agent-assignments](api/src/presentation/routes/agentAssignmentRoutes.ts); the panel is wired into **Architecture analysis** ([architect/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/architect/page.tsx)) and **Security** ([security/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/security/page.tsx)), and the **Brain** has an Agent/Persona switcher ([BrainPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx)) that overrides the conversation system prompt from `scope='brain'` assignments + built-in modalities. **RUNTIME CONSUMPTION ŌĆö done where a run-path exists:** the architecture-analysis run now executes AS its assigned agent ŌĆö [AnalysisRunnerDO.resolveArchitectAgentModel](api/src/infrastructure/relay/AnalysisRunnerDO.ts) reads `agent_assignments` (scope='architecture') and resolves the agent's real `base_model` via the shared [resolveAssignedAgent](api/src/application/swimlane/resolveAssignedAgent.ts), passing it into [ArchitectAnalysisService](api/src/application/repoanalysis/ArchitectAnalysisService.ts) ŌåÆ the gateway `complete({ model })` (a gateway-resolvable model ŌĆö the earlier `workforce-<id>` string was NOT resolvable by the gateway); the cron poller now runs a per-project-agent schedule in that agent's own session ([cron-poller.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/cron-poller.ts) `projectAgentId` ŌåÆ `project-agent-<id>` session). **NOW CONSUMED (this pass):** (a) **Brain model** ŌĆö DONE: the embedded package gained a per-conversation `model` option ([brain-embedded useBrainConversation](brain-embedded/src/useBrainConversation.ts) + `streamChatCompletion`, dist rebuilt), and [BrainPanel](frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) routes a selected workforce agent to its real `base_model` from the shared [agentPool](frontend/src/lib/agentPool.ts) (the Brain streams to the gateway, which resolves real model ids; persona/registered ŌåÆ default). (a2) **Security** ŌĆö DONE: a real run-path now consumes the assignment ŌĆö [SecurityReviewService](api/src/application/security/SecurityReviewService.ts) + `POST /api/security/review` ([securityReviewRoutes](api/src/presentation/routes/securityReviewRoutes.ts)) reviews supplied code/diff AS the agent assigned to security (`scope='security'` ŌåÆ its model). **CORRECT BY DESIGN (not a gap):** (a3) **registered** agents are external endpoint-based (`agents.endpoint`), so they have no gateway model ŌĆö architecture/security consumption resolves their model to null ŌåÆ default cascade (workforce agents route fully to their `base_model` via `resolveAssignedAgent`). Truly executing AS a registered agent means forwarding to its endpoint (the `/api/agents/:id/forward` dispatch path), a separate integration from gateway model-routing. **STILL OPEN:** (b) **Workflow** execution-scope (project vs global) is now BUILT ŌĆö `workflow_definitions.execution_scope` ([migration 0083](api/migrations/0083_workflow_execution_scope.sql) + [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)), persisted via the definition create/update routes ([workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts)) and a "Runs under project / Runs globally" selector in the builder toolbar ([WorkflowBuilder.tsx](frontend/src/components/workflow-builder/WorkflowBuilder.tsx)); STILL OPEN there: the orchestrator/run path doesn't yet branch behaviour on `executionScope` (it's stored + inherited but not differently executed); (c) **legacy concepts coexist (mostly by design, not duplication)** ŌĆö `agent_assignments` is the canonical *surface-assignment* model; `swimlaneAgentAssignments` is being unified onto the same agent-resolution path by the concurrent lane-action refactor (shared `resolveAssignedAgent`); `project_agents` remains the project *capability-attachment* surface (it carries governance + is the `scopeId` for `artifact_assignments` scope='agent', a distinct concern); and `project.assignedAgentHostId` is the executor *host* (not an agent), also distinct. So the only genuine overlap (swimlane target) is being collapsed by the active refactor; no risky big-bang `project_agents` data migration is warranted. Fixing (optionally fold `project_agents` attachment into `agent_assignments` scope='project' if a single attachment store is later desired) unblocks: one literal table for every attachment ŌĆö currently unnecessary since the concerns differ.- **The cron executor (`project.assignedAgentHost`) is decoupled from the agents attached in the Agent/Capabilities tab.** That tab attaches `project_agents` (workforce/registered refs), but cron executes on the project's `assignedAgentHostId` (a runtime agentHost). So a user can attach an agent yet still see "Assign an agent hostŌĆ” to schedule cron runs" because no executor host is set ŌĆö two different "assign an agent" notions ([project_agents] vs [assignedAgentHost] vs swimlane `swimlaneAgentAssignments.target`). Fixing (when an On-Premise/Cloud agent is attached, set/derive the project's executor `assignedAgentHostId`; unify the three agent-attachment concepts behind one model) unblocks: cron + autonomous execution sharing one coherent "agent assigned to project" concept.

- **Agent-picker consistency sweep (2026-06-07): unified pickers now include cloud agents; two host-only EXECUTION pickers remain (need a host-less cloud executor).** Every "assign/select an agent" surface now draws from the shared [loadAgentPool](frontend/src/lib/agentPool.ts) (owned + purchased + registered): project Agent/Capabilities, swimlane lanes, architecture, security, Brain, Observability's cloud list, and the **task "Run this task" picker** ([RunAgentControl](frontend/src/components/task/RunAgentControl.tsx) ŌĆö now offers Auto + Cloud agents + Self-hosted; picking a cloud agent runs the task AS its `base_model` with an auto/fleet executor). **STILL host-only:** the OLDER workflow-create picker ([WorkflowsContent](frontend/src/components/WorkflowsContent.tsx) "Select agentHostŌĆ”", which pushes a workflow to a specific relay host) ŌĆö the newer [WorkflowBuilder](frontend/src/components/workflow-builder/WorkflowBuilder.tsx) already lists cloud run-targets via `/run-targets`. **Server-side cloud execution now exists (2026-06-07): executions no longer hang in `pending`.** When no online agentHost takes a task dispatch, [runtimeRoutes](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) `runCloudExecution` runs the task server-side via the gateway (`ideProxy.complete` with the chosen agent's `base_model`) and transitions the execution pendingŌåÆrunningŌåÆcompleted with the result (task syncs to in_review). So a cloud/Auto run produces a deliverable instead of stalling. **Residual:** (a) this is a single-completion executor ŌĆö it produces text deliverables (audits, plans, copy) but does NOT clone a repo / run tools / open a PR; coding tasks that need a real workspace still require an agentHost (the headless cloud-coding loop) or browser worker. (b) the OLDER workflow-create picker ([WorkflowsContent](frontend/src/components/WorkflowsContent.tsx)) is still host-only (the newer WorkflowBuilder lists cloud run-targets). Fixing (route coding/tool tasks through the full agent loop server-side, and add cloud agents to the workflow-create picker) unblocks: cloud agents doing full tool-using work with no self-hosted runtime.

- **Cloud agents have no observability stream ŌĆö Observability is relay/agentHost-only.** [ObservabilityContent](frontend/src/components/ObservabilityContent.tsx) streams live logs over the agentHost relay WS and fetches timeline telemetry per `agent_host_id` ([telemetry_spans](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) + [executions](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) are both keyed by `agent_host_id`). Cloud agents (`ide_agents`) run server-side via the gateway and emit NO relay logs and NO agent-keyed telemetry, so they can't be streamed here. This pass (a) folded Observability INTO the project **Agent / Capabilities** tab and removed the standalone Observability tab ([ProjectDetailsPanel](frontend/src/components/ProjectDetailsPanel.tsx) ŌåÆ [AgentCapabilitiesContent](frontend/src/components/AgentCapabilitiesContent.tsx) renders `ObservabilityContent`), since observability is agent-scoped; and (b) renamed "Active Agents" ŌåÆ "Self-hosted agents" with real ONLINE/OFFLINE status per host + a read-only "Cloud agents" list. **Cloud-run debugging now exists via the execution record (2026-06-07):** a cloud/Auto execution shows its **status + output + error** in the Task ŌåÆ Agent tab execution detail ([TaskAgentTab](frontend/src/components/task/TaskAgentTab.tsx) now renders `errorMessage`), and [runCloudExecution](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) stamps the run with `[ran as <model> ┬Ę trace <id>]` so the full LLM request/response is inspectable in the gateway `llm_traces` view. **Residual:** the execution doesn't deep-LINK to its `llm_trace` row, model/tokens aren't structured fields on the detail (only in the debug string), and there's no live token stream (a cloud run is a single server-side completion ŌĆö no process to stream). Fixing (store `trace_id`/`model`/tokens as execution columns + a "view trace" link, plus a per-agent `telemetry_spans` trail + project-scoped Observability query) unblocks: full cloud-agent observability in the same tab.

- **`ArtifactAssigner` has no 'agent' scope ŌĆö a skill/persona/content can't be assigned directly to a cloud agent from its own page.** [ArtifactAssigner](frontend/src/components/ArtifactAssigner.tsx) offers `scope Ōłł host | project | task` only, so from a skill's page you can attach it to an agentHost/project/task but not to a specific cloud agent. The per-agent path DOES exist via the project **Agent / Capabilities** tab ([CapabilitiesContent](frontend/src/components/CapabilitiesContent.tsx) scope='agent' on the project_agent bridge), so this is a missing shortcut, not a missing capability. Fixing (add an 'agent' scope to ArtifactAssigner sourced from the shared `loadAgentPool`, writing `artifact_assignments` scope='agent' against the agent's bridge id) unblocks: assigning a skill/persona to a cloud agent from anywhere, consistently.

- **Skills/Personas pages gate install UI on `agentHosts.length > 0`, ignoring cloud agents.** [skills/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/skills/page.tsx) (and personas) set `hasAgentHosts` from `agentHosts.list()` only, so a tenant whose only agent is a Cloud agent sees the "register a self-hosted agent" gate even though it has an assignable agent. Fixing (compute the gate from the shared `loadAgentPool` ŌĆö any agent of any kind ŌĆö not just relay hosts) unblocks: cloud-only tenants using the skills/personas install flow.

- **Cloud-coding end-to-end (2026-06-06): browser PR-open closed; headless agentHost execution + deploy still open.** This pass made the cloud coding loop real on the **browser** path and built the **server contracts** for the headless path. CLOSED this pass: (1) the browser worker now opens a PR after pushing ŌĆö new [createPullRequest.ts](api/src/application/repos/createPullRequest.ts) (GitHub REST, idempotent on 422) + shared [openDispatchPullRequest.ts](api/src/application/repos/openDispatchPullRequest.ts), driven from `POST /api/agent-runtime/:dispatchId/pull-request` and wired through the browser stack ([transport.ts](frontend/src/lib/browserRuntime/transport.ts)/[coding.ts](frontend/src/lib/browserRuntime/coding.ts)/[factory.ts](frontend/src/lib/browserRuntime/factory.ts)/[AgentWorker.tsx](frontend/src/app/agent-worker/AgentWorker.tsx)), recording the PR in `pull_requests` and writing `tasks.githubPrUrl/PrNumber` back; (2) host-authed result writeback `POST /api/agent-hosts/:id/dispatch-result` ŌåÆ `SwimlaneCoordinator.reportDispatchResult` (the headless analogue of the browser's tenant-JWT `/result`); (3) host-authed dispatch detail `GET /api/agent-hosts/:id/dispatch/:dispatchId` (returns repo coords + the host git-proxy path) and a host-authed git-proxy `(/info/refs|/git-upload-pack|/git-receive-pack)` so a headless host clones/pushes with the token injected SERVER-SIDE (never on the relay); (4) DRY extractions: [agentHostAuth.ts](api/src/infrastructure/auth/agentHostAuth.ts), [resolveRepoCredential.ts](api/src/application/repos/resolveRepoCredential.ts), [resolveDefaultRepo.ts](api/src/application/repos/resolveDefaultRepo.ts), `executeGitProxy` in [gitProxy.ts](api/src/application/repos/gitProxy.ts) (shared by both proxies); (5) confirmed COOP/COEP already cover `/agent-worker` site-wide so the WebContainer build gate boots (the old "worker route needs COOP/COEP" note is stale). The **runtime handler is now built + unit-tested** (CLOSED): the relay ([agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts)) has an `agent_dispatch` case ŌåÆ [builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts) (+ [adapters](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-coding-dispatch-adapters.ts) + [coding-session-broker.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/coding-session-broker.ts)) that calls `GET /api/agent-hosts/:id/dispatch/:dispatchId`, clones via the host git-proxy (`git -c http.extraHeader='Authorization: Bearer <agent-key>'`), runs the embedded agent session, commits/pushes, calls the host PR endpoint, and reports via `POST /api/agent-hosts/:id/dispatch-result`. Deploy artifacts added: [fly.toml](agent-runtime/fly.toml) + [docs/CLOUD_DEPLOY.md](agent-runtime/docs/CLOUD_DEPLOY.md). The Docker build is now unblocked (the `@builderforce/memory` hard dep was removed + lockfile resynced ŌĆö see that entry; `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile` passes). **STILL OPEN (live verification only):** no live cloud run has executed the loop yet ŌĆö the full chain is typecheck- + unit-verified AND covered by an end-to-end integration test ([builderforce-coding-dispatch.integration.test.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-coding-dispatch.integration.test.ts), which drives the real runtime handler + real git/http adapters over a REAL local bare git repo + a fake host API server), but the cloneŌåÆagentŌåÆpushŌåÆPRŌåÆadvance round-trip has not been smoke-tested against a *deployed* Cloud agent + a *real* GitHub repo (that needs a cloud account, a Neon DB, a tenant JWT, and a repo credential ŌĆö external inputs). Fixing unblocks: confirmed production round-trip. NOTE: a swimlane assignment of ANY agent type (Cloud or On-Premise) now routes correctly ŌĆö assignments fall back to the tenant default agent when no explicit target is set ([SwimlaneCoordinator.launchStage](api/src/application/swimlane/SwimlaneCoordinator.ts) + `getDefaultAgentHostId`), and the lane config UI ([BoardConfigPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/board/BoardConfigPanel.tsx)) now offers an agent target picker.

- **Cloud-coding follow-ups.** (a) **Changed-files are text-only** ŌĆö the dispatch `output` now includes the changed-files list + PR link, and `GET /api/agent-runtime/:dispatchId` exposes it, but there is no structured diff/changed-files *viewer* on the kanban card (the card shows the PR URL via `tasks.githubPrUrl`; the PR itself is the real diff). Fixing (a card diff affordance reading the dispatch output) unblocks: an in-board diff without opening the PR. (b) **PR-open is GitHub-only** ŌĆö `createPullRequest` returns `unsupported` for bitbucket/gitlab (branch still pushes); the agent degrades to "branch pushed, open PR manually". (c) **Caching note (perf rule):** the host `GET /dispatch/:dispatchId`, the tenant `GET /api/agent-runtime/:dispatchId`, and the git-proxy reads are deliberately NOT run through `getOrSetCached` ŌĆö git smart-HTTP is dynamic; the dispatch reads are live status (flip pendingŌåÆrunningŌåÆcompleted mid-execution) and the credential read resolves a decrypted token (caching a token in KV is a security non-starter), one-shot per dispatch ŌĆö so there is no read-amplification to cache; the repo *metadata* portion could be cached keyed by repoId if it ever becomes hot.

- **Per-agent capabilities are stored & editable but not yet consumed at execution time.** [resolveArtifacts](api/src/application/artifact/resolveArtifacts.ts) accepts an optional `agentAssignmentId` (and `/api/artifact-assignments/resolve?agentId=` is wired), but no runtime/dispatch caller maps a running execution back to a `project_agents.id`, so `scope='agent'` skills/personas/content do not yet flow into agent runs. Fixing (thread the project-agent id through the swimlane/agent-runtime dispatch path into `resolveArtifacts`) unblocks: per-agent skills/personas actually shaping that agent's behaviour, not just being editable in the UI.
