  the first draft is written (the header invites updates but there's no `prd_update` flow appending a signed
  section + re-commit); (2) agents can't update the ticket description/status via a tool (no agent-facing
  task-mutation tool / agent-user identity); (3) the assigned agent isn't rendered as a name/AgentChip on the
  card (the `assigned_agent_ref` id reaches the frontend but isn't resolved to the agent's name/avatar);
  (4) Auto/default runs have no `cloudAgentRef`, so no agent identity to assign. Fixing unblocks: collaborative,
  attributed PRD authoring + agents visibly owning and editing their tickets.

- **`commitFileToRepo`/`commitPrdToRepo`/`createPullRequest` are GitHub-only.** Bitbucket/GitLab return a typed
  `unsupported` result, so the PRD-as-pending-change + PR flow only lands on GitHub repos; other providers keep
  the PRD in the DB (PRD tab) with no branch. Fixing (implement the branch+commit+PR REST calls per provider)
  unblocks: the git pending-change flow on non-GitHub repos.

- **The AnthropicŌćäOpenAI streaming translation needs live validation against the Claude Agent SDK.** The bridge's
  `createAnthropicStreamEncoder`/`pipeOpenAiSseToAnthropic` map OpenAI SSE deltas ŌåÆ Anthropic Messages events
  (text + tool_use), unit-tested for the common sequences ŌĆö but interleaved/parallel tool-call streaming and
  partial-JSON edge cases haven't been exercised by a real SDK run (no live model available here). Fixing
  (run the V2 SDK against `/llm/v1/messages` and reconcile any tool_use streaming gaps) unblocks: confidence the
  default (no-BYO-key) V2 path drives the agent loop correctly.

- **Live execution stream is per-isolate; assistant-text deltas aren't pushed mid-run.** The
  `/executions/:id/stream` WS subscriber map ([runtimeRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts))
  lives in one Worker isolate, and self-hosted mid-run frames arrive at the relay DO (a different object), so
  assistant token deltas don't reach the execution panel live ŌĆö the [AgentExecutionPanel](frontend/src/components/agent/AgentExecutionPanel.tsx)
  now re-polls the `trace` every 4s while running to surface live tool-calls/file-changes (Changes/Tools),
  but the Output thread only fills from the terminal result or the cloud path's single assistant event.
  Fixing (host execution streaming in a Durable Object, or have the relay DO forward `chat.message` deltas to
  an execution-events channel) unblocks: true token-streaming Output for self-hosted runs.

- **The per-execution `trace` endpoint returns the empty fallback for panel-submitted runs ŌĆö `execution.sessionId`
  is never linked to the agent's `"main"` session.** [RunAgentControl](frontend/src/components/task/RunAgentControl.tsx)
  submits with no `sessionId`, so [RuntimeService.submit](api/src/application/runtime/RuntimeService.ts) stores
  `sessionId: null`, but the agent always runs/persists telemetry under sessionKey `"main"`
  ([builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts) runV1/runV2/steering + the V2 sinks).
  The [`/executions/:id/trace`](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts) handler guards on `!plain.sessionId`
  and returns `{usageSnapshots:[], toolEvents:[]}`, and even past the guard it joins
  `toolAuditEvents.sessionKey === execution.sessionId` ŌĆö so the Agent Tab's **Tools** sub-tab (and any
  per-execution usage/output read) is always empty for self-hosted runs, despite the agent persisting the data
  under `"main"` (which is why the per-agentHost **Observability** page, which does NOT filter by session, shows it
  fine). This contradicts the entry above (the 4s trace re-poll surfaces *file-changes* via the separate taskId-keyed
  `taskFileChanges`, not tool-calls). Fixing (thread a per-execution `sessionId` ŌĆö e.g. `exec-<id>` ŌĆö through the
  dispatch contract ŌåÆ agent-runtime sessionKey + telemetry sinks + steering injection, then drop the `!sessionId`
  fallback; OR map `execution.sessionId` to the agent's session at submit) unblocks: correct per-execution Tools /
  usage / output in the ticket panel, and removes cross-execution telemetry bleed when an agentHost runs more than
  one task in session `"main"`. NOTE this pass shipped the minimal Agent-Tab fixes only: the steering directive now
  renders optimistically (the per-isolate stream echo was being dropped) and the panel links out to Observability
  for full diagnostics ŌĆö by design the ticket tab stays minimal and the full firehose lives on Observability.

- **Content artifacts have no body store ŌĆö only the slug is injectable, on both cloud and on-prem.** The 2026-06-07 capability pass wired assigned Skills/Personas/Content into the cloud system prompt ([capabilityContext.ts](api/src/application/artifact/capabilityContext.ts) ŌåÆ [runCloudExecution](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts#L765)) and on-prem (V1 persona via [assigned-capabilities.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts) ŌåÆ `buildEmbeddedSystemPrompt` `personaPrompt`; V2 via the SDK prompt preamble), with a `capabilities.load` event on the Observability timeline both for cloud ([recordCloudToolEvent](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)) and on-prem ([builderforce-relay `syncAssignedCapabilities`](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts)). **Residual:** `artifact_type = 'content'` has no backing table ŌĆö `marketplace_skills` / `platform_personas` exist but there is no `marketplace_content`, and the marketplace purchase path already notes "personas/content default to 0 for now" ([marketplaceRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/marketplaceRoutes.ts)). So both paths can only inject the assigned content *slugs* as references ("Assigned content references: ŌĆ”"), not the actual document bodies. Fixing (add a `marketplace_content` table with a `body`/`markdown` column + publish/CRUD routes, then fetch + inject bodies in `loadCapabilityContext` and read them on-prem in `buildAssignedCapabilityAppend`) unblocks: content artifacts that actually carry their text into the agent's context instead of a bare slug reference.

- **On-prem V2 (Claude Agent SDK) injects assigned skills as slug references only ŌĆö not full SKILL.md bodies like V1.** The V1 pi-embedded path builds the rich `<available_skills>` block via `resolveSkillsPromptForRun` ([attempt.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/pi-embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts)), but the V2 capability preamble ([buildAssignedCapabilityAppend](agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts)) only lists the assigned skill slugs and tells the SDK agent to read the matching SKILL.md if present in the workspace (cwd is the ticket repo, not the agent's managed skills dir). Personas (full definition) and content refs are at parity; skills are not. Fixing (resolve the workspace/managed skill entries for the V2 cwd and inject the same formatted skills prompt V1 uses, or sync the assigned SKILL.md files into the ticket workspace) unblocks: V2 agents getting full skill instructions, not just names.

- **High-risk built-in tools still don't auto-gate through `ask_human` ŌĆö escalation is opt-in by the model.** This pass shipped the model-facing [askHumanTool](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/tools/ask-human-tool.ts) (registered in [builderforce-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforce-tools.ts)) so the LLM can *choose* to bubble up an approval/question/feedback and block on the human via the shared [approvalGate](agent-runtime/src/infra/approval-gate.ts). **Residual:** no destructive built-in tool *forces* the gate ŌĆö [bash-tools.exec](agent-runtime/src/agents/bash-tools.exec.ts) git-push / `rm` / file-delete branches still run without calling `requestApproval`, so a model that doesn't think to call `ask_human` can still take an irreversible action unprompted. Fixing (wire `approvalGate.request({kind:'approval'})` into the destructive branches of the exec/file tools behind a policy flag, defaulting on for `git push`/delete/spend/external-send) unblocks: enforced human-in-the-loop on dangerous actions, not just model-discretion escalation.

- **PM visualizers shipped + hardened (Planning tab + roadmap embed + standalone embeds).** Migration [0121](api/migrations/0121_pm_visualizers.sql) added nullable `project_id` to `roadmap_items`/`feature_scores` + the `task_dependencies` DAG table; the tracker factory ([segmentTrackerRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/segmentTrackerRoutes.ts)) gained `projectScoped`+`cacheNs`+`bumpVersionKeys`; dependency routes (write-time cycle gate + post-insert compensating delete, [taskDependencies.ts](api/src/application/task/taskDependencies.ts)) + cached epic-tree + composed ROI rollup ([roiRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/roiRoutes.ts)); frontend `PmVisualizersContent` (Epics tree/flow, Roadmap timeline/gantt/map, ROI) under [`/projects?tab=pm`](frontend/src/app/projects/page.tsx), the `roadmap` embed, and standalone `dependency-graph`/`rice-matrix`/`roi-dashboard` embeds. **Closed in the gap-closing pass:** cycle time uses the board-agnostic createdŌåÆcompleted definition shared with the workforce scorecards/DORA; per-task agent-LLM spend now surfaces in the ROI rollup (`byTask`); the ROI cache uses a 60s TTL so hot-path LLM spend stays fresh while structural writes (task status / sprint / cost / feature-roi) invalidate immediately; the check-then-insert cycle race is closed by a post-insert re-verify + compensating delete (neon-http has no advisory locks); `dep_type` (FS/SS/FF/SF) is now user-selectable + labelled on edges; roadmap CRUD (create/edit/delete) lives in a shared `RoadmapItemPanel` used by both the timeline and the Gantt (a Gantt bar click now opens the editor); the standalone embed surfaces are registered + rendered; the `project_id`-on-sprints/cost/feature-roi item was retired as a non-defect (a sprint legitimately spans projects, the cost model + feature-roi are segment concepts, and project sprint-spend is correctly derived via `tasks.sprint_id`). **Remaining genuine future work:** (1) **Human-labor / time cost** ŌĆö ROI's `$ spent` covers agent LLM cost (per task + per project) + sprint burn + the segment cost model, but there is still no human-effort/time-tracking dimension (needs a time-tracking feature, not just a column). (2) **`dep_type` is metadata only** ŌĆö SS/FF/SF are stored + displayed but no scheduling engine consumes them to shift bars (the roadmap Gantt is roadmap-item-based, not task-dependency-based); a task-dependency-driven Gantt that honours the relation types is the follow-on. (3) **ROI has no materialized view** ŌĆö the rollup recomputes live behind the 60s cache; revisit only if a very large portfolio makes the live aggregate slow.

- **#1994 server backend SHIPPED ŌĆö `/api/studio/voice-clones/*` is live, metered, cached, consent-gated.** Built the full route family ([studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts), mounted in [index.ts](api/src/index.ts)): create (Pro-gated via new `checkProFeature` on [planLimitsGuard.ts](api/src/presentation/middleware/planLimitsGuard.ts) + consent attestation + R2 reference upload), cached list/marketplace (version-token read-through), `POST /:id/synthesize`, R2 audio stream, delete (R2 purge + cache bump). Schema: `studio_voice_clones` / `studio_voice_clone_licenses` / `studio_voiceovers` + 2 enums ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)), migration [0127](api/migrations/0127_studio_voice_clones.sql). The synthesis spine ([voiceCloneService.ts](api/src/application/studio/voiceCloneService.ts)) enforces owner-or-license access + consent + provider gates, serves through a read-through cache whose persistent tier is the unique-keyed `studio_voiceovers` row (sha256(cloneId+text+speed+lang) ŌĆö identical re-synth is free, no re-bill), stores audio to R2, and meters per-second cost to `llm_usage_log` (`voice_clone_synthesis`). The bytes-returning provider adapter ([ttsProvider.ts](api/src/application/studio/ttsProvider.ts), separate from the string-only llm-client per PRD ┬¦3.1) is config-driven (`VOICE_CLONE_TTS_URL`/`_KEY`); unconfigured ŌåÆ honest 503, never fake audio. 12 backend tests green, API type-checks 0 errors. The npm `ServerCloneProvider` already targets this exact route. **Residual (migration not applied):** 0127 is additive/idempotent but per project convention NOT auto-run against the operator's Neon DB ŌĆö `npm --prefix api run db:migrate` before the routes can persist. **Residual (TTS provider):** synthesis returns 503 until `VOICE_CLONE_TTS_URL` is provisioned (a trained in-house model server or a vendor); this is the deliberate Option-B seam ŌĆö wiring it makes cloning audible on every device.

- **Voice residuals after this pass:** (1) **Trained weights** ŌĆö the studio encoder/codec/acoustic models are deterministic seeded *reference* impls (correct shapes/conditioning/streaming, placeholder weights ŌåÆ acoustic texture, not intelligible speech); intelligibility needs the Phase 2 training run, dropping trained matrices behind the identical interfaces. (2) **Marketplace checkout/license purchase** ŌĆö `studio_voice_clone_licenses` + the access check exist and are honored, but there is NO buy/checkout route that CREATES a license (95/5 split, CC-on-buyer per PRD ┬¦6); listing a clone as `marketplace` works, purchasing one does not. (3) **Provenance/moderation (┬¦5 GA gate)** ŌĆö consent attestation is enforced on create, but provenance disclosure on listings, the moderation gate on publish, and an audio watermark are not built. (4) **G2P + WGSL** ŌĆö char-level tokenizer (no phonemizer) and CPU SSM scan (no WebGPU Mamba kernel). (5) **LLM-flow wiring (#1995/#1997)** ŌĆö scriptŌåÆnarration / dubbing / pitch surfaces don't yet route their text through the narration seam (those studio UIs aren't in the repo).

- **Voice-clone foundation (Phase 1 + 2) shipped into `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio`; trained weights + the server synthesize route are the open seams.** Built the in-browser, weight-free, device-routed clone stack under [studio/src/engine/voice](studio/src/engine/voice): Phase 1 ŌĆö shared DSP ([audio-frames.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/audio-frames.ts): FFT, mel filterbank, melŌåÆPCM vocoder), the x-vector-style [speaker-encoder.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/speaker-encoder.ts) (stats-pooled identity embedding), and the RVQ [neural-codec.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/neural-codec.ts) (PCMŌåödiscrete tokens); Phase 2 ŌĆö the SSM [ssm-acoustic-model.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/ssm-acoustic-model.ts) ((text+speaker)ŌåÆcodec tokens on the same `h_{t+1}=A┬Ęh_t+B┬Ęx_t` recurrence as [mamba-coherence.ts](studio/src/engine/mamba-coherence.ts), Cartesia's SSM-over-codec bet), the [voice-clone-engine.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/voice-clone-engine.ts) orchestrator (device-routed via the shared `probeDevice`), and the swappable [provider.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/provider.ts) seam. 28 voice tests green; studio builds ESM/CJS/DTS. **#1994 (server synthesize): NOW SHIPPED** ŌĆö `POST /api/studio/voice-clones/:id/synthesize` + the `studio_voice_clones`/`studio_voice_clone_licenses`/`studio_voiceovers` tables + the full route family exist (see the "#1994 server backend SHIPPED" entry above; migration 0127). **Residual (weights):** the encoder/codec/acoustic models are deterministic seeded *reference* implementations ŌĆö correct shapes, conditioning, and streaming recurrence, but **placeholder weights**, so output is structured voice-/text-dependent acoustic texture, not intelligible speech. Intelligibility needs the Phase 2 *training* run (codec + speaker encoder + SSM acoustic model on a licensed multi-speaker corpus); trained matrices drop in behind the identical interfaces (`NeuralCodecOptions.codebooks`, `AcousticWeights`). **Residual (G2P):** [text-tokenizer.ts](studio/src/engine/voice/text-tokenizer.ts) is char-level; a graphemeŌåÆphoneme front-end drops in behind `tokenizeText` without touching the acoustic model. **Residual (WGSL):** the SSM scan runs on the CPU Float32 fallback; the WebGPU Mamba kernel (same gap as the diffusion-coherence WGSL kernel above) makes the on-device path fast. Fixing #1994 is the highest-leverage next step ŌĆö it makes the marketing claim true on every device.

- **`@seanhogg/builderforce-voice` npm package shipped (client seam); it is the consumer contract for hired.video, ahead of the server it calls.** New publishable package at [voice/](voice) (tsup dual ESM/CJS, 13 tests green): `resolveNarrationEngine()` / `VoiceClient` pick the on-device clone (free, WebGPU) ŌåÆ metered server (`ServerCloneProvider`) ŌåÆ honest named-voice fallback, with `getEngineUnavailableReason` as the single source of truth for the "can I clone now" UI (PRD ┬¦4 + ┬¦7). The on-device path is structurally typed against the studio engine so `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio` stays an optional peer. **Residual:** the `ServerCloneProvider` calls the #1994 endpoint that doesn't exist yet, so only the on-device and fallback paths run end-to-end today; and the four LLM creation flows (scriptŌåÆnarration, dubbing panel, value-prop/pitch, calibration read-script ŌĆö PRD ┬¦4 #1995/#1997) are **not yet wired** to route their generated text through this seam (those studio UI surfaces aren't in the repo). Wiring them once the studio UI + #1994 land unblocks "the AI wrote it and it speaks in my voice" across every studio format.

- **Agent-execution telemetry now has unit coverage on the discrete WRITERS, but the full-LOOP wiring is still integration-only (2026-06-14).** Added [`cloudTelemetry.test.ts`](api/src/application/runtime/cloudTelemetry.test.ts) (8 tests ŌĆö drives the real `recordCloudToolEvent`/`recordCloudUsage`/`emitModelSelection`/`emitCodingModelDegraded` against a fake `Db`, asserting `tool_audit_events` rows are keyed `exec:<id>` with cloud attribution, that usage dual-writes `usage_snapshots` AND `llm_usage_log` with the `engine:'cloud'` marker + ticket/project rollup, and that each writer is best-effort/never-throws) and [`workflow-telemetry.test.ts`](agent-runtime/src/infra/workflow-telemetry.test.ts) (9 tests ŌĆö on-prem `WorkflowTelemetryService` populates all three sinks per span: the day's JSONL audit file, the Builderforce workflow/task REST + OTel `/api/telemetry/spans` HTTP sync with `Authorization`/`X-AgentHost-Id`/`X-Trace-Id` headers, and the live relay hook; covers task token/cost metrics, the `task.fail` path, trace-id lifecycle, local-only no-sync, and throw-isolation). To make the cloud writers testable, three module-private helpers in `cloudAgentEngine.ts` were `export`ed (no behavior change). **Boundary / defensive coverage ADDED 2026-06-14:** `cloudTelemetry.test.ts` (+6) injects wrong/hostile values and proves the best-effort contract ŌĆö a circular `detail` (JSON.stringify throws) records nothing but never throws, a dead `Db` on BOTH usage ledgers never throws, an unknown plan + blank model still emits a planning row, and `emitCodingModelDegraded` is a strict no-op for junk/sentinel models (no false alarm); [`cloudDispatch.test.ts`](api/src/application/runtime/cloudDispatch.test.ts) (+6) feeds every untrusted-payload reader (`parseModel`/`parseCloudAgentRef`/`parseRepoId`/`parseRemediation`/`markReaperRequeued`/`wasReaperRequeued`/`withDefaultModel`) non-JSON garbage + `'null'` (the `JSON.parse('null')===null` sharp edge) + wrong-type values, asserting safe defaults (undefined/null/unchanged) over a throw; `workflow-telemetry.test.ts` (+4) proves a non-numeric `agentNodeId` skips the numeric OTel proxy but still REST-syncs, a rejecting `fetch` never blocks the JSONL audit, and an invalid `startedAt` (NaN duration ŌåÆ JSON `null`) still records. **DATA-QUALITY GAP ŌĆö Ō£ģ FIXED 2026-06-14:** bad token counts can no longer reach the billing ledger. - **Unified Agent Engine ŌĆö engine seam CONVERGED (Phase A done 2026-06-14); tool-layer reuse REDESIGNED after a hardening-superset finding.** Validation of the Agent Engine seam (PRD [12](specs/builderforce/12-prd-unified-agent-engine.md)) found three *separate* loops: (1) **cloud** `CloudToolLoopEngine`/`runCloudToolLoop` consumes the shared `@builderforce/agent-tools` registry via `CapabilityProvider`; (2) **on-prem TASK** (`runV2Engine`ŌåÆ`claude-agent-sdk-runner.ts`) ran the Claude SDK's own 6 built-ins inline; (3) **on-prem SESSION** (`embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts`) runs ~40 native `AgentTool`s. **DONE this pass (Phase A):** on-prem now implements the SAME shared `AgentEngine` contract cloud does ŌĆö new [`infra/sdk-agent-engine.ts`](agent-runtime/src/infra/sdk-agent-engine.ts) `ClaudeSdkAgentEngine` wraps the SDK runner and `runV2Engine` drives it via `run(input)ŌåÆAgentRunResult`; a V3 is now a sibling `AgentEngine` (mirrors cloud `resolveAgentEngine`). `tsgo` 0; 3 unit tests + 826 infra tests green (the lone `gateway-lock.test.ts` failure is a pre-existing env/lock collision, unrelated). No tool-layer/TUI change. **CRITICAL FINDING (rescopes the tool work):** the on-prem native session tools ([`agents/coding-tools.ts`](agent-runtime/src/agents/coding-tools.ts)) are NOT duplicates of the thin shared `core-tools` ŌĆö they carry sandbox variants, workspace guards, per-provider schema normalization, model-context-scaled read budgets, image sanitization, `apply_patch`, background-process mgmt, owner-only/subagent policy pipelines, before-tool-call hooks, and abort wrapping. The original Phase B ("delete native defs, use the shared registry") would REGRESS that hardening. **Phase D DONE (2026-06-14):** shared `resolveEngineById(registry,id,default?)` in `@builderforce/agent-tools` engine.ts; BOTH seams use it ŌĆö relay `resolveEngine` AND cloud `resolveAgentEngine` (now an id-keyed factory registry) ŌĆö so a V3 is one registry entry on either surface, via the same helper. `agent-runtime` tsgo 0 + `api` tsc 0; 4 resolver tests green. (The `toolsFor`/`toolsForCapabilities` "drift" was actually thin already-DRY delegations ŌĆö not collapsed.) **Prereq resolutions (2026-06-14):** gating = capability (machine) vs policy (caller) are ORTHOGONAL layers, keep both ŌĆö encoded in `capabilities.ts` (not a blocker); streaming `ctx.onUpdate?` DEFERRED (no consumer until exec/process converge). **NEW gap:** shared `RepoReadCapability.readFile` is text-only ŌåÆ converging `read_file` would lose native image-reading; the read capability needs a media affordance first (read stays native until then). **Phase B tool-CONTRACT convergence LANDED for the file subset (2026-06-14, operator "close the blocker").** Built [`buildNodeCapabilityProvider`](agent-runtime/src/agents/node-capability-provider.ts) (disk twin of cloud `buildCloudProvider`: guarded list/read/`runCodebaseSearch` + mkdir-p write / BOM-CRLF-tolerant unique edit / no-op-on-missing delete, every path workspace-root-guarded) and gave [`registryToAgentTools`](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/agent-loop/tool-adapter.ts) a PRODUCTION caller via [`buildConvergedFileTools`](agent-runtime/src/agents/converged-coding-tools.ts) ŌĆö shared `write_file`/`edit_file` exposed under the NATIVE names `write`/`edit` (model-facing contract + `tool-display.json` keys unchanged), plus additive `delete_file`/`list_files`. Wired into `createBuilderForceAgentsCodingTools` behind config opt-in `tools.fs.convergedFileTools` (default OFF, NON-sandboxed only), folded in BEFORE the existing normalize/hook/abort/policy pipeline so the hardening is preserved. `tsgo` 0, `oxlint` 0, 25 tests green; default path byte-unchanged. **REMAINING (live gate now a flag flip, not a code blocker):** (1) an owner-run cross-provider smoke test (Anthropic-OAuth/OpenAI/Gemini) that the model drives the converged tools as well as native, then flip `tools.fs.convergedFileTools` ON by default; (2) a sandbox-aware Node provider (fs-bridge backed) so sandboxed sessions converge too; (3) converge `read` (needs a shared read-capability media affordance ŌĆö text-only today, would lose native image-reading) + `exec`/`process` (needs streaming `ctx.onUpdate?`); (4) `search_code` left native (the on-prem `codebase_search` would otherwise double); Phase C ŌĆö drive the SDK task runner's tools through the shared registry. Full plan: [PRD 12](specs/builderforce/12-prd-unified-agent-engine.md) ┬¦5/┬¦9. Fixing unblocks one drop-in V3 engine + one tool definition per tool on every surface. Flow diagram + end-to-end/divergence assessment: [12a](specs/builderforce/12a-unified-agent-engine-flow.md).

- **Converged on-prem `write`/`edit` narrow file scope to the workspace root (vs native's opt-in guard) ŌĆö verify before the default-on flip.** Surfaced by the [12a flow assessment](specs/builderforce/12a-unified-agent-engine-flow.md) ┬¦3.3: the shared `write_file`/`edit_file` contract is repo/workspace-relative by design, so [`buildNodeCapabilityProvider`](agent-runtime/src/agents/node-capability-provider.ts) unconditionally rejects out-of-workspace paths, whereas native `write`/`edit` allow absolute paths outside the root unless `tools.fs.workspaceOnly` is set. A non-sandboxed session that today writes outside its workspace (legacy `workspaceOnly=false`) loses that once `tools.fs.convergedFileTools` is enabled ŌĆö a (safer) behavior NARROWING, not a break. Fixing/confirming (decide whether the converged provider should honor a non-guarded mode when `workspaceOnly=false`, or keep always-guarded as the intended hardening) unblocks: a clean default-on flip with no surprise scope regression for out-of-workspace writers.

- **Engine consolidation: retire V1 entirely, collapse to one surface-agnostic V2 engine with FULL capability parity on every surface (local / container / durable) ŌĆö no reduced tool set anywhere (operator decision, 2026-06-13).** Today three divergent tool sets encode the same branching in three places ŌĆö `CLOUD_AGENT_TOOLS` (7), `CONTAINER_AGENT_TOOLS` (8), and the local `pi-coding-agent` set (~40 tools) in [agent-runtime/src/agents/pi-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/pi-tools.ts)+[builderforce-tools.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/builderforce-tools.ts) ŌĆö and On-Prem (Hosted) still runs the legacy V1 pi loop ([builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts) `runV1Engine`) instead of V2. V1 has **no remaining unique capability**: the V2 cloud loop already drives the vendor-neutral `CODING_MODEL_POOL` via the OpenAI-shaped `proxy.complete()` and needs no tenant Anthropic key (the "V2 requires BYO key" premise is false ŌĆö see [anthropicMessagesBridge.ts](api/src/application/llm/anthropicMessagesBridge.ts)). The work: **(1) CapabilityProvider refactor ŌĆö Ō£ģ SHIPPED 2026-06-13 (keystone).** The three divergent tool lists AND the ~160-line per-tool dispatch `if/else` in `runCloudToolLoop` are replaced by ONE capability-gated registry. A new runtime-agnostic shared package [`@builderforce/agent-tools`](packages/agent-tools/) (no `node:*`, no Worker `Env`, no `pi-agent-core` ŌĆö bundles under both `moduleResolution: bundler` and `NodeNext`) defines the contract: `ToolDefinition` (OpenAI schema + `requires: Capability[]` + `execute(args, ctx)`), the `Capability` set (`repo.read`/`repo.search`/`repo.write`/`repo.delete`/`shell`/`process`/`static-check`/`human`/`memory`/`web`/`orchestrate`/`message`/`media`), `CapabilityProvider` (the surface's service bag), `ToolRegistry` (filters tools per surface BY capability ŌĆö `CLOUD_AGENT_TOOLS`/`CONTAINER_AGENT_TOOLS` are now DERIVED and byte-stable, not hand-maintained), the `AgentEngine` DI seam, and the 9 core tool DEFINITIONS ([core-tools.ts](packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts)) so the SAME objects run on every surface. `api` consumes it: [cloudAgentTools.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentTools.ts) is now just the two cloud capability SETS + derived schema arrays + step budgets; [cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts) adds `buildCloudProvider` (git-API repo read/write/delete + shell-free static-check + approvals-queue human, owning the write/delete bookkeeping) and dispatches via `cloudToolRegistry.dispatch`, with `CloudToolLoopEngine`/`resolveAgentEngine` the injectable engine seam wired at `runCloudExecution` (the finish honesty + anti-stub gates and the ask_human pause stay loop policy, fed by tool `control` signals). `agent-runtime` ALSO consumes it: [buildNodeCapabilityProvider](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/node-capability-provider.ts) (disk + REAL shell, path-escape-guarded) + a [pi-tool adapter](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/pi-tool-adapter.ts) run the same cloud tool definitions on-prem ŌĆö proven by [pi-tool-adapter.test.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/shared-tools/pi-tool-adapter.test.ts) (write/read/list via disk; run_command via shell; capability gating; root-escape block). Both packages type-check; api type-check + 682 tests green + wrangler `--dry-run` bundle resolves the alias; agent-runtime type-check + the cross-runtime test green. Wiring: tsconfig `paths` in both consumers (tsc + esbuild) plus a vitest resolve-alias in each (vitest ignores tsconfig paths). **Residual tail of (1):** 12 tools are shared `ToolDefinition`s now (the original 9 + `edit_file`/`web_fetch`/`web_search` added 2026-06-13 ŌĆö full per-tool classification in the dedicated catalogue-completion entry below); - **Cloudflare account API token was leaked to chat transcript on 2026-05-23.** A real `cfut_*` Workers AI token was pasted as part of a curl example and is now in conversation history (cacheable / loggable on any party that handled the message). The key was never committed to the repo (read from `env.CLOUDFLARE_AI_API_TOKEN` set via `wrangler secret put`), but the leaked token still grants Workers AI quota until rotated on the Cloudflare dashboard (My Profile ŌåÆ API Tokens ŌåÆ roll the existing token). Fixing (rotate the token in the Cloudflare dashboard and `npm run secrets:from-env` after updating `api/.env`) unblocks: confidence that the leaked credential is dead. Mirrors the existing NVIDIA-API-key-leak entry from 2026-05-10 ŌĆö same playbook.

- **72 React-hooks ergonomics warnings demoted from error to warn.** [frontend/eslint.config.js](frontend/eslint.config.js) downgrades `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect`, `react-hooks/refs`, `react-hooks/purity`, `react-hooks/immutability`, and `react-hooks/preserve-manual-memoization` because `eslint-plugin-react-hooks` v6 + the React Compiler plugin started flagging dozens of legitimate pre-existing patterns (fetch-on-mount, ref-mirror, manual `useCallback`) as errors and broke the deploy. Patterns themselves are not bugs ŌĆö ergonomics suggestions. Fixing (refactor each warning to the React-Compiler-blessed shape, then re-promote to error) unblocks: catching genuinely-unsafe state mutations during review.

- **`eslint-config-next` is a major version ahead of `next` (16.1.6 vs 15.5.2) ŌĆö the root cause of the React-Compiler hook-rule wall above.** [frontend/package.json](frontend/package.json) pins `eslint-config-next@16.1.6` against `next@15.5.2`; the v16 config is what enables the React-Compiler-era `react-hooks` rules. The ergonomics rules are demoted to `warn` in [frontend/eslint.config.js](frontend/eslint.config.js), but `react-hooks/rules-of-hooks` correctly stays at error ŌĆö and that stricter ruleset broke the deploy build a second time via a *false positive*: a plain async event handler named `usePrompt` in [frontend/src/app/prompts/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/prompts/page.tsx) was misclassified as a Hook purely because of its `use` prefix and flagged for being called inside a callback (fixed this pass by renaming to `applyPrompt`). Until the versions are aligned, every future `use`-prefixed non-hook helper will re-trip the same error-level break. Fixing (pin `eslint-config-next` to `15.x` to match `next@15.5.2`, OR deliberately upgrade `next` to 16 and budget the hook-rule refactor) unblocks: a lint ruleset that matches the framework version, and no more naming-driven false-positive build breaks.

- **`requireTenantAccess` unit test uses a hand-rolled Drizzle chain mock.** [api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.test.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.test.ts) `mockDb()` synthesizes `select().from().where().limit()` chains with canned `[row]` returns. If the auth path grows another link (e.g. `.orderBy`, `.innerJoin`), the mock returns `undefined` and the test still passes while production breaks. Fixing (shared test helper or a real in-memory pg) unblocks: confidence that gateway-auth refactors are caught by tests, not prod.

- **RepoŌåÆIDE import is a one-way snapshot capped at 200 files / 5MB, and never clears stale workspace files first.** This pass added "Import to IDE" ([SourceControlContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/sourcecontrol/SourceControlContent.tsx) ŌåÆ `GET /api/repos/repositories/:id/contents`, [importRepoContents.ts](api/src/application/repos/importRepoContents.ts)) so a connected repo hydrates the editable workspace and runs in WebContainer. **Residuals:** (1) caps ŌĆö a repo with >200 importable files or >5MB of text is partially imported (skips surfaced in the UI as "imported N of M"); full import needs pagination/streaming or the GitHub tarball endpoint. (2) Import **overlays** the existing workspace via `saveFile` without first clearing it, so files from a prior template/import that no longer exist in the repo linger as stale entries. (3) It's **one-way** ŌĆö there's no "commit IDE edits back to the connected repo" action from the IDE; write-back still relies on the taskŌåÆPR flow ([openTaskPullRequest.ts](api/src/application/repos/openTaskPullRequest.ts)). (4) ~~GitHub-only~~ **RESOLVED 2026-06-13:** `readRepoFile`/`listRepoFiles` (and therefore the import) now route GitLab/Bitbucket through the shared, tested `RepoSource` (GitHub keeps its inline path ŌåÆ no-regression; +unit tests) ŌĆö only `searchRepoCode`/`compare` remain GitHub-only (no cross-provider equivalent yet). Fixing the rest unblocks: full-repo, two-way IDE workspaces (caps + overlay-clear + write-back remain).

- **The durable cloud Worker executor can statically validate config but still can't run the project build/type-check/tests in-run (no shell).** `runCloudToolLoop` now has `search_code` (indexed GitHub code search ŌĆö closed the "blind file-by-file exploration ŌåÆ band-aid edit" failure of exec #52), routes through the curated coding pool, and `run_checks` is now a REAL static validator ŌĆö it re-parses the agent's committed JSON/YAML config via [verifyWrittenFiles.ts](api/src/application/repos/verifyWrittenFiles.ts) (`JSON.parse` + the runtime `yaml` dep; zero false positives) and blocks a clean finish on a parse error. **Residual (inherent to the shell-less surface):** TS/JS type-checking needs the whole program + node_modules types and tests/build need a shell ŌĆö neither is possible in a Worker (the `typescript` dep is dev-only; bundling tsc would add ~1MB for *syntax-only* checking and a hand-rolled JS tokenizer would risk false positives that wrongly block agents). So full build/type/test verification stays with CI-on-PR + human review (and the existing webhook CIŌåÆauto-fix loop, [ingestRepoCiEvent.ts](api/src/application/ci/ingestRepoCiEvent.ts)). True in-run shell verification needs the long-lived **Container** surface (`run_command`, future infra) or routing V2 to the agent-runtime Claude Agent SDK loop with a sandbox. Fixing that unblocks: V2 cloud agents that type-check/test before shipping, not just config-validate. Related to the "Cloud agents wired but only happy-path validated" entry above.

- **Migration `0098_task_specs_and_spec_status.sql` not yet applied to any live DB.** The Product-Management PRD feature (taskŌåöPRD many-to-many via `task_specs`, destructive `spec_status` enum swap `reviewed/approvedŌåÆready`, `doneŌåÆcomplete`, and `DROP COLUMN tasks.spec_id`) is implemented, type-checks, and passes all 488 api tests + drift check, but the migration is a destructive enum swap + column drop and was deliberately NOT auto-run against the operator's Neon DB. Running it (`npm --prefix api run db:migrate` against the intended dev DB, then verify `\d+ specs` shows the new enum, `\d task_specs` exists, `tasks` has no `spec_id`, backfill count == prior `COUNT(*) WHERE spec_id IS NOT NULL`, then re-run for idempotency) unblocks: the whole feature going live. Note the partial unique index `uq_task_specs_primary ON task_specs(task_id) WHERE is_primary` is migration-only (the drift checker doesn't track partial indexes) ŌĆö confirm it exists post-apply.

- **Stub detection has a hard static-analysis ceiling: a byte-valid stub is indistinguishable from real code.** The anti-stub finish gate ([scanWrittenForPlaceholders](api/src/application/repos/scanForPlaceholders.ts), wired into `finish` in [cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)) now catches both the announced stubs (`// In a real ŌĆ”`, `assuming ŌĆ” exists`, `mock <noun>`, bracketed `[Platform Name]`, `replace with actual`) AND the silent structural ones (empty typed function body, `throw new Error('not implemented')`, `return null as Foo`, `// TODO`/`FIXME`, hard-coded `@example.com` / `your-api-key` literals) ŌĆö paired with the `delete_file` tool and the prior-branch-diff context so dead code is both detectable and removable. **Irreducible residual:** a stub that is *syntactically valid, comment-free, and returns a plausible hard-coded value* (e.g. `return "BuilderForce"` standing in for a real lookup, or a `return null;` that reads exactly like a legitimate guard) cannot be told apart from correct code by any static check without crossing into false positives ŌĆö that is a model-quality problem, not a detector gap, and it folds into the **"Routing pools are hand-maintained"** entry above (route coding tasks off the weak free-pool tail, e.g. `gemini-2.5-flash-lite`, so they aren't generated in the first place). No further detector work is warranted; closing it lives in model routing.

- **Standup/Planning round-table ceremony shipped (live multiplayer + Epic/sprint drag); five residuals.** This pass built a reusable [CeremonyStage](frontend/src/components/ceremony/CeremonyStage.tsx) (round table of human+agent seats; drag a backlog ticket onto a seat to assign, onto an Epic to group, onto the sprint bar to schedule, onto the center to mark Done) available both as a dedicated route ([/ceremonies](frontend/src/app/ceremonies/page.tsx) + sidebar nav) and a full-screen overlay from the Tasks board ([TaskMgmtContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) "Start standup/planning"). Live multiplayer via a new [CeremonyRoomDO](api/src/infrastructure/relay/CeremonyRoomDO.ts) (presence + cursor + `changed` relay, keyed `ceremony:<projectId>`, bound `CEREMONY_ROOM` / migration tag v7) and the [useCeremonyRoom](frontend/src/lib/ceremonyRoom.ts) hook. Full Epic support: PATCH/POST `/api/tasks` now accept `taskType`/`parentTaskId`/`sprintId` ([taskRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/taskRoutes.ts) ŌåÆ [TaskService](api/src/application/task/TaskService.ts) ŌåÆ [TaskRepository](api/src/infrastructure/repositories/TaskRepository.ts)), the taskŌåösprint link is migration [0115](api/migrations/0115_sprint_task_assignment.sql) (`tasks.sprint_id` FK, ON DELETE SET NULL), and the frontend [Task](frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts) type + `tasksApi.tree/decompose` + `sprintsApi` are exposed. The `broadcastRoom` helper was extracted to a [shared module](api/src/infrastructure/relay/broadcastRoom.ts) (DRY with poker/retro) and the assignee encode/decode helpers to [lib/taskAssignee.ts](frontend/src/lib/taskAssignee.ts). **Residuals:** (1) **Migration 0115 not yet applied to a live DB** ŌĆö schema-drift check + 646 api tests pass, but `tasks.sprint_id` must be added by running `npm --prefix api run db:migrate` against the dev DB (verify the column + `idx_tasks_sprint`, re-run for idempotency). (2) **Presence identity is self-reported** by the client's `join` frame ŌĆö the DO does not re-verify the JWT per frame (the WS upgrade itself is auth-gated under `/api/agile`); server-stamped identity is a follow-up. (3) **`changed` propagation is client-driven** ŌĆö broadcast on local-mutation success, so a peer who mutates while disconnected won't notify others; a server-authoritative broadcast from `taskRoutes` after PATCH would close this. (4) **Ceremonies are ephemeral** (room == project; no persisted standup/planning session history, no retro/poker integration). (5) **No DnD-library affordances** ŌĆö native HTML5 drag has no drop-preview ghost/keyboard a11y, and the seat in-flight stacks (standup) can overlap when many members ring a small table; a future pass could switch to dnd-kit or cap/auto-layout the ellipse. The task detail in the ceremony is a lightweight read-only panel that links back to the full board drawer (the board's rich `renderTaskCard`/drawer wasn't extracted ŌĆö see the related Epic-decomposition board-tree-UI residual). Fixing unblocks: governed, persistent ceremonies with server-trusted presence and a unified task card across board + table.

- **Ceremony tracking + scorecards + power meters shipped (Phase 2); reconciled with the parallel member-metrics effort.** Ceremonies are now *measured*: migration [0119](api/migrations/0119_ceremony_sessions.sql) (renamed from a colliding `0116` ŌĆö the parallel effort had already taken 0116/0117/0118) adds `ceremony_sessions` + `ceremony_participants` and board-level `standup_turn_mode`/`standup_turn_seconds`; [ceremonyRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ceremonyRoutes.ts) gains session CRUD (`GET /sessions`, `POST /sessions`, `PATCH /sessions/:id/turn`, `POST /sessions/:id/complete`, all MANAGER+). Each seat gained a **power meter** (load vs real `maxConcurrentWip` capacity ŌåÆ [ScorecardPanel](frontend/src/components/ceremony/ScorecardPanel.tsx) slide-out) and a **briefcase** (assigned-count + status dots ŌåÆ [AssignedWorkPanel](frontend/src/components/ceremony/AssignedWorkPanel.tsx)). **Reconciliation (important):** a parallel effort landed a fully-wired member-metrics system (`/api/members/metrics|profiles|dora`, `member_profiles`/`task_status_transitions`/`member_metrics_period`/`deployment_events`, `recordStatusTransition` in task PATCH); per that, the duplicate `computeScorecards`/`GET /scorecards` I first wrote was **deleted** and the ceremony UI now consumes `membersApi.metrics`/`profiles` (DRY). Two trivial parallel-WIP test breakages were fixed to keep the build green: `workforceMetrics.test.ts` null-guards, and a missing `runtimeApi.taskRepoStatus` spy in `AgentExecutionPanel.test.tsx` (their component added the fetch; their test didn't mock it). API 653 tests + frontend 218 tests pass. **Residuals:** (1) **Migrations 0115 + 0116ŌĆō0119 not yet applied to a live DB** ŌĆö schema-drift check passes; run `npm --prefix api run db:migrate` and verify the new tables/columns. (2) **Auto-dispatch on Complete is client-driven** (facilitator's browser submits the runs) ŌĆö a disconnect mid-Complete drops some runs; server-side dispatch from `POST /sessions/:id/complete` is the hardening follow-up. (3) **Scorecard cache is TTL-only** (the parallel `/api/members/metrics` cache); ceremony adds no write-invalidation. (4) **Turn timing is wall-clock from `turn_started_at`** ŌĆö no pause/resume; a tab closed mid-turn over-counts until the next advance/complete. (5) **Power-meter cap falls back to a soft constant (8)** when a member has no `member_profiles` row. (6) **Human/host specialization, success-rate, latency, rating** remain "No data yet" where the member-metrics system has no signal (cloud-agent-rich, human-sparse by design).

- **`orchestrate` tool's planning push is not task-linked ŌĆö tool-side plumbing DONE, but no `taskId` SOURCE in the session context.** [orchestrate-tool.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/tools/orchestrate-tool.ts) now accepts a `taskId` option and forwards it to `pushSpec` (links the PRD as the task's primary) [1277]. **Real remaining blocker (deeper than the original entry assumed):** the construction context has no taskId to pass ŌĆö `createBuilderForceAgentsTools`/`BuilderForceAgentsToolsOptions` carry agent-session fields but NO `taskId` (host-side `/spec` orchestration runs in a general agent session, not a per-task dispatch). Fixing that source-threading unblocks: host-side `/spec` PRDs landing as the task's primary.

- **Production gateway worker is running stale code (deploy artifact dated Mar 8) ŌĆö months behind `main`.** The on-disk bundle [api/.wrangler/tmp/deploy-rfNsY3/index.js](api/.wrangler/tmp/) predates the FREE-attempt cap, the Gemini premium fallback, and the current catalog. - **"Project integration keys" section has no edit / token-rotate UI.** This pass added repository edit (key-switch), a per-repo "Test" accessibility probe (`POST /api/repos/repositories/:id/test` via [resolveRepoCredential](api/src/application/repos/resolveRepoCredential.ts)), and edit/remove icons to [SourceControlContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/sourcecontrol/SourceControlContent.tsx); it also wired `credentialId` into the Brain `repos.add`/`repos.update` capabilities ([platformActions.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/platformActions.ts)) so a key switch is no longer silently dropped, and coerced `credentialId: '' ŌåÆ null` in the repo PATCH/POST so an empty selection clears the uuid FK instead of failing and "reverting". **Still missing:** [IntegrationCredentialsManager](frontend/src/components/integrations/IntegrationCredentialsManager.tsx) (the "Project integration keys" card) exposes only Test/Delete/Add ŌĆö no edit to rename a key or rotate its secret, even though `integrationsApi.update` + the backend `PATCH /api/integrations/:id` already support both. - **First-party server-side MCP server covers projects + tasks only ŌĆö other domains not yet wired.** A built-in MCP server now exposes platform capabilities in-process through the gateway ([api/src/application/llm/builtinMcpService.ts](api/src/application/llm/builtinMcpService.ts), merged into `GET /v1/mcp/tools` + dispatched in `POST /v1/mcp/call` under the `builtin` extension id in [llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)), so external/headless MCP clients and the agent-runtime can call platform actions, not just the browser Brain (which skips the `builtin` set via [McpExtensionsBridge](frontend/src/components/brain/McpExtensionsBridge.tsx) since it has the richer client manifest). **Full READ parity 2026-06-13:** `CATALOG` now exposes EVERY named domain server-side via tenant-scoped `ctx.db` queries ŌĆö projects, tasks (full CRUD via services), plus **workflows** (list/get), **specs/PRDs** (list/get), **prompts** (list), **approvals** (list), **agents** (list), **boards** (list), **cron** (list) [1296] (+unit test asserting all advertise). Deliberately NOT done as raw `ctx.db` writes ŌĆö those would bypass each domain's validation/business rules; doing it right means routing each write through that domain's service/repo with a tenant guard (extract a thin service where none exists). Read consumers (headless/cron discovery) have full parity now; write parity is the remaining per-domain service work.

- **No CI step runs `db:migrate` against an ephemeral DB before deploy ŌĆö missing-`CREATE` schema drift only surfaces in production.** This pass fixed a hard production-deploy crash (`relation "contributors" does not exist`) caused by the entire contributor/team/report/team-memory subsystem (schema sections 6bŌĆō6f) being defined in [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) and wired into routes ([analyticsRoutes](api/src/presentation/routes/analyticsRoutes.ts), [contributorRoutes](api/src/presentation/routes/contributorRoutes.ts), the P4-5 team-memory mesh) but never given a `CREATE TABLE` migration ŌĆö the tables only ever existed locally via `drizzle-kit push`. Migration 0056's `to_regclass()` guards silently no-op'd against the absent tables, masking the drift until 0069 ALTERed `contributors` unguarded. New migration [0068a_create_contributor_team_subsystem.sql](api/migrations/0068a_create_contributor_team_subsystem.sql) backfills the creates (idempotent, post-0056/pre-0069 shape, also creates the `activity_event_type`/`report_type`/`report_schedule` enums that were likewise never created). The remaining gap: the `db:migrate` job in [.github/workflows](.github/workflows) applies migrations straight to the production Neon branch with no prior dry-run, and [check-schema-drift.mjs](api/scripts/check-schema-drift.mjs) is not gated in CI to catch a schema-table that has no creating migration. Fixing (a CI job that spins a throwaway Neon branch or local Postgres, runs `db:migrate` from empty + then `check-schema-drift.mjs`, and fails the build on either error before the deploy job runs) unblocks: missing-migration / drift bugs caught in PR instead of as a prod deploy crash. NOTE: `team_memory` (the cross-claw mesh) was among the silently-uncreated tables, so that feature was non-functional in any push-free environment until 0068a.

- **The `pgTable`-block regex in [check-schema-drift.mjs](api/scripts/check-schema-drift.mjs) was merging adjacent tables ŌĆö now fixed, but exposed `claw_skill_assignments` as a push-only table.** The drift checker's table-capture regex (`...\n\}\)`) could not close a `}, (t) => [ ... ]` constraints block, so it ran past the closing brace and swallowed the *next* table's declaration under the first table's name ŌĆö fabricating ~96 phantom column entries in [.schema-drift-allowlist.txt](api/scripts/.schema-drift-allowlist.txt) (e.g. `dev_team_members.report_type`/`.delivery_hour`/`.recipients`, which are really `report_schedules` columns; `report_subscriptions.claw_id`/`.summary`, which are `team_memory` columns). This pass fixed the regex (`\n\}\s*[,)]` ŌĆö close on `}` followed by `)` or `,`) and rebuilt the allowlist down to the 110 genuinely-grandfathered push-only entries (parsed-table coverage rose to all 142). The fix un-hid [clawSkillAssignments](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) ŌĆö the claw-scoped sibling of `tenant_skill_assignments` ŌĆö which, like its sibling and the whole base cluster (`tenants`, `users`, `coderclaw_instances`, `marketplace_skills`, `projects`, `tasks`, `executions`), has **no `CREATE TABLE` migration** yet is queried unguarded at runtime ([skillAssignmentRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/skillAssignmentRoutes.ts), [clawRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/clawRoutes.ts)) ŌĆö the same `relation "X" does not exist` prod-crash class 0068a fixed for the contributor cluster. It was grandfathered (matching its sibling) rather than migrated, since converting it alone while leaving its push-only FK targets (`coderclaw_instances`, `marketplace_skills`) un-migrated would be inconsistent. Fixing (a `0073`-style idempotent `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` migration that converts the whole push-only baseline cluster ŌĆö base tables + both skill-assignment tables ŌĆö to tracked migrations, then dropping their allowlist entries) unblocks: skill assignment + base CRUD working in any push-free environment, and shrinking the grandfather list toward zero.

- **[ROUTABLE SIGNAL DONE 2026-06-13] `/models` catalog ŌĆö pricing-context + admin-invalidate residuals only.** Part (a) shipped [1305]: each `CatalogModel` is annotated `routable` + `pool: 'free'|'pro'` computed from the curated vendor catalog (`catalogEntry` in [modelCatalog.ts](api/src/application/llm/modelCatalog.ts), +unit test), and the Models page surfaces it as a "Ō£ō Routable" chip, a "Routable" field/column, and a "Routable only" filter ([ModelsPageClient.tsx](frontend/src/app/models/ModelsPageClient.tsx) + [modelCatalog.ts](frontend/src/lib/modelCatalog.ts)) ŌĆö a visitor now sees which models the cascade actually serves. **Residual:** (b) the per-1M pricing is still OpenRouter's verbatim point-in-time number with no effective-rate/markup context; (c) no admin "invalidate catalog cache" button (it ages out on the 1h KV TTL) ŌĆö a manual `invalidateCached(env, 'openrouter-catalog:v1')` action would force-refresh after an upstream pricing change.

- **`telemetry_spans` had no `CREATE TABLE` migration ŌĆö fixed in 0073; `agents` + `approval_rules` remain push-only.** Same drift class as 0068a (contributor cluster) and the `0073`-style note above: [telemetrySpans](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) was declared in schema.ts and queried unguarded by [GET /api/analytics/activity-calendar](api/src/presentation/routes/analyticsRoutes.ts), but only ever existed via the `drizzle-kit push` baseline ŌĆö no tracked migration created it, and 0056's `to_regclass()` guard silently no-op'd its `segment_id` block against the absent table. - **Native client apps were migrated into [apps/](apps/) as raw source but are not branded or CI-wired.** This pass consolidated the Android/iOS/macOS/shared clients (627 tracked files) out of the now-archived `SeanHogg/BuilderForceAgents` repo (the renamed-and-deprecated `coderClaw` repo) into [apps/](apps/), closing the "native apps have no home in Builderforce.ai" gap. **Still deferred:** (a) ~445 of those files still carry `coderclaw` branding, including the Android package namespace `ai.coderclaw.android` ([apps/android/app/build.gradle.kts](apps/android/app/build.gradle.kts), [AndroidManifest.xml](apps/android/app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml) and the whole `java/ai/coderclaw/android/**` tree), iOS/macos bundle ids, and in-app copy ŌĆö none rewritten to the BuilderForce brand; (b) the apps are standalone gradle/xcode projects with no entry in any Builderforce.ai build/CI pipeline (the repo has no root `pnpm-workspace.yaml`/`package.json`), so they are parked source that nothing builds, tests, or releases; (c) `apps/ios/fastlane/.env.example` had to be force-added past the root `.gitignore` `.env.*` rule ŌĆö fine for a template, but the fastlane signing/release flow it documents is not connected to any pipeline here. - **Agent API-key prefix migration `clk_`ŌåÆ`bfa_` is half-done (dual-accept live; legacy keys not yet rotated/dropped).** New BuilderForce Agents are now minted as `bfa_*` ([agentHostRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/agentHostRoutes.ts) `generateApiKey('bfa')`) and auth accepts BOTH `bfa_`/`clk_` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)), so no new credential carries the retired "claw" brand and existing `clk_` keys keep working. **Remaining:** (a) rotate already-issued `clk_*` keys to `bfa_*`, then delete the `clk_` acceptance branch + the `'clk'` cache-namespace string ([keyResolutionCache.ts](api/src/infrastructure/auth/keyResolutionCache.ts)) once none remain; (b) the **`clu_`** legacy user-bootstrap key ([HashService.ts](api/src/infrastructure/auth/HashService.ts), minted in [AuthService.ts](api/src/application/auth/AuthService.ts)) is also a `cl*` brand remnant ŌĆö rename under the same dual-accept playbook if still in use. Fixing unblocks: zero "claw" in any credential prefix.

- **Marketing feature copy lives in three unconnected lists (pre-existing DRY gap).** The new auto-assign / agents-ship-code capabilities were placed on the [/agents page](frontend/src/app/agents/page.tsx) (the agent marketing surface that renders its full hardcoded list). Separately, the landing page ([page.tsx](frontend/src/app/page.tsx)) has its own inline feature list, and [content.ts `FEATURES`](frontend/src/lib/content.ts) is consumed ONLY by [RegisterPageClient.tsx](frontend/src/app/register/RegisterPageClient.tsx) as `FEATURES.slice(0, 6)`. Three sources, no shared component. Fixing (one `Feature`-shaped source in content.ts ŌĆö icons included ŌĆö consumed by all three surfaces, dropping the per-page arrays and the register slice) unblocks: a single source of truth so a new capability appears everywhere at once.

- **README architecture/integration sections still document STALE pre-rename code artifacts.** Top-of-file marketing prose is now rebranded, but deeper sections (the orchestration-portal route list ~58ŌĆō63, the self-bootstrap walkthrough ~522ŌĆō805, the architecture diagram ~410ŌĆō447) still name `/api/claws`, `ClawRelayDO`, `.coderClaw/`, `X-Claw-Signature`, and the `coderclawllm/workforce-*` model id ŌĆö identifiers that were renamed in code (`/api/agent-hosts`, `AgentHostRelayDO`, `.builderforce/`, `X-AgentHost-Signature`) per the rebrand section below. - **`cosineSimilarity` is duplicated in the gateway (can't import the WebGPU library into a Worker).** [`api/src/application/llm/semanticCache.ts`](api/src/application/llm/semanticCache.ts) carries a local copy of the cosine maths that also lives in `@builderforce/memory`'s `similarity` module, because importing the memory package would drag the WebGPU engine into the Worker bundle. The two must stay in sync by hand. Fixing (extract a zero-dep `@builderforce/similarity` micro-package both can import, or a shared `vector-math` source file) removes the drift risk.

- **Agent-produced PR is recorded in `pull_requests` but never surfaced on the kanban card or anywhere in the frontend.** [RepoService.recordPrResult](api/src/application/repos/RepoService.ts) updates the `pull_requests` row (number/url/status) but does NOT write the resulting URL back onto `tasks.githubPrUrl`, and the frontend never calls the `GET /api/repos/projects/:projectId/pull-requests` list endpoint ([repoRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/repoRoutes.ts)) ŌĆö `builderforceApi.ts` has no repos/PR client. The only PR link shown on a card ([TaskMgmtContent.tsx:634](frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx) / drawer :1215) comes from the manually-typed `githubPrUrl` form field, so an autonomously-created PR is invisible until a human pastes the link. Fixing (write `githubPrUrl` back onto the task in `recordPrResult`, OR add a repos/PR client + a "PRs / changes" tab that reads the pull-requests list) unblocks: closing the agentŌåÆvisible-change loop without manual copy-paste. This is the "code changes are tracked and you can see what the cloud agent changed" requirement ŌĆö backend records it, frontend does not display it.

- **Two cron patterns coexist now.** [/api/approvals/escalate](api/src/presentation/routes/approvalRoutes.ts) is HTTP-triggered with a `CRON_SECRET` query param (requires an external scheduler to hit the URL), while [vendor health probe](api/src/index.ts) uses the native Cloudflare `scheduled()` handler + `[triggers] crons` block in [api/wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml). The native handler is the right pattern on Workers ŌĆö it has no public surface to abuse and doesn't depend on an external scheduler. Fixing (migrate `escalate` into `scheduled()` alongside the vendor probe, drop the `CRON_SECRET` route) unblocks: single cron pattern, one less public endpoint.

- **The frontend's `@seanhogg/builderforce-embedded` must be a real junction, not a copy ŌĆö and the embed package must be pre-built.** On this Windows/MSYS host `ln -s` COPIED the package dir into `frontend/node_modules/@seanhogg/builderforce-embedded`, so a package rebuild didn't propagate and the frontend type-checked against stale types until the copy was replaced with a `mklink /J` junction. A clean checkout / CI must (a) run the workspace install so the `link:` dep becomes a proper junction, and (b) `cd builderforce-embedded && npm run build` before `next build`, since the frontend imports the built `dist`. Fixing (a root install+build step that links + builds the embedded packages, mirroring studio/brain) unblocks: reproducible builds where embed-package changes are actually seen by the frontend.

- **ID-type collision: spec uses `uuid String` PKs + a fresh `Tenant` model; platform `tenants.id`/`projects.id`/`tenant_members` are integer `serial`.** ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)). Two `tenants` tables can't coexist. - **No CI-level e2e covers the studio's actual in-browser ONNX execution ŌĆö nine invariants are unit-tested, the rest needs a real GPU browser.** Nine layers locked by unit tests in [studio/src/engine/](studio/src/engine/): (1) ORT WASM/JS version match; (2) per-model UNet input names; (3) per-input dtypes (LCM `timestep`=float32, SD-Turbo=int64); (4) `reportProgress` fans out (silent-hang UX); (5) `buildOrtSessionOptions` pins `graphOptimizationLevel: 'basic'`; (6) `checkMemoryForModel` reports when probed memory < minimum (inert for WebGPU ŌĆö `null` is honest); (7) `explainOrtError` translates std::bad_alloc, graph-fusion AND `DXGI_ERROR_DEVICE_HUNG` / `Device is lost` (Windows TDR) into actionable diagnostics; (8) `lighterModelHint` never suggests the failing model, and only suggests models that fit available memory; (9) `runSession` wrapper routes every `session.run` through the same translator (catches device-loss at runtime, not just at session create). Plus init-time `assertSessionMatchesSpec` + a `device.lost`-promise listener that emits a clear progress message when the GPU device is reset. Still needing a real WebGPU browser: (a) UNet output name (we pick first Float32); (b) `timestep_cond` embedding values match LCM training; (c) CLIP-L pad-id holds for SD-Turbo; (d) actual VRAM fit; (e) progress timeline end-to-end. Need a Playwright job on a GPU runner.

- **WebGPU doesn't expose actual VRAM ŌĆö `approxMemoryMb` is `null` for the WebGPU device path, so the pre-flight memory check is effectively inert there.** [studio/src/engine/device-router.ts](studio/src/engine/device-router.ts) previously derived "memory" from `adapter.limits.maxBufferSize`, which is a SPEC LIMIT (2 GB default) ŌĆö not memory. That falsely blocked 16GB GPUs as "insufficient." Honest fix in this pass: return `null`. The post-hoc `explainSessionCreateError` still translates a real `std::bad_alloc` into an actionable message, so the OOM case is still well-handled ŌĆö just at the failure point, not predictively. A real predictive check would need a tiny calibration probe (allocate progressively larger GPUBuffers until one fails) at engine init ŌĆö non-trivial and out of scope for this pass. Fixing (add the calibration probe behind a `prepFlight` option) unblocks: honest pre-download "you don't have enough" rather than a 5-minute download ŌåÆ OOM cycle.

- **Real-time collaboration WS is opt-in via `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL` ŌĆö no default, no spam, but also no collab in stacks without the worker.** [frontend/src/hooks/useCollaboration.ts](frontend/src/hooks/useCollaboration.ts) used to fall back to `${NEXT_PUBLIC_WORKER_URL}/api/collab` ŌåÆ `localhost:8787` (the api worker, no collab route) ŌåÆ infinite reconnect loop spamming the console. Hook now returns inert refs when the env var isn't set and logs once. Cost: developers who *do* want collab in dev must (a) deploy the `worker/` package's `CollaborationRoom` Durable Object, and (b) set `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL=ws://localhost:PORT/api/collab`. Fixing (document the env var in [README.md Quick Start](README.md), add to `docker-compose.yml`, or wire a sensible default once the collab worker ships in dev compose) unblocks: collab works out of the box.

- **Two studio packages need (re)publishing + npm auth setup: engine `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio@0.2.0` (breaking ŌĆö React layer removed) and the brand-new `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio-embedded@0.1.0`.** The engine was split: `0.1.x` carried `StudioPanel`; `0.2.0` is engine-only and the React layer moved to the new `-embedded` package. Both are built locally but unpublished ŌĆö the publishing environment's `~/.npmrc` token is dead (a `404 PUT` on publish), so they need either a fresh `NPM_TOKEN` repo secret or OIDC trusted publishers. (3) For zero-secret CI thereafter, add trusted publishers at `https://www.npmjs.com/package/<name>/access` for each. Until (1)+(2), external `npm install @seanhogg/builderforce-studio` still resolves the old `0.1.x` (with the now-removed React exports) ŌĆö the in-app IDE is unaffected since it consumes both via local `link:`.

- **`docker compose up` requires `NEON_DATABASE_URL` in `api/.dev.vars` ŌĆö the stack cannot bundle Postgres because the api uses `@neondatabase/serverless` HTTP transport.** [api/src/infrastructure/database/connection.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/connection.ts) calls `neon(url)` which speaks Neon's HTTP `/sql` endpoint, not raw PG protocol. A bundled `postgres:16` service won't accept Neon HTTP queries; bridging requires a community proxy like `ghcr.io/timowilhelm/local-neon-http-proxy` plus a runtime `neonConfig` override to point the driver at it. Out of scope for v0 docker (free Neon signup is 30 seconds and gives the same shape as production). Fixing (add the proxy service + `neonConfig.fetchEndpoint` override gated on a `LOCAL_NEON=1` env var) unblocks: truly zero-prereq `docker compose up`, contributor onboarding without a Neon account.

- **README references `@seanhogg/ssmjs` as an installed dependency in two places, but it is not in `frontend/package.json`.** [README.md "AI Training Studio" bullet at line 35](README.md) claims `uses @seanhogg/ssmjs / Transformers.js with WebGPU` and the [On-Device AI Stack diagram at line 359-377](README.md) shows `SSM.js (@seanhogg/ssmjs)` as a layer over `mambacode.js`. [frontend/package.json](frontend/package.json) only ships `mambacode.js: github:SeanHogg/Mamba` and `@huggingface/transformers ^3.8.1` ŌĆö the actual integration is `MambaModelProvider` in [frontend/src/lib/model-provider.ts](frontend/src/lib/model-provider.ts) and the in-tree [mamba-engine.ts](frontend/src/lib/mamba-engine.ts). - **Migration 0069 has not been applied to any DB and the calendar/library flows have never run end-to-end.** Typecheck (api + frontend) and schema-drift pass, but no DB has the new columns/tables, so the activity-calendar query, agent sync, and prompt publish/use/star paths are unproven against live data. Fixing (apply 0069, sync agents on a tenant with active claws + ingested git activity, publish and use a public prompt) unblocks: confidence the features work, not just compile.

- **Migration 0072 has not been applied to any DB; the pipeline has never run end-to-end against live data.** Type-check (api + frontend), schema-drift, and unit tests pass, but no DB has the `repo_analysis_*` tables and no real repo has been analyzed, so the DO alarm progression (`fetching ŌåÆ analyzing:* ŌåÆ writing_back ŌåÆ completed`), the provider API calls against real GitHub/Bitbucket/GitLab, the project-details write-back, and the `project_memories` seed are unproven live. The `ANALYSIS_RUNNER` DO migration tag `v3` in [wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml) is also unapplied. Fixing (apply 0072 + 0099 + `wrangler deploy` to register the DO, map a repo with a stored credential, run an analysis on a Pro and a Free tenant) unblocks: confidence the feature works, not just compiles.

- **Migration 0074 is authored but not applied to any live DB.** `integration_credentials.project_id` + the `gitlab` enum value exist in [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) + [0074_integration_project_scope.sql](api/migrations/0074_integration_project_scope.sql) and `check:schema` passes, but no `npm run db:migrate` ran (headless env). Until applied, project-scoped key creation and GitLab credentials 500 at runtime. Fixing (run `db:migrate` per environment) unblocks: the feature working in prod. Same caveat as the 0070/0071/0072 entries.

- **Yjs collab seeding can double-insert if the websocket sync lands after the local seed.** [CodeEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/CodeEditor.tsx) now seeds an empty `ydoc.getText(filePath)` from the persisted file content on (re)bind so the binding never blanks a file. When `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL` is set, the y-websocket provider may sync authoritative remote content *after* this local seed, producing duplicated text. Inert today (collab is opt-in and unset in prod). Fixing (gate the seed on `provider.synced`/`once('sync')`, or only seed when the room is known-empty) unblocks: safe content seeding once real-time collaboration is enabled.

- **Migration 0075 is authored but not applied to any live DB.** `ide_agents` gains nullable `project_id` + `tenant_id`/pricing/runtime/`published` columns and the `gitlab`-style additions, but no `npm run db:migrate` ran (headless env). Until applied, `POST /api/workforce/agents` + `/mine` 500 with "column does not exist". Fixing (run `db:migrate` per environment) unblocks: cloud-agent create/publish working in prod. Same caveat as 0070ŌĆō0074.

  (1) **npm: `npm deprecate @seanhogg/coderclaw` (exists @ 2026.3.21) + publish
  `@seanhogg/builderforce-agents` (404, unpublished)** ŌĆö BLOCKED: `npm whoami` returns **401**, no
  valid publish token here. The package now builds, so this is a one-command release once
  authenticated. (2) **`coderclaw.ai`ŌåÆ`builderforce.ai` DNS/301** + the install-script endpoint +
  Discord handle ŌĆö need registrar/Cloudflare DNS access (app-level `_redirects` + Astro redirects
  are already in place). (3) The generated `docs-site/src/assets/install-script.svg` + the
  `credits.md` "CLAW + TARDIS" easter-egg still say "claw" ŌĆö cosmetic, regenerate/reword when the
  mascot decision lands.

- **Migration `0100_human_request_kinds.sql` not yet applied to any live DB.** This pass generalized `approvals` into human-in-the-loop *requests* (the agent's `ask_human` bubble channel): added `kind` (`approval`/`question`/`feedback`), `response_text`, an `'answered'` value on the `approval_status` enum, and two `(tenant_id, ŌĆ”)` indexes ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)). The migration is additive + idempotent (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, `ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS`) but, per project convention, was NOT auto-run against the operator's Neon DB. Note the `ALTER TYPE ŌĆ” ADD VALUE` runs as its own statement in the HTTP migration runner ([migrate.mjs](api/scripts/migrate.mjs)) ŌĆö fine on PG12+ outside a txn. Until it's applied (`npm --prefix api run db:migrate`), the API's insert/update of `kind`/`response_text` will fail against the old shape and the Approvals & Q&A tab plus the `ask_human` tool can't persist. Running it unblocks: the whole question/feedback escalation feature going live.

- **IDE reference panel SHIPPED ŌĆö `/ide/voice` Voice Studio validates the full UX end-to-end, on-device AND server.** New page ([ide/voice/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/ide/voice/page.tsx)) + [VoiceClonePanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/VoiceClonePanel.tsx) + api client ([voiceClones.ts](frontend/src/lib/voiceClones.ts)) + sidebar nav entry: create a clone (name + **file OR mic capture** + required consent), list voices, synthesize text, play audio with live word-highlighting, and an honest "Cloning unavailable ŌĆö <reason>" banner (PRD ┬¦7). Frontend type-checks 0 errors. **On-device gap CLOSED:** the panel now prefers the FREE on-device WebGPU path ŌĆö [captureAudio.ts](frontend/src/lib/captureAudio.ts) (`decodeAudioData` fileŌåÆPCM + `MicRecorder`) feeds the studio `VoiceCloneEngine` to enrol a speaker embedding client-side, and synthesis routes through the package's own `VoiceClient.narrate` seam ([voiceEngine.ts](frontend/src/lib/voiceEngine.ts)) ŌĆö on-device when an embedding is held, else the metered server ŌĆö so the IDE dogfoods the exact contract hired.video consumes (DRY: no bespoke frontend resolver). The studio engine is dynamic-imported (lazy, client-only) so it degrades to server if absent/no-WebGPU; an engine badge surfaces which path is live. `@seanhogg/builderforce-voice` added as a frontend link dep. Superseded `voiceClones.synthesizeVoice`/`fetchVoiceoverObjectUrl`/`SynthesisUnavailable`/`listMarketplaceVoices` were deleted (zero refs). **Residuals:** (1) on-device embeddings persist in `localStorage` only (per-device, not synced ŌĆö the server's no-leak contract means a new device must re-enrol or use the server path); (2) no in-IDE marketplace **browse** UI yet (the catalog route exists but buy/checkout backend doesn't ŌĆö see voice residual #2 above).
- **`awaiting_workflow` parked tickets have no park-age timeout (T8 residual, 2026-06-14).** A ticket parked on a spawned `run_workflow` (migration 0171) waits indefinitely for the workflow to settle; if that workflow is dropped or never reports, the ticket is stuck in `awaiting_workflow` with no fallback (`resumeParkedWorkflows` only acts on a settle signal). Fixing (a park-age timeout that routes a stale parked ticket to `needs_attention`) unblocks: no permanently-stuck lane tickets.

- **Historical migration-prefix collisions are grandfathered, not renumbered (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** `.migration-collisions-allowlist.txt` whitelists 8 long-applied duplicate prefixes (0009/0014/0018/0060/0064/0068/0075/0076) because renumbering applied migrations is a release-level ledger op. Fixing (a coordinated renumber + `_migrations` ledger update + redeploy) unblocks: a fully collision-free history with an empty allowlist.

- **No empty-DB `db:migrate` dry-run in CI ŌĆö Neon-infra blocked (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** `check-migrations.mjs` fails CI on duplicate prefixes, but nothing applies the full migration set to an ephemeral DB pre-deploy, so a missing-`CREATE`/ordering bug still surfaces only in prod. Blocked on a CI-provisioned ephemeral Neon/Postgres. Fixing unblocks: schema drift caught at PR time, not prod.

- **Isolation-Tracks README table and `.github/isolation-tracks.json` are hand-maintained ŌĆö drift risk (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** The `check-track-scope` guard reads the JSON manifest while the README renders the human table; the two can diverge. Fixing (a generator that renders the README table FROM the manifest in CI) unblocks: a single source of truth for track ownership (DRY).

### Cloud Agent Boards (added 2026-06-01 ŌĆö migrations 0064ŌĆō0068; swimlanes / board-sync / PRD / repos / agent dispatch)


Execution + autonomous advancement + in-browser coding are now wired and tested (migration 0068 `agent_dispatches`): `SwimlaneCoordinator.startTicket` compiles the lane's agents into dispatches and routes them (claw push via `ClawStageDispatcher`/`CLAW_RELAY`, or browser PULL); `reportDispatchResult` aggregates the stage and autonomously advances the ticket (or routes to needs_attention ŌĆö never a silent advance). The user-facing worker tab ([frontend/src/app/agent-worker/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/agent-worker/page.tsx)) claims `browser` dispatches; for a repo-targeted task it CODES in-browser ŌĆö the agent's model proposes file edits, which are applied and pushed through the server-side git-proxy via isomorphic-git (`frontend/src/lib/browserRuntime/{gitClient,coding,factory}.ts`), with an optional WebContainer build/test gate that blocks a push on failure. Backed by `POST /api/agent-runtime/claim` + `/result` and `POST /api/git-proxy/:repoId/...`. Orchestration is unit/render-tested; the live WebContainer boot + isomorphic-gitŌåögit-proxy round-trip are integration-validated in a real tab only. Remaining roadmap items:

### Agentic Workflow Builder (added 2026-06-02 ŌĆö migration 0060; visual IPAAS-style workflow authoring + LLM-logic nodes)


A drag-and-drop builder ([WorkflowBuilder](frontend/src/components/workflow-builder/WorkflowBuilder.tsx) on `@xyflow/react`, route `/workflows/builder`) lets tenants compose workflow graphs from a node palette that includes LLM-logic nodes ŌĆö **memory** (recall/write), **knowledge base** (query/ingest), **train** ŌĆö plus **agent-run** and ETL/trigger/output nodes. Graphs persist as reusable `workflow_definitions` (migration [0060](api/migrations/0060_workflow_definitions.sql), [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts), [workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts)) and compile through the shared contract ([domain/workflowGraph.ts](api/src/domain/workflowGraph.ts)) into orchestrator steps; CoderClaw's [orchestrator](../coderClaw/product/src/coderclaw/orchestrator.ts) now executes the LLM-logic/ETL node kinds in-process via dedicated handlers. The shape mirrors the existing execution-record + telemetry-graph surfaces, so a definition run appears in the monitoring UI for free.

The six original roadmap items were closed in a follow-up pass: **portalŌåÆhost execution** (host-authed `POST /api/workflows/claim` + `/:id/host-result` in [workflowRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/workflowRoutes.ts), a [WorkflowPollerService](../coderClaw/product/src/infra/workflow-poller.ts) wired in [server-startup.ts](../coderClaw/product/src/gateway/server-startup.ts), and `orchestrator.createWorkflowFromTasks`); **memory-write / KB-ingest / train** (real delegates on [SsmMemoryAdapter](../coderClaw/product/src/infra/orchestrator-ports-adapter.ts) ŌåÆ `remember`/`learn`/`distillAndSave`, plus a `train` port); **ETL evaluation** ([node-eval.ts](../coderClaw/product/src/coderclaw/node-eval.ts) ŌĆö safe, eval-free predicate/transform); **YAML isomorphism** (`definitionToYaml`/`yamlToDefinition` + `/:id/export` + `/import`); and **caching** (canonical [getOrSetCached](api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts) L1+L2 on the definitions list). ### BurnRateOS embed / identity-federation spec (doc 05) ŌĆö security review 2026-05-31

The federation gap was accepted by design. Remaining roadmap items:

### Segment tier (tenant ŌåÆ segment ŌåÆ entity isolation for multi-tenant integrators)


Tenancy is two-tier today (tenant ŌåÆ entity); customers who are themselves multi-tenant (e.g. BurnRateOS as one tenant, serving their own end-clients) have no way to isolate their end-clients. Target model: a **segment** = (account, company) of the integrator's client, sitting between tenant and entity. **Segmentation is opt-in per tenant (not all customers are multi-tenant), but when a tenant is segmented, isolation is a HARD, non-bypassable rule** ŌĆö a forgotten filter is a breach, not a bug. The following gaps were identified in the 2026-05-31 evaluation pass and are unbuilt:

#### Embed rail ŌĆö re-embedding BuilderForce into BurnRateOS ([builderforce-embedded](builderforce-embedded/), [frontend/src/app/embed](frontend/src/app/embed/))


The host-side embed component + the frame-side transport LANDED this pass (built, type-checked, 11 tests green): `@seanhogg/builderforce-embedded` exports the single DRY `<BuilderForceEmbed view=ŌĆ” token=ŌĆ” />` (sandboxed iframe, secure postMessage JWT handoff ŌĆö token never in the URL, auto-resize, deep-link sync); the BuilderForce frontend serves the iframe half at `/embed/[view]` ([useEmbedFrame](frontend/src/lib/embed/useEmbedFrame.ts) imports the protocol from the package so the two ends can't drift); and `middleware.ts` sets `frame-ancestors` for `/embed/*`. BurnRateOS can start swapping its `/product/*`,`/agile/*`,`/governance/*` pages to `<BuilderForceEmbed>` now. **Still open:**

#### Spec alignment ŌĆö BurnRateOS PM/Agile extraction ([specs/builderforce/](specs/builderforce/))


The `specs/builderforce/` PRD set (docs 00ŌĆō06) designs extracting BurnRateOS's Product-Management + Agile-Survival domains into BuilderForce as the system of record, re-embedded back via SSO + the embed rail. The tenancy design in the spec (TenantŌåÆSegmentŌåÆEntity, `resolveSegment` chokepoint, `(tenantId, segmentId)` on every entity) MATCHES the segment-tier plan above and is sound. But the spec is written greenfield (Prisma/uuid, BuilderForce-owns-nothing-identity) and collides with the platform that already exists. Reviewed 2026-05-31; the following alignment gaps are unbuilt:

already exists; NOT `AgentRuntime` ŌĆö that route surface already exists). Done + verified: DB rename
