### Voice cloning (VibeVoice ŌåÆ SSM clone foundation) ŌĆö Phase 1+2 in studio, server route #1994 shipped, IDE panel shipped; trained weights + marketplace-checkout remain

### Real-time project board (added 2026-06-14) ŌĆö project room WebSocket push for the whole project surface

The project board/kanban/calendar/list + open task drawer are now live for concurrent humans + agents: a per-project room (`SessionRoomDO`, key `project:<id>`) pushes `{type:"changed"}` over `GET /api/projects/:id/stream`; the frontend subscribes via `useRealtimeRoom` and refetches. Task create/update/move/delete broadcast from `taskRoutes`; execution lifecycle broadcasts via the `setExecutionBoardSink` hook in `executionEvents` ŌåÆ `makeExecutionBoardSink` (resolves taskIdŌåÆprojectId). Card chips also resolve cloud agents by name and show agent run history (prior + queued). **Open residuals:**
- **Bypassed status writers:** execution status writes that do NOT route through `notifyExecutionSubscribers` (e.g. `staleExecutionReaper` raw SQL, some `CloudRunnerDO`/`AnalysisRunnerDO` direct `db.update(executions)`) won't push to the board ŌĆö those transitions only surface via the `useBoardLiveRuns` reconcile backstop poll (8s/30s). Fixing = funnel all execution-status writes through one notifier (or add a DB-trigger/outbox fan-out) so every transition is real-time. Unblocks: drop the backstop poll entirely.
- **Dispatch feed still polled:** lane-header dispatch chips (`boardsApi.dispatches`) refetch on the room push, but `SwimlaneCoordinator` dispatch-only status changes that don't emit an execution `status_change` won't trigger a push. Low impact; covered by the backstop.
- **Cross-isolate WS loss:** the room DO fan-out is per-isolate like every other room here; the backstop poll is the intentional reconciliation (mirrors `useExecutionStream`). A missed frame self-heals within one poll interval.

---

### Autonomous lane chaining on agent completion (added 2026-06-14) ŌĆö next lane's agent now kicks off after an auto-move

A cloud agent finishing a ticket advanced its lane via `RuntimeService.update` writing `tasks.status` directly, which bypassed the `maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry` trigger that the human board-drag PATCH uses ŌĆö so the next lane's configured agent never started (only human drags chained). Fixed by an injected `onLaneEntry` sink (wired in `buildRuntimeService`, shared by the Worker and `CloudRunnerDO`) that fires the SAME trigger when a COMPLETED run moves a ticket into a new non-terminal lane. Loop-safe: the auto-run dispatch stamps `laneKey` into its payload, and the trigger skips a same-lane re-entry (keyed on lane, not agent, so a genuine handoff to a different lane staffed by the same agent still runs). **Open residuals:**
- **No position-based stage routing on the execution path:** `RuntimeService` hardcodes `RUNNINGŌåÆin_progress` and `COMPLETEDŌåÆin_review`, so autonomous chaining is a single hop into `in_review` ŌĆö it does NOT walk `backlogŌåÆtodoŌåÆreadyŌåÆin_progress` by swimlane position. A ticket whose agent completes in an early lane jumps straight to `in_review`, skipping intermediate lanes' agents. The richer position/`action_type`-driven advance lives only in the parallel `SwimlaneCoordinator` (agent_dispatches model), which the execution-based board does not route through. Fixing = unify the two advance models (or teach the execution path to resolve the next lane by swimlane position + action). Unblocks: true multi-stage BAŌåÆDevŌåÆQA pipelines on the V2 cloud-agent board.
- **`in_review` default gate is `human`:** the loop-prone case only arises if an operator overrides `in_review` (or another completion-target lane) to `gate:'auto'` and staffs it; the same-lane guard covers that, but a mis-staffed auto-gated review lane is still a config smell worth surfacing in the lane editor.

---

### VS Code extension ŌĆö coding agent + browser sign-in built; backend deploy pending (added 2026-06-17, updated 2026-06-20)

The `clients/vscode/` extension + dual-registry publish pipeline (Marketplace via `vsce` + Open VSX via `ovsx`, `.github/workflows/publish-vscode.yml`) ships a working coding agent. **Now done & verified (compiles, packages, installed locally):**
- Ō£ģ **In-folder agent editing** ŌĆö agentic tool-calling loop (`agent.ts`) over sandboxed file tools (`fileTools.ts`: read/write/edit/list/delete, path-guarded to the open folder, re-rooted on folder change) with Apply/Skip approval gated by `permissionMode`.
- Ō£ģ **Codebase scan + knowledge summary** ŌĆö `codebaseScan.ts` does a bounded, skip-list-aware walk ŌåÆ one summary call ŌåÆ writes `.builderforce/architecture.md` + a grounding summary injected as agent context; read-through cached by a file-tree version token (`.builderforce/scan.json`); **Rescan Codebase** command forces refresh.
- Ō£ģ **Browser device-code sign-in** ŌĆö extension `auth.ts` `AuthenticationProvider` runs the RFC 8628 flow (paste-key fallback); **backend built**: migration `0201_device_authorizations.sql`, `deviceAuthorizations` schema, `DeviceAuthService` (mints a tenant `bfk_*` gateway key, encrypted one-time delivery), `/api/auth/device/{code,approve,token}` routes, and the frontend `/activate` verify page. API + frontend type-check clean; migration/schema-drift checks pass.
- Ō£ģ **Real mascot icon** (agentHost brand mark).

**Open residuals (specced in [specs/builderforce/14-prd-vscode-extension.md](specs/builderforce/14-prd-vscode-extension.md)):**
- **Device-code + editor-key backend not deployed** ŌĆö the only blocker for browser sign-in working in prod: apply migration `0201` to Neon + deploy the API worker (`api && npm run deploy`) + deploy the frontend (`frontend && npm run cf-deploy`). The unified `/activate` page now serves BOTH device approval (`?code=`, auto-returns the key, no copy/paste) AND a copy-button editor key (no code) via `POST /api/auth/editor-key` (`DeviceAuthService.mintEditorKey`, NOT owner-gated). Root cause of the earlier bad fallback: `/settings/api-keys` returns early for non-owners (`if (!isOwner)`), so it shows no key button ŌĆö the extension fallback now opens `/activate` instead. Until deployed, prod has none of this, so the extension's paste box opens `/activate` which will 404 against current prod. *(Infra/deploy ŌĆö needs live env + secrets.)*
- **"Never leave VS Code": embed the real web pages in the editor (DRY, no rebuild; deploy pending)** ŌĆö instead of reimplementing workforce/board/etc. natively, the extension opens the existing `/embed/<view>` pages as editor webview panels (`src/embedPanel.ts`) and bridges auth via the existing embed postMessage protocol (`builderforce-embed/v1` readyŌåÆauth), handing over a tenant JWT from `getTenantJwt` (bfk exchange). Commands **Open Board** / **Open PageŌĆ”** (kanban/backlog/roadmap/sprints/retros/poker/velocity/prd/ideas/feature-roi) with the selected project deep-linked via `#projectId=`. **Frontend unlock (1 shared helper, both layers):** `embedTrust.ts` now trusts the `vscode-webview:` scheme (`isVsCodeWebviewOrigin`) for the inbound `auth` postMessage, and `middleware.ts` adds `vscode-webview:` to the `/embed` `frame-ancestors` CSP ŌĆö without these, VS Code's random `vscode-webview://<guid>` origin is blocked by both the CSP and `isTrustedHostOrigin`. **Residuals:** (a) needs `frontend && npm run cf-deploy` to take effect (prod `/embed` still blocks `vscode-webview:` until then); (b) no `workforce` embed view exists in the registry (`builderforce-embedded/src/views.ts` is product/agile/security pillars only) ŌĆö add `/embed/workforce` + a view entry to embed the people+agents grid; (c) embed views self-gate on tenant embed `capabilities` (`/api/embed/config` must be enabled for the tenant). *(T7 IDE client + T2 frontend.)*
- **VS Code as the 3rd agent runtime: project/task management + tracked human-in-the-loop connection (built; deploy pending)** ŌĆö the extension is now a "local coder agent" alongside Cloud and On-Prem. **Backend (new, type-checks + drift pass; needs `api && npm run deploy`):** `POST /api/auth/tenant-api-key-token` exchanges the editor's `bfk_*` key for a tenant JWT minted AS the key's creator (so `/api/projects`+`/api/tasks` are reachable as the human ŌĆö they require `authMiddleware`, which `bfk` keys can't satisfy directly); `vscode_connections` table (migration 0202) + `POST /api/vscode/connect` heartbeat + `GET /api/vscode/connections` to record/show which user has a live VS Code coder agent per tenant. **Extension:** a "Project & Tasks" tree (`src/projectsTree.ts`, `src/bfApi.ts`, `src/projectState.ts`) ŌĆö Select Project ŌåÆ lists tasks ŌåÆ click/right-click to **start a chat session linked to a task** (session carries projectId/taskId, injected as agent context) or **set task status** (partial PATCH, which fires the server-side lane automation so a human can dispatch agents from the editor); connection heartbeat on sign-in + every 5 min. **Residuals:** (a) no `'vscode'` value in the `agent_type` enum yet, so tasks can't be *assigned to* the VS Code agent (only the human assignee links it) ŌĆö add via a future migration + downstream handling; (b) the workforce/observability UI doesn't render `vscode_connections` yet (endpoint exists, no frontend card); (c) pending-changes/diff review is the standard editor (no per-task diff panel yet). *(T7 IDE client + T3 auth + T4.)*
- **IDE UX restructured to Claude-Code model (sidebar session list + center editor chat)** ŌĆö the Activity Bar view is now a `TreeDataProvider` (`src/sessionsTree.ts`) of persisted sessions (`src/sessionStore.ts`, per-workspace `workspaceState`); **New Session** / clicking a row opens the chat as a webview **editor panel in the center** (`src/chatPanel.ts`, `createWebviewPanel` in `ViewColumn.Active`) so changes are reviewable side-by-side ŌĆö all STABLE API, no proposed flag, publishable. The old in-sidebar `ChatViewProvider` was deleted; shared agent/run logic via `runAgent`+`buildSystemMessages`, model selection via `src/modelState.ts`, grounding via `src/grounding.ts`. Residual: sessions persist transcript only (not per-session model or tool history); no Local/Web toggle yet (Local only).
- **Native chat: participant DONE but needs a Copilot-Chat host to surface; dedicated tab blocked on proposed API** ŌĆö BuilderForce registers as `@builderforce` via the STABLE Chat Participant API (`src/chatParticipant.ts`, reuses agent loop/tools/grounding; prompt+grounding shared via `src/prompt.ts`/`src/grounding.ts`). CONSTRAINT discovered: the `@`-participant only appears inside **GitHub Copilot Chat's** ask box ŌĆö Claude Code / Codex / Roo bring their own chat UIs and do NOT host third-party participants, so on a machine without GitHub Copilot Chat the participant has no surface (it's registered but invisible). The dedicated agent-session TAB with a SESSIONS list (like CLAUDE CODE / CODEX) uses the `chatSessionsProvider`/chat-sessions controller API, which is **proposed** (`enabledApiProposals`, mid providerŌåÆcontroller migration) ŌĆö not publishable, Insiders/`--enable-proposed-api` only. Options to actually match the CLAUDE CODE/CODEX tab UX: (a) keep the webview sidebar (works everywhere, no host needed ŌĆö the recommended surface), or (b) adopt the proposed sessions API for a sideload-only build the user launches with the proposal flag (unpublishable + fragile until it stabilizes). Needs an explicit user decision. *(T7 IDE client.)*
- **`BrainPanel` not reused yet** ŌĆö the webview is vanilla HTML/JS; reusing the real chat UI requires extracting the Brain UI into `@seanhogg/builderforce-brain-embedded/ui` (app couplings made injectable) and repointing the frontend, then deleting the app-resident copies. Unblocks one-source-two-hosts chat (no fork). *(T2 ┬Ę App UI & Brain.)*
- **Learned routing (PRD 13) not consumed** ŌĆö IDE runs should classify action type, read the cached `routing:<scope>` table, compute local SSM `routingBias` (Node host), seed via `rankModelsForAction`, and write outcomes back via a new `POST /llm/v1/run-outcome`; needs `run_model_outcomes` (now shipped via 0197) extended with `source`/`client_run_id` + nullable `execution_id`. Coordinate the migration with the PRD 13 owner so it lands once. *(T3 + T4.)*
- **Key-revoke endpoint missing** ŌĆö `signOut`/`removeSession` clears the local key but no server-side `POST /api/auth/keys/revoke` invalidates the minted `bfk_*` gateway-side. Unblocks true sign-out/rotation.
- **Gateway chat 500 `invalid input syntax for type integer: "0.9"` (FIXED in code; deploy pending)** ŌĆö `enforceDailyTokenCap` in `llmRoutes.ts` interpolated `1 - CACHE_READ_MULTIPLIER` (=0.9) and `CACHE_CREATION_MULTIPLIER - 1` as bare bound params next to integer token columns, so neon-http/Postgres inferred them as `integer` and rejected `"0.9"` ŌĆö 500'ing every `/v1/chat/completions` and `/v1/messages` (our-models branch) call once a tenant had any usage rows. Fixed by `::float8` casts (Math.floor already re-integers the cap). Needs `api && npm run deploy` to clear in prod. *(T3.)*
- **Agent tool-calling assumes OpenAI-style `tools`** ŌĆö models in the pool that don't support function-calling won't edit files (they'll just chat). Pick a tool-capable model via **Pick Model**. A non-tool fallback (fenced-action parsing) is a possible future hardening.
- **Grounding map (FIXED) + on-prem `.builderforce/` parity** ŌĆö the scan summary previously listed only top-level workspace dirs, so the agent couldn't locate nested sub-projects (e.g. `Builderforce.ai/clients/vscode`) and walked the tree via `list_files`, burning tokens. Now `codebaseScan.ts` writes an on-prem-style `.builderforce/` (context.yaml, project-map.md, architecture.md, memory/, README, scan.json) and injects a COMPACT deterministic map (sub-project/manifest locations + directory tree) into the agent so it locates files without walking. Residual: no knowledge-loop yet (the extension doesn't append per-run session notes into `.builderforce/memory/` like the on-prem `KnowledgeLoopService` does) ŌĆö adding it would compound grounding over time. *(T7 IDE client / T5 parity.)*
- **Superadmin capped by free-plan token limit (FIXED in code; deploy + cache TTL pending)** ŌĆö `enforceDailyTokenCap` already bypasses the cap when `access.isSuperadmin`, but the `bfk` tenant-API-key resolution branch in `llmRoutes.ts` hardcoded `isSuperadmin: false` and never looked up the key's creator, so a superadmin-minted editor key (and the IDE editor key) authenticated with no superadmin status and got the free 10k/day cap. Fixed by `leftJoin(users)` on `tenantApiKeys.createdByUserId` ŌåÆ propagate `users.isSuperadmin` through the cached payload into `TenantAccess.isSuperadmin` (mirrors the JWT path). Needs `api && npm run deploy`; also the existing key's resolution may be cached in `AUTH_CACHE_KV` without the flag until its TTL expires (or mint a fresh key post-deploy). *(T3.)*
- **Free-plan token cap makes agentic coding impractical on free tier** ŌĆö agent tool-loops resend context each turn, so a few rounds exceed the free plan's 10,000 tokens/day (`plan_token_limit_exceeded`, HTTP 429). The grounding map reduces burn (fewer list/read calls) but real in-IDE coding needs Pro. Surface a clear upsell in the extension when 429 hits (the gateway message is now shown verbatim). *(Product/plan ŌĆö not a bug.)*

- **VS Code Projects/Tasks 401 "Token has been revoked or expired" (FIXED in code; deploy pending)** ŌĆö `/api/auth/tenant-api-key-token` returned 200 but `/api/projects` 401'd. Confirmed via the new **Diagnose Connection** command: `signJwt` always stamps a `jti` (`payload.jti ?? crypto.randomUUID()`), and `authMiddleware` rejects any jti without a matching active `authTokens` row ŌĆö the exchange never persisted one. Fix: the exchange now `persistToken(...)`s the minted token (mirrors `/api/auth/web/login` + `/tenant-token`) and requires `tenantApiKeys.createdByUserId` (FK ŌåÆ users.id; returns 400 if absent). Also hardened the extension: `bfApi.authed` throws `HTTP <status> <body>`, tree/selectProject show the real error, and `bfApi.diagnose` probes each hop. Needs `api && npm run deploy`. **Adjacent latent bug (same root cause):** `/api/auth/agentHost-token` also signs via `signJwt` (gets a jti) without persisting ŌĆö agentHost tokens would 401 the same way on jti-checked routes; fix it the same way (persistToken) when next touched. *(T3 auth + T7 IDE client.)*

- **Acknowledgements "OpenAgentHost" upstream links ŌĆö verified real, left as-is (logged for awareness)** ŌĆö `frontend/src/app/agents/acknowledgements/page.tsx` (~L54, L62) links to `https://openclaw.ai` and `https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw` as the historical upstream ("BuilderForce Agents started as a fork of OpenAgentHost"). Web-checked during the 2026-06-21 public-page gap pass: both resolve to a **real, active** project (OpenClaw ŌĆö a local-first personal AI assistant with the same multi-channel/skills narrative), so they are a genuine external acknowledgement, not a dead placeholder ŌĆö left untouched per instructions. Note only: the prose names the project "OpenAgentHost" while the links/URLs say "openclaw" ŌĆö a naming inconsistency (likely a rebrand-rename artifact across this app's copy), not a broken link. No fix applied. *(Public copy / acknowledgement.)*

- **Marketing header dropdowns are CSS-only (no JS aria-expanded / touch toggle)** ŌĆö the new `frontend/src/components/MarketingHeader.tsx` Product mega-menu + Resources dropdown open on `:hover`/`:focus-within` only. Keyboard users can open them (focus-within) and mobile uses the separate hamburger drawer, so no flow is broken, but the `<button>` triggers never reflect a live `aria-expanded` state and there is no click-to-toggle for hybrid touch+pointer devices. Fixing it (small `useState` open-index + click/Escape handling + `aria-expanded`) would make the desktop menus fully WCAG-conformant. *(T1 ┬Ę Marketing & SEO Web.)*

- **Ō£ģ Public Prompt Library was empty ŌĆö seeded 15 curated SYSTEM prompts (migration 0210)** ŌĆö `/prompts` showed nothing because the public gallery (`GET /api/prompts/public`) only returns rows with `visibility='public'` and there was no seed. Resolved by seeding real rows so they are first-class (searchable/starrable/usage-tracked, identical to a user-published prompt): `api/migrations/0210_seed_system_prompts.sql` creates a reserved system tenant (`builderforce-system`, `isolation_mode='single'`) + its default segment, then inserts 15 public prompts authored as "Builderforce" across Entrepreneurs/Testing/Coding/Business Analysis/Marketing Research (entry + version 1, idempotent via NOT EXISTS on the public slug). The earlier client-side built-in approach (`frontend/src/lib/builtinPrompts.ts` + merge logic) was **deleted** as duplicative ŌĆö the page now consumes the API only. Also fixed in the same pass: `/prompts` used `PageContainer` (app-shell wrapper, left-aligned) instead of the `.page-inner` centered hero used by every other public/marketing browse page (`models`, `marketplace`) ŌĆö now aligned. **Remaining step:** the seed only takes effect once the migration runs ŌĆö `cd api && npm run deploy` (runs `migrate.mjs` then deploys the worker). *(T9 migration + T1 Marketing.)*

- **Hero forest backdrop is stylized vector, not photoreal (asset-blocked)** ŌĆö `frontend/src/components/WaveBackdrop.tsx` renders a canvas fly-through forest that draws sprite images from `/public/hero/*.svg` (procedural triangle tree as fallback). The SVG sprites are richer now (organic scalloped tiers, gradients, a light side, an feTurbulence texture filter) but hand-coded vector cannot match contextqa.com's painted/photographic trees. The render pipeline already draws ANY image from `SPRITE_SRCS`, so reaching contextqa-grade is purely an ASSET swap: drop high-res transparent tree PNGs (licensed or AI-generated) into `/public/hero/` and list them in `SPRITE_SRCS` ŌĆö zero code change. Alternatively replace the whole canvas with a looping `<video>` of a forest fly-through (also un-gated by reduce-motion). Blocked only on sourcing the art. *(T1 ┬Ę Marketing & SEO Web.)*

- **Hero backdrop pivoted to a procedural solar-system fly-through (supersedes the forest/water art-blocked entries)** ŌĆö `frontend/src/components/WaveBackdrop.tsx` is now a canvas+rAF deep-space flight: warp starfield + procedurally-shaded planets (rings, bands, glow) that approach from centre, grow, and fan off to the sides, with occasional meteor clusters. Procedural spheres render well with NO external art, so the earlier "needs photoreal tree/water PNGs" blockers no longer apply to the hero. Hero text is forced light in both themes (dark space backdrop). Residual polish: the scene is dark in light-mode too (intentional), and planet variety/pacing can be tuned. *(T1 ┬Ę Marketing & SEO Web.)*

### Agentic Tester ŌĆö platform-native schedulable agent (added 2026-06-21)

Made the Agentic Tester a fully platform-driven, schedulable agent and **deleted the GitHub-Action surface** (`qa.yml` + `agentic-tester.yml` removed). **Built this pass:** machine-token auth ([qa-e2e/src/bf.ts](qa-e2e/src/bf.ts) ŌĆö `BF_AGENT_TOKEN` decodes its `tid`; operator login is dev-only, fixing the `npm run explore` "Missing BF_QA_PASSWORD" break); per-project **schedules** (`qa_schedules`, migration [0209](api/migrations/0209_qa_schedules.sql)) configured in the UI ([QaContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx) `SchedulesSection`); a **sweep** ([runQaExplorationSweep.ts](api/src/application/qa/runQaExplorationSweep.ts)) on the `*/5` cron that enqueues a heatmap exploration per due schedule + re-arms `next_run_at`; **managed container dispatch** ŌĆö the runner is now a Cloudflare Container ([QaRunnerContainerDO.ts](api/src/infrastructure/relay/QaRunnerContainerDO.ts) + `[[containers]]` binding `QA_RUNNER_CONTAINER`, image the self-contained in-tree [api/qa-container/](api/qa-container/) `server.mjs` ŌĆö wired like `api/container`, not a cross-dir path); **token minting + dispatch** ([dispatchQaRunner.ts](api/src/application/qa/dispatchQaRunner.ts) ŌĆö `signJwt` `claw:qa-tester` tenant token, proxied `POST /run`) wired into both the sweep and the manual "Run" endpoint; marketing copy ([content.ts](frontend/src/lib/content.ts)). Residual gaps:

- **QA runner container deploy: binding provisions, image now slimmed to fit ŌĆö pending a green deploy + first live run.** The `QA_RUNNER_CONTAINER` binding provisions fine (confirmed in a 2026-06-22 deploy log). The first deploy FAILED on `Image too large: needs 2760MB, limited to 2000MB` because the full `mcr.microsoft.com/playwright` image bundles chromium+firefox+webkit. FIXED: [api/qa-container/Dockerfile](api/qa-container/Dockerfile) now starts from `node:22-bookworm-slim` and installs **only** chromium via `npx playwright install --with-deps chromium` (+ cache cleanup), which should land ~0.8ŌĆō1.2GB; `server.mjs` launches chromium with `--no-sandbox --disable-dev-shm-usage` for root-in-container. Still UNVERIFIED until the next `wrangler deploy` confirms the slim image is < 2000MB and a first exploration actually drives a browser end-to-end (Chromium boot under the CF firecracker sandbox is the remaining unknown). If it's still over, fall back to `chromium-headless-shell`. *(T9 ┬Ę Platform / T4 ┬Ę Cloud Runtime.)*
- **One-shot container model vs. Cloudflare's persistent-server expectation is unproven.** `QaRunnerContainerDO` keeps a warm server (`sleepAfter='10m'`); `server.ts` acks `/run` then runs the exploration in-process and self-reports ŌĆö but this exact lifecycle (one DO instance per `qa-exec:<id>`, browser launch inside the CF container, `enableInternet` egress to the site-under-test) has never executed. Risk areas: Chromium boot under the CF container sandbox, and whether a long run outlives the DO's request budget. Fixing: a live dispatch against a real exploration. *(T4 ┬Ę Cloud Runtime.)*
- **Agentic Tester isn't a first-class `ide_agents` registry entry / not in the unified `workflow_triggers` builder.** It's scheduled via its own `qa_schedules` surface, not selectable as a Workforce agent. Fixing (register an `ide_agents` row `agent_subtype='agentic_tester'`; route a `workflow_triggers` schedule to it) unblocks: one consistent "pick an agent ŌåÆ schedule it" UX. *(T8 ┬Ę Workflows / T10 ┬Ę QA.)*
- **Migrations 0206/0209 + all the above verified by typecheck + schema-drift only ŌĆö not applied to any live DB, never run end-to-end.** Fixing: apply migrations, provision the binding, configure a schedule, watch the sweep enqueue ŌåÆ dispatch ŌåÆ drain. *(T9 ┬Ę Platform.)*

### Repo-backed Designer + tenant "LLM" object (added 2026-06-21)

Turned the web Designer into a repo-backed IDE and introduced the tenant **"LLM"** (a named, reusable model config). **Built this pass:** migration [0211](api/migrations/0211_designer_repo_and_tenant_models.sql) (`projects.origin`, `project_repositories.last_synced_*`, new `tenant_models` table) + Drizzle schema; tenant-model service + the single `resolveTenantModel` resolver ([tenantModelService.ts](api/src/application/llm/tenantModelService.ts)) wired into BOTH the gateway `/v1/chat/completions` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) and the cloud agent loop `runCloudToolLoop` ([cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)); CRUD routes ([tenantModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/tenantModelRoutes.ts), mounted `/api/llm/models`); the DesignerŌåörepo bridge ([repoBridge.ts](api/src/application/ide/repoBridge.ts) ŌĆö import/commit/create-repo/status, reusing the cloud-native repo read/write helpers, no on-prem host) + IDE routes + auto-import-on-open ([ideRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts)); frontend shared `ModelSelect` + `useLlmModels` tenant-model loader + My-LLMs UI (`/llms`) + `RepoSyncControl` + `IdeAgentPanel` (new IDE "­¤ż¢ Agent" tab embedding `RunAgentControl` + `AgentExecutionPanel`) + `ProjectOriginBadge`. Residual gaps:

- **Tenant-model sampling `params` (temperature/top_p) are applied at the gateway path only, NOT inside the V2 cloud agent loop.** The Brain / on-prem / external `/v1/chat/completions` callers honour `params`; the cloud agent loop honours the model + system prompt + persona but `@builderforce/agent-tools`' `AgentRunInput` doesn't carry generation params, so a tenant model's temperature is ignored on cloud V2 runs. Fixing (thread params through `AgentRunInput` ŌåÆ the proxy completion call) unblocks consistent sampling behaviour across every surface. *(T3 ┬Ę Gateway / T5 ┬Ę agent-tools.)*
- **No persona picker in the My-LLMs editor.** `tenant_models.persona_id` is supported server-side and composed by `resolveTenantModel`, but the editor only sets name/base-model/system-prompt/temperature/visibility ŌĆö there's no UI to attach a marketplace persona. Fixing (a persona `<select>` fed by `/api/personas/mine`) unblocks persona-backed LLMs from the UI. *(T2 ┬Ę App UI.)*
- **Trained SSM model not yet selectable as a tenant-model base.** `tenant_models.trained_model_ref` exists as the seam but nothing writes it or runs against it; the `llm`-modality trained model can't yet be the base of an LLM config. Planned (config-now/trained-later per the approved plan). Fixing unblocks "train your own model, then use it as an LLM everywhere." *(T6 ┬Ę Studio / T3 ┬Ę Gateway.)*
- **`createRemoteRepo` is GitHub-only; GitLab/Bitbucket return unsupported.** Import + commit-back work for all three providers (shared RepoSource + commit helpers), but creating a clean repo from the IDE is implemented only for GitHub (`POST /user/repos`). Fixing (GitLab `POST /projects`, Bitbucket repo create) unblocks the create-repo on-ramp for non-GitHub tenants. *(T4 ┬Ę Repos.)*
- **Designer commit-back has no concurrency/merge guard.** `commitWorkspaceToRepo` force-updates each workspace file onto the branch and deletes base files absent from the workspace; a concurrent change to the same branch could be overwritten (no rebase/conflict detection). Acceptable for v1 single-editor flow. Fixing (compare against `last_synced_sha`, refuse/merge on drift) unblocks safe multi-actor editing. *(T4 ┬Ę Repos.)*
- **`project_repositories.last_synced_sha` is added but never populated** (import stamps `last_synced_ref` + time only; commit diffing reads the base tree live). Fixing (capture the head sha at import) unblocks the concurrency guard above. *(T4 ┬Ę Repos.)*
- **Migration 0211 verified by typecheck only ŌĆö not applied to any live DB, never run end-to-end.** Same standing caveat as 0209. Fixing: apply the migration, then exercise create-LLM ŌåÆ run; connect-repo ŌåÆ open-in-IDE (auto-import) ŌåÆ edit ŌåÆ commit/PR; create-repo-from-IDE. *(T9 ┬Ę Platform.)*
